# 2026-06-04 · quant-ph 论文速递


## 连贯的交换遗憾和无障碍学习

**Original Title:** Coherent Swap Regret and Channel-Proof Learning

**Authors:** Sohail Sarkar

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02655v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02655v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

外部遗憾只有通过固定的选择取代一个人的行为才能证明稳定。在量子游戏中，这错过了一个自然的物理动作：玩家可以将局部完全正痕迹保留（CPTP）地图应用到它实际接收或准备的状态。我们引入了一致交换后悔作为针对所有此类局部CPTP偏差的后悔基准，并给出了一种通过具有定点播放规则的CPTP Choi切片上的熵镜像上升来实现$O（\SQRT{dT\log d}）$一致交换后悔的算法。   主要结果是三层偏差级景观。替代渠道以$eta（\squtt {T\log d}）$的速率恢复普通外部遗憾。单位通道，包括单位偏差和单位混合，具有零极小极大遗憾。确定性的测量和准备渠道已经强制要求中地平线机制中的$Q（\SQRT{dT\log d}）$reprice，并且该比率也足以应对所有CPTP偏差。因此，困难来自推荐寄存器的非单位使用，而不仅仅来自量子一致性。   作为一种应用，有限量子游戏中的去中心化全信息学习在$T=O（\max_i d_i\log d_i/\varepsilon ' 2）$回合后达到$\varepsilon$-大约可分离的量子相关均衡。我们通过介导量子推荐协议的通道防护性来识别这些均衡，对适用于任意有限维状态的本地CPTP利用性进行SDP审计，并在哈尔随机纯状态探测下包括具有伪后悔$O（d #


### Abstract

External regret certifies stability only against replacing one's behavior by a fixed alternative. In a quantum game, this misses a natural physical move: a player can apply a local completely positive trace-preserving (CPTP) map to the state it actually received or prepared. We introduce coherent swap regret as the regret benchmark against all such local CPTP deviations, and give an algorithm achieving $O(\sqrt{dT\log d})$ coherent swap regret via entropic mirror ascent on the CPTP Choi slice with a fixed-point play rule.
  The main result is a three-level deviation-class landscape. Replacement channels recover ordinary external regret at rate $Θ(\sqrt{T\log d})$. Unital channels, including unitary deviations and mixtures of unitaries, have zero minimax regret. Deterministic measurement-and-preparation channels already force $Ω(\sqrt{dT\log d})$ regret in the moderate-horizon regime, and this rate is also sufficient for all CPTP deviations. Thus the hardness comes from non-unital use of the recommendation register, not from quantum coherence alone.
  As an application, decentralized full-information learning in finite quantum games reaches an $\varepsilon$-approximate separable quantum correlated equilibrium after $T=O(\max_i d_i\log d_i/\varepsilon^2)$ rounds. We identify these equilibria with channel-proofness of mediated quantum recommendation protocols, give an SDP audit for local CPTP exploitability applicable to arbitrary finite-dimensional states, and include a probing-bandit extension with pseudo-regret $O(d^{4/3}T^{2/3}(\log d)^{1/3})$ under Haar-random pure-state probes.


---


## 利用相空间分布探索非线性超冷量子气体的信息论度量

**Original Title:** Probing information theoretic measures of nonlinear ultracold quantum gases using phase-space distributions

**Authors:** Mariyah Ughradar, Ramkumar Radhakrishnan, Siddharth Kumar Tiwari, Vikash Kumar Ojha

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02656v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02656v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

我们使用相空间分布，特别是Wigner和Husimi准概率分布，来研究由Gross Pitaevskii方程描述的和谐俘获玻色--爱因斯坦凝聚体。从平均场底态波函数，我们构建了两种分布及其位置和动量空间边缘，并使用这些来计算一组全面的信息论测量：香农、韦尔和雷尼的信息;费舍尔信息;累积和交叉累积剩余信息;互信息;和库巴克--莱布勒、杰弗里斯、柯西·施瓦茨和雷尼的分歧。研究这些量作为代表性RB-85凝聚物的$s$波散射长度的函数，我们发现，更强的排斥相互作用会推动相空间离域增加，这可以通过香农和韦尔尔的单调增长来看出，而费舍尔信息显示了互补趋势--位置空间中增加和动量空间中减少，以与全球费舍尔不确定性界限一致的方式。伦尼（Rényi）的熵和分歧测量进一步揭示了非经典干扰的系统性抑制，以及从维格纳（Wigner）到胡西米（Husimi）表示的过程中向更经典的相空间结构的转变，基于维格纳（Wigner）和胡西米（Husimi）的互信息以更大的相互作用强度收敛。我们注意到，由于Gross Pitaevskii框架将多体状态视为平均场积，因此这里计算的互信息量化了有效单体分布的共乘相空间变量之间的统计依赖性，而不是真正的粒子粒子纠缠。


### Abstract

We use phase space distributions, specifically the Wigner and Husimi quasi probability distributions, to study harmonically trapped Bose--Einstein condensate described by the Gross Pitaevskii equation. From the mean field ground state wavefunction we construct both distributions and their position and momentum space marginals and we use these to compute a comprehensive set of information theoretic measures: Shannon, Wehrl, and Rényi entropies; Fisher information; cumulative and cross cumulative residual entropies; mutual information; and Kullback--Leibler, Jeffreys, Cauchy Schwarz, and Rényi divergences. Studying these quantities as a function of the $s$-wave scattering length for a representative Rb-85 condensate, we find that stronger repulsive interactions drive increased phase space delocalization, seen by a monotonic growth of Shannon and Wehrl entropies, while the Fisher information shows the complementary trend -- increasing in position space and decreasing in momentum space in a manner consistent with the global Fisher uncertainty bound. Rényi entropies and divergence measures further reveal a systematic suppression of non classical interference and a shift toward more classical phase space structure in moving from the Wigner to the Husimi representation, with Wigner and Husimi based mutual informations converging at larger interaction strength. We note that, because the Gross Pitaevskii framework treats the many body state as a mean field product, the mutual information computed here quantifies statistical dependence between the conjugate phase space variables of the effective one body distribution rather than genuine particle particle entanglement.


---


## 利用共振腔提高S频段里德堡原子微波接收机的灵敏度

**Original Title:** Sensitivity Enhancement of S-Band Rydberg Atom Microwave Receiver Using Resonant Cavity

**Authors:** Yipeng Xie, Xinbing Chen, Mingwei Lei, Meng Shi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02669v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02669v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

基于里德堡原子的微波电场传感因其固有的优势（例如绝对校准、宽带可操作性以及与室温设备的兼容性）而引起了越来越多的兴趣。限制灵敏度的一个关键瓶颈是里德伯原子和射入微波场之间的低效耦合，特别是当检测自由空间中传播的弱信号时。在这里，我们提出并通过实验验证了一种将喇叭天线与微波共振腔集成的方案，以显着改善S频段自由空间信号接收的这种耦合。我们在铯蒸气池中使用双量子激发方案，系统地描述了三种配置下的传感性能：裸池、直接腔注入和与喇叭天线耦合的腔，该天线在1 m距离内捕获自由空间微波信号。在天线耦合腔配置中，我们在接收天线处实现了2.33 nV/厘米/$\SQRT{\text{Hz}}$的最佳灵敏度，与优化的裸蒸汽电池配置相比，这相当于增强了约17.9分贝。我们的研究结果提供了一种实用有效的方法来提高里德伯原子传感器的灵敏度，促进它们在现实世界的微波计量和无线通信应用中的采用，这些应用必须可靠地测量弱自由空间电场。


### Abstract

Rydberg atom-based microwave electric field sensing has attracted growing interest owing to its inherent advantages, such as absolute calibration, wideband operability, and compatibility with room-temperature devices. A critical bottleneck that limits sensitivity is the inefficient coupling between the Rydberg atoms and the incident microwave field, particularly when detecting weak signals propagating in free space. Here we propose and experimentally validate a scheme that integrates a horn antenna with a resonant microwave cavity to significantly improve this coupling for free-space signal reception in the S-band. Using a two-photon excitation scheme in a cesium vapor cell, we systematically characterize the sensing performance under three configurations: a bare cell, direct cavity injection, and a cavity coupled to a horn antenna that captures free-space microwave signals over a 1 m distance. In the antenna-coupled cavity configuration, we achieve an optimal sensitivity of 2.33 nV/cm/$\sqrt{\text{Hz}}$ at the receiving antenna, which corresponds to an enhancement of approximately 17.9 dB compared to the optimized bare vapor cell configuration. Our findings offer a practical and effective route to boost the sensitivity of Rydberg atomic sensors, facilitating their adoption in real-world microwave metrology and wireless communication applications where weak free-space electric fields must be reliably measured.


---


## 无惩罚量子优化应用于格子蛋白质折叠

**Original Title:** Penalty-free quantum optimization applied to lattice protein folding

**Authors:** Leif Gellersen, Anders Irbäck, Lucas Knuthson, Stefan Prestel

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02104v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02104v2

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

识别格子蛋白的最小能量结构是一个具有挑战性的离散优化问题。量子方法，例如模拟量子模拟模拟量子模拟和基于门的量子逼近优化算法（QAOA），可以在将其映射到二进制表示后解决这个问题，这通常涉及引入惩罚项来强制执行有效的链配置。然而，在这个问题和许多相关问题中，可以通过将搜索空间限制在冲突图中的独立集并使用为最大独立集问题设计的QAOA混合器来避免使用二次罚项。在这项工作中，我们实现并探索了用于格子蛋白折叠的QAOA变体。这里，目标函数仅由蛋白质能量和简单的线性偏差项组成，没有二次罚分。我们通过对长度为$N=4$和$N=6$的格子蛋白的量子电路的经典模拟来验证这种方法。为了探索更大的系统，我们进一步引入了一种启发式迭代局部搜索方案，通过该方案，我们使用最多26个量子位的局部子图成功折叠了长度高达$N=14$的网格蛋白质。


### Abstract

Identifying minimum-energy structures of lattice proteins is a challenging discrete optimization problem. Quantum approaches such as analog quantum annealing and the gate-based quantum approximate optimization algorithm (QAOA) can address this problem after mapping it to a binary representation, which typically involves introducing penalty terms to enforce valid chain configurations. However, in this and many related problems, the use of quadratic penalty terms can be avoided by restricting the search space to independent sets in a conflict graph and using a QAOA mixer designed for the maximum independent set problem. In this work, we implement and explore this QAOA variant for lattice protein folding. Here, the objective function consists solely of the protein energy together with a simple linear bias term, without quadratic penalties. We validate this approach through classical simulations of the quantum circuits for lattice proteins of lengths $N=4$ and $N=6$. To explore larger systems, we further introduce a heuristic iterative local-search scheme, with which we successfully fold lattice proteins with lengths up to $N=14$ using local subgraphs with at most 26 qubits.


---


## 量子相空间理论：基础与应用

**Original Title:** Theory of Quantum Phase Space: Foundations and Applications

**Authors:** Demin Huang, Biao Wu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02675v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02675v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

本文简要回顾了量子相空间理论，从其基本原理和标准量子准概率分布的性质开始，特别是Wigner、Husimi Q和Glauber-Sudarshan P函数。我们讨论了这些分布的内在局限性，例如负值的出现和相空间模糊。这篇评论的很大一部分强调了最近的理论发展，特别是量子瓦尼尔基础。这种方法在希尔伯特空间和离散相空间之间建立了一个正映射，在相空间中产生真正的概率分布，从而为纯量子状态提供了依赖于基本的信息。此外，我们将布尔冈的非周期基作为规避巴利安-洛定理所施加的约束的理论框架进行了研究。这些发展为基于量子瓦尼尔基的数值研究提供了实用工具，以及理解标准正交相空间表示的局部化极限的概念基准。


### Abstract

This article provides a concise review of quantum phase space theory, beginning with its foundational principles and the properties of standard quantum quasi-probability distributions, specifically the Wigner, Husimi Q, and Glauber--Sudarshan P functions. We discuss the intrinsic limitations of these distributions, such as the appearance of negative values and phase-space blurring. A significant portion of this review highlights recent theoretical developments, particularly the quantum Wannier basis. This approach establishes a unitary mapping between the Hilbert space and a discretized phase space, yielding a genuine probability distribution in phase space and thereby providing a basis-dependent entropy for pure quantum states. Furthermore, we examine Bourgain's nonperiodic basis as a theoretical framework to circumvent the constraints imposed by the Balian--Low theorem. These developments provide practical tools for numerical studies based on the quantum Wannier basis, as well as conceptual benchmarks for understanding the localization limits of orthonormal phase-space representations.


---


## 连续变量QKD中的多维协调：回顾、编码方案和开源模拟

**Original Title:** Multidimensional Reconciliation in Continuous-Variable QKD: Review, Coding Schemes, and Open Source Simulation

**Authors:** Lucien Martial, Alexis Rosio, Eleni Diamanti, Adrien Cassagne, Baptiste Gouraud

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02323v2

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02323v2

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

连续可变量子密钥分发（CV-QKD）需要高效的协调技术才能在低信噪比和长距离下工作。多维协调通过将物理高斯量子通道转换为虚拟二进制输入加性高斯白噪音（BIAWGN）通道来解决这一挑战，从而实现现代错误纠正码的使用。在这项工作中，我们回顾了多维和解的原则，特别关注代数维度1、2、4、8之外的多维结构。我们描述了虚拟通道的构造，讨论了反向协调的实用编码方案，并分析了它们与线性误差纠正码的集成。我们还提出了一个开源模拟框架HDirac，可实现任意维度的多维协调，并使用它来评估最先进的低脂码。结果强调了维度、协调效率和帧错误率之间的关键权衡，为CV-QKD系统设计提供了实用指导。


### Abstract

Continuous-variable quantum key distribution (CV-QKD) requires highly efficient reconciliation techniques to operate at low signal-to-noise ratios and long distances. Multidimensional reconciliation addresses this challenge by transforming the physical Gaussian quantum channel into a virtual binary-input additive white Gaussian noise (BIAWGN) channel, enabling the use of modern errorcorrecting codes. In this work, we review the principles of multidimensional reconciliation, with a particular focus on high-dimensional constructions beyond the algebraic dimensions 1, 2, 4, 8. We describe the construction of the virtual channel, discuss practical coding schemes for reverse reconciliation, and analyse their integration with linear error-correcting codes. We also present an opensource simulation framework, HDirac, implementing multidimensional reconciliation for arbitrary dimensions, and use it to evaluate state-of-the-art LDPC codes. The results highlight key trade-offs between dimension, reconciliation efficiency, and frame error rate, providing practical guidance for CV-QKD system design.


---


## 基于机器学习的变分算法量子错误缓解

**Original Title:** Machine Learning-based Quantum Error Mitigation for Variational Algorithms

**Authors:** Nikita Korolev, Kirill Lakhmanskiy, Daniil Rabinovich

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02697v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02697v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

基于机器学习的量子错误缓解（ML-QEM）已成为提高有噪量子算法性能的一种有前途的方法。然而，现有的ML-QEM方法对变分电路的适用性通常有限，并且依赖于不可访问的无噪训练数据。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种针对变分量子算法定制的实用ML-QEM协议，该协议通过模拟（近）Clifford电路来生成训练数据。这些数据用于模型选择和训练，产生一个缓解模型，该模型可以纠正具有任意参数的变分电路，并在相似结构的不同目标汉密尔顿元之间进行传输。我们在各种噪音模型下针对高达$n=12$量子位的谢灵顿-柯克帕特里克Hamilton量的变分量子本征解算器（VQE）任务上对所提出的方法进行了基准测试，分析其对可训练性的影响，并将其性能与标准零噪音外推（ZNE）进行比较。结果表明，在所有测试设置中都能实现一致的数次错误抑制，并且在高噪音状态下比ZNE具有优越的性能，为拟议协议对当今NISQ处理器的适用性提供了证据。


### Abstract

Machine Learning-based quantum error mitigation (ML-QEM) has emerged as a promising approach for improving the performance of noisy quantum algorithms. However, existing ML-QEM methods often have restricted applicability to variational circuits and rely on inaccessible noiseless training data. In this work, we propose a practical ML-QEM protocol tailored to variational quantum algorithms, which generates training data by simulating (near-)Clifford circuits. This data is used for model selection and training, producing a mitigation model that can correct variational circuits with arbitrary parameters and transfer across different target Hamiltonians of similar structure. We benchmark the proposed method on the Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE) task for the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick Hamiltonian of up to $n=12$ qubits under various noise models, analyzing its effect on trainability and comparing its performance against standard Zero-Noise Extrapolation (ZNE). The results demonstrate consistent several-fold error suppression across all tested settings and superior performance over ZNE in the high-noise regime, providing evidence for the applicability of the proposed protocol to present-day NISQ processors.


---


## 监测的三维Bose-Hubbard模型中强到弱对称性破缺的平均场描述

**Original Title:** A mean-field description of strong-to-weak symmetry breaking in the monitored three-dimensional Bose-Hubbard model

**Authors:** Yicheng Tang, Pradip Kattel, J. H. Pixley

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02713v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02713v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

强到弱自发对称性破缺已成为受监控和开放量子系统中的一种新型有序形式，但迄今为止，其特征主要依赖于非局部诊断。在这里，我们为监控玻色子格子系统开发了Gutzwiller平均场框架，从而能够直接模拟三维空间中的随机测量动态。将这种方法应用于具有局部密度测量和Lindbladian消散的监测Bose-Hubbard模型，我们识别出突破椭圆平均局部序参数的强到弱对称性。我们发现，这个局部有序参数在与电荷锐化转变相同的测量强度附近变得至关重要，并且表现出洛伦兹不变性，相关长度指数$v\simeq 1.2$，与电荷锐化转变的指数相当，这表明这两种现象可能源于一个共同的潜在临界点。我们的工作建立了强到弱对称性破缺的局部特征，揭示了其与电荷尖锐化的联系，并为监测的博斯-哈伯德模型的未来实验提供了具体的预测。


### Abstract

Strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking has emerged as a novel form of ordering in monitored and open quantum systems, yet its characterization has so far primarily relied on nonlocal diagnostics. Here, we develop a Gutzwiller mean-field framework for monitored bosonic lattice systems, enabling the direct simulation of stochastic measurement dynamics in three spatial dimensions. Applying this approach to the monitored Bose-Hubbard model with local density measurements and Lindbladian dissipation, we identify strong-to-weak symmetry breaking through a trajectory-averaged local order parameter. We find that this local order parameter becomes critical near the same measurement strength as the charge-sharpening transition and exhibits Lorentz invariance with a correlation-length exponent, $ν\simeq 1.2$, comparable to that of the charge-sharpening transition, suggesting that the two phenomena may originate from a common underlying critical point. Our work establishes a local characterization of strong-to-weak symmetry breaking, reveals its connection to charge sharpening, and provides concrete predictions for future experiments on the monitored Bose-Hubbard model.


---


## 在单个元表面生成的镊子阵列中捕获11，000个原子

**Original Title:** Trapping 11,000 Atoms in a Tweezer Array Generated by a Single Metasurface

**Authors:** Yuqing Wang, Zhongchi Zhang, Tao Zhang, Yuxuan Liao, Hanteng Wang, Ye Tian, Binjie Ji, Yujia Wu, Luming Ma, Chen Qing, Chengshu Li, Wei Zhang, Yidong Huang, Wenjun Zhang, Xue Feng, Wenlan Chen, Hui Zhai

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02715v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02715v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

物理量子位数的可扩展性是通用容差量子计算机面临的核心挑战。原子阵列量子计算机固有的可扩展性源于原子量子位的相同性质，因此可用的量子位资源主要受到可以捕获和控制的原子数量的限制。在这里，我们在镊子阵列中稳健地捕获11，000个单独的原子，从而使可用的量子位资源在所有量子计算平台中首次达到数万个规模。这一进步是通过直径约2厘米的单个元表面实现的，它可以生成整个镊子阵列，而不需要显微镜目镜，从而最大限度地提高激光功率效率。大口径确保了约1.5厘米的工作距离，允许元表面放置在真空室外部，并避免了真空内操作的技术复杂性。我们使用渗透相转变的统计理论进一步描述了随机加载的原子阵列。这项工作朝着10，000量子位规模的量子计算机迈出了重要的第一步。


### Abstract

The scalability of physical qubit numbers is a central challenge toward a universal fault-tolerant quantum computer. The inherent scalability of atom array quantum computers stems from the identical nature of atomic qubits, so the available qubit resource is primarily limited by the number of atoms that can be trapped and controlled. Here, we robustly trap 11,000 individual atoms in a tweezer array, thereby enabling the available qubit resource to reach the tens-of-thousands scale for the first time among all quantum computation platforms. This advance is enabled by a single metasurface, approximately 2 cm in diameter, that generates the entire tweezer array without the need for microscope objectives, thereby maximizing laser-power efficiency. The large aperture ensures a working distance of about 1.5 cm, allowing the metasurface to be placed outside the vacuum cell and avoiding the technical complications of in-vacuum operation. We further characterize the randomly loaded atom array using the statistical theory of percolation phase transitions. This work takes an important first step toward a quantum computer at the 10,000-qubit scale.


---


## 静止量子钟中的共振延迟：提高阈值屏蔽

**Original Title:** Resonant delay in a stationary quantum clock: Lifting the threshold mask

**Authors:** Paul C. W. Davies, Damien A. Easson

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02718v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02718v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

量子渡越时间有着悠久的不等效定义的历史，包括相时间、停留时间和量子钟结构。在此背景下，我们重新审视Salecker-Wigner-Peres静态量子钟，将其视为相敏散射可观测值，时钟时间由跨相互作用区域的传输移的能量衍生物定义。对于真正紧支持的一维势，我们表明原始静止佩雷斯时钟一般包含一个普适的\（1/\squtt {E}\）连续边项，其系数由低能量散射数据固定。对于吸引平方井来说，这个阈值奇异性是从消失的外部动量和相关的散射匹配继承的，而不是从共振延迟本身继承的。我们推导出平方井的精确稳定时钟时间，并引入一种新的阈值减时钟观测值。除了特殊的零能量调谐之外，减法消除了普遍的低能量项并隔离了共振贡献。与停留时间和传输维格纳相延迟的比较表明，阈值减去时钟在隔离传输共振附近获得了预期的局部洛伦兹形式。在连续体边缘附近，如果\（\varepŸ\）表示与阈值的失调，则共振峰仅增长为\（\varepŸ &{-1/2}\），而未扣除阈值背景增长为\（\varepŸ &{-3/2}\）。对称的屏障--井--屏障腔和数字不对称的两步吸引井提供了补充控制。结果是一种新的阈值减去固定时钟候选者，它将通用阈值运动学与极点敏感共振延迟分开。


### Abstract

Quantum transit times have a long history of inequivalent definitions, including phase times, dwell times, and quantum-clock constructions. In this context we revisit the Salecker--Wigner--Peres stationary quantum clock as a phase-sensitive scattering observable, with clock time defined by the energy derivative of the transmission phase shift across the interaction region. For real compactly supported one-dimensional potentials, we show that the raw stationary Peres clock generically contains a universal \(1/\sqrt{E}\) continuum-edge term whose coefficient is fixed by low-energy scattering data. For the attractive square well, this threshold singularity is inherited from the vanishing exterior momentum and the associated scattering matching, rather than from resonant delay itself. We derive the exact stationary clock time for the square well and introduce a new threshold-subtracted clock observable. Away from exceptional zero-energy tuning, the subtraction removes the universal low-energy term and isolates the resonant contribution. Comparison with the dwell time and the transmission Wigner phase delay shows that the threshold-subtracted clock acquires the expected local Lorentzian form near isolated transmission resonances. Near the continuum edge, if \(\varepsilon\) denotes the detuning from threshold, the resonant peak grows only as \(\varepsilon^{-1/2}\), whereas the unsubtracted threshold background grows as \(\varepsilon^{-3/2}\). A symmetric barrier--well--barrier cavity and a numerical asymmetric two-step attractive well provide complementary controls. The result is a new threshold-subtracted stationary-clock candidate that separates universal threshold kinematics from pole-sensitive resonant delay.

## 在量子硬件上模拟凝聚态物理

**Original Title:** Simulating Condensed Matter Physics on Quantum Hardware

**Authors:** Ruizhe Shen, Tianqi Chen, Tommy Tai, Jin Ming Koh, Pouyan Ghaemi, Ching Hua Lee

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02721v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02721v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

量子硬件平台在模拟凝聚态物质的能力方面变得越来越复杂，包括但不限于强相关、拓扑和非平衡现象。本文综述了基于量子硬件的凝聚态模拟的最新进展，主要强调基于门的数字量子计算机模拟，模拟实验作为补充基准进行讨论。我们首先回顾主要的硬件平台，包括超导量子比特，捕获离子，超冷原子，里德堡阵列，光子系统，和莫尔量子材料。然后，我们介绍数字量子模拟的基本组成部分。在此基础上，我们讨论了凝聚态物理学的代表性应用，涵盖了底态问题、强相关物质、拓扑相、非平衡动力学、开放系统物理学和受高能物理启发的模拟。最后，我们总结了最先进的量子模拟工作流程中使用的关键方法学工具。我们强调，目前的有噪音的量子模拟不仅可以作为近期演示，而且可以作为未来容差量子模拟所需的编码、诊断协议和错误控制策略的原型。


### Abstract

Quantum hardware platforms are getting increasingly sophisticated in their ability to simulate condensed matter, including but not limited to strongly-correlated, topological, and non-equilibrium phenomena. This review surveys recent progress in quantum-hardware-based simulations of condensed matter, primarily emphasizing gate-based digital quantum computer simulation, with analog experiments discussed as complementary benchmarks. We first review major hardware platforms, including superconducting qubits, trapped-ions, ultracold atoms, Rydberg arrays, photonic systems, and moire quantum materials. We then introduce the basic ingredients of digital quantum simulation. Building on this foundation, we discuss representative applications to condensed-matter physics, spanning ground-state problems, strongly correlated matter, topological phases, non-equilibrium dynamics, open-system physics, and high-energy-physics-inspired simulations. Finally, we summarize key methodological tools used in state-of-the-art quantum-simulation workflows. We emphasize that present noisy quantum simulations serve not only as near-term demonstrations, but also as prototypes for the encodings, diagnostic protocols and error-control strategies required for future fault-tolerant quantum simulation.

## 林德布拉德动力学中的几何去相关时间

**Original Title:** Geometric Decoherence Time in Lindbladian Dynamics

**Authors:** Rishabh Jha, Stephan Haas, Abhinav Prem

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02743v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02743v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

开放多体系统中退散的开始缺乏以二体纠缠丧失为基础的动态时间尺度。在这里，我们引入了$geographical $ $decohering $ $time$，定义为对数负性和Rényi之间单调关系的最早时刻-$\tfRAC{1}{2}$ entropy --在纯状态的任何二分区中完全相等--在开放系统进化下崩溃，信号传递了信息，但没有伴随的纠缠增长。我们在单粒子高斯动力学和多体林德布拉德进化中建立了这个标准。我们表明，量子互信息提供了一种补充的长期诊断：它的渐进消失相当于双分区中稳态的因式分解，这是一个严格比可分性强的条件，每当产品稳态以指数方式接近时，负性和互信息共享相同的衰变率。在存在强对称性的情况下，这种跟踪可能会失败--在纠缠消失后，残余经典相关性可以继续存在。在损益平衡的Kitaev链中，我们推导出一个封闭形式的解，并表明在相同的消耗下，拓扑相比平凡相维持更长的相干时间，并且在手征对称点处存在局部极小值。在相互作用的XXZ链中，精确的多体进化表明，局部$Z$-去相保留了剩余的经典相关性，而损益则恢复了负性的互信息跟踪。我们的结果将几何退散时间建立为跟踪退散开始的动态尺度。


### Abstract

The onset of decoherence in open many-body systems lacks a dynamical timescale grounded in the loss of bipartite entanglement. Here, we introduce the $geometric$ $decoherence$ $time$, defined as the earliest moment the monotone relation between logarithmic negativity and Rényi-$\tfrac{1}{2}$ entropy -- exactly equal across any bipartition for pure states -- breaks down under open-system evolution, signaling entropy growth without accompanying entanglement growth. We establish this criterion in both single-particle Gaussian dynamics and many-body Lindbladian evolution. We show that quantum mutual information provides a complementary long-time diagnostic: its asymptotic vanishing is equivalent to factorization of the steady state across the bipartition, a condition strictly stronger than separability, and whenever a product steady state is approached exponentially in trace norm, negativity and mutual information share the same decay rate. In the presence of a strong symmetry, this tracking can fail -- residual classical correlations can survive after entanglement has vanished. In the Kitaev chain with balanced gain and loss, we derive a closed-form solution and show that the topological phase sustains longer coherence times than the trivial phase at identical dissipation, with a local minimum at the chiral-symmetric point. In the interacting XXZ chain, exact many-body evolution shows that local $Z$-dephasing preserves residual classical correlations, whereas gain and loss restore the mutual-information tracking of negativity. Our results establish the geometric decoherence time as a dynamical scale tracking the onset of decoherence.

## 金刚石氮空位中心宽带微波场的垂直磁力测量

**Original Title:** Vector Magnetometry with Broadband Microwave Fields in Nitrogen-Vacancy Centers in Diamond

**Authors:** Tom R. Rieckmann, Arezoo Afshar, Aaron Z. Goldberg, Lilian Childress, Stefan Scheel, Khabat Heshami

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02749v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02749v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

我们提出了一种使用氮空位（NV）中心的全载体磁力测量的新方法。与传统的光学检测磁共振技术相比，我们的方法采用两个不同的宽带微波脉冲，并在传输通过NV传感器媒体后对其进行测量，从而捕获由于塞曼效应而导致的接地三重线的线分裂。两个垂直极化的微波脉冲允许通过读取不同取向的NV中心来独立解析所有磁场分量。使用深度神经网络分析模拟数据，我们希望其功效能够很好地转化为实验。我们的方法在不同的磁场分量上产生的灵敏度在5美元~\mathrm {pT}/\SQRT {\mathrm {Hz}}$和100美元~\mathrm{pT}/\SQRT{Hz}}$之间，同时在70美元的信噪（SNR）比下实现大约$\mathrm{nT}$的准确度。通过能够准确测量低至25美元的磁场，消除了对地球磁场以外偏置场的需求。


### Abstract

We present a novel method for full vector magnetometry using nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers. In contrast to conventional optically detected magnetic resonance techniques, our method employs two distinct broadband microwave pulses and measures them after transmission through the NV sensor medium, thus capturing the line splitting of the ground state triplet due to the Zeeman effect. Two orthogonally polarized microwave pulses allow resolving all magnetic field components independently by reading out differently oriented NV centers. Simulated data is analyzed using deep neural networks, whose efficacy we expect to translate very well to experiments. Our method yields sensitivities between $5~\mathrm{pT}/\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$ and $100~\mathrm{pT}/\sqrt{\mathrm{Hz}}$ across different magnetic field vector components, while achieving approximately $\mathrm{nT}$ accuracy at a signal-to-noise (SNR) ratio of $70~\mathrm{dB}$. By being capable of accurately measuring magnetic fields down to $25~\mathrm{μT}$, the need for a bias field beyond Earth's magnetic field is eliminated.

## 含动态物质的（1+1）维$U（1）$格点规范理论的量子模拟模拟

**Original Title:** Photonic Analog Quantum Simulation of (1+1)-Dimensional $U(1)$ Lattice Gauge Theory with Dynamical Matter

**Authors:** Nathan R. Gonzalez, Thea Budde, Klemen Kersic, Zia Steele, Alex H. Rubin, Joao C. Pinto Barros, Marina Radulaski, Marina Krstic Marinkovic

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02756v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02756v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

提出了一种基于JCH模型的模拟量子模拟U（1）$格点规范理论的光子方案。在这里，在强耦合制度的腔量子电动力学的相互作用腔阵列映射到交替的物质和规范场网站的自旋1/2量子链接模型。与其他模拟LGT量子模拟方法相比，我们的方法实现了所需的规范不变的动力学通过跳跃的极化激元激发之间的阵列网站。跳跃映射到规范理论通过精确调谐的极化激元共振在个别腔。使用精确对角化，我们表明JCH模型的实时演变准确地复制了量子链接模型的实时演变。最后，我们讨论了在光和超导系统中通过可扩展实现的超经典模拟能力的可行途径。这为理解具有更高维度物质的格点规范理论的实时动力学提供了一条新颖的途径。


### Abstract

We propose a photonic scheme for analog quantum simulation of a $U(1)$ Lattice Gauge Theory (LGT) with dynamical matter based on the Jaynes-Cummings-Hubbard (JCH) model. Here, an array of interacting cavities in the strong-coupling regime of cavity Quantum Electrodynamics is mapped onto the alternating matter and gauge-field sites of the spin-1/2 Quantum Link Model. In contrast to other analog LGT quantum simulation methods, our approach implements the desired gauge-invariant dynamics through the hopping of polaritonic excitations among the array sites. The hopping is mapped to the gauge theory via precise tuning of polaritonic resonances in individual cavities. Using exact diagonalization, we show that the real-time evolution of the JCH model accurately replicates that of a Quantum Link Model. Finally, we discuss feasible routes to the beyond-classical simulation capability with scalable implementations in photonic and superconducting systems. This provides a novel route towards understanding the real-time dynamics of lattice gauge theories with matter in higher dimensions.

## 通过将交流磁体集成到超导量子位设计中来增强量子位性能

**Original Title:** Enhanced qubit performance by integrating altermagnets into superconducting qubit designs

**Authors:** Johanne Bratland Tjernshaugen, Morten Amundsen, Jacob Linder

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02761v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02761v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

确定一种材料平台来创建既可调又能对环境噪音有弹性的量子位，是实现实际有用的量子计算需要克服的主要障碍之一。为此目的，一种追求的途径是使用具有固有的旋转相关相互作用（例如旋转轨道耦合或磁性）的超量子位。然而，最近发现的称为交流发电机的材料在这种背景下基本上仍未被探索。我们在这里使用微观计算来确定当包括互磁约瑟夫森结时，如何修改超导量子位的性质。关键的量子位性能参数，包括分裂、非调和性、退相干和单/耦合量子位门操作时间，根据交流材料的特征性质，例如内尔场的强度和系统中交流相对界面的晶体学取向，显示出丰富的行为。我们特别关注transmon设计，并表明量子位受到了很好的保护，防止退相干，同时在0-$pi $转变点附近和处于$ph $-状态时都表现出优异的非调和性。我们建议，通过使用应变，可以将互磁量子位移出其保护状态，以实现更快的门操作时间，然后移回其保护状态。我们还讨论了交流磁性质如何影响通量量子位和氟里昂。我们的结果表明，由于互磁性能带结构的独特性质，将互磁性材料集成到现有的超导量子位设计中可以大幅提高其性能。


### Abstract

Identifying a materials platform for creating qubits that are both tunable and resilient towards environmental noise is one of the main hurdles that need to be overcome to realize quantum computation that is practically useful. One pursued avenue to this end is to use superconducting qubits with intrinsic spin-dependent interactions, such as spin-orbit coupling or magnetism. However, the recently discovered class of materials known as altermagnets remain largely unexplored in this context. We here use microscopic calculations to determine how the properties of superconducting qubits are modified when altermagnetic Josephson junctions are included. The key qubit performance parameters, including splitting, anharmonicity, decoherence, and single/coupled-qubit gate operation times, display rich behavior depending on the characteristic properties of the altermagnetic material, such as the strength of the Néel field and the crystallographic orientation of the altermagnetic relative interfaces in the system. We focus in particular on the transmon design and show that the qubit is very well protected against decoherence and simultaneously shows superior anharmonicity both near 0-$π$ transition points and when it is in a $φ$-state. We propose that by using strain, the altermagnetic qubit can be moved out of its protected regime to enable faster gate-operation times, and then moved back to its protected state. We also discuss how the altermagnetic properties influence flux qubits and fluxonium. Our results suggest that integration of altermagnetic materials into existing superconducting qubit design can substantially improve their performance due to the unique properties of the altermagnetic band-structure.


---


## QUIVER：大型ML模型中增强表示的量子知情观点

**Original Title:** QUIVER: Quantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations in Large ML Models

**Authors:** Aritra Bal, Michael Binder, Markus Klute, Benedikt Maier, Michael Spannowsky

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02785v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02785v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

大型机器学习模型从多模式输入中受益匪浅，这些输入提供了同一示例的补充视图。我们引入了QUIVER（增强表示的量子知情视图），这是一种用量子费舍尔观点丰富了经典数据驱动特征的范式：由变分量子电路（VQC）捕获的更高级相关性的几何激励、与基础无关的总结，训练执行相同的任务。与经典的特征增强不同，量子费舍尔信息矩阵编码所学习的量子状态管的固有几何形状。虽然这种受量子信息理论启发的特征图通常对于经典建模来说并不平凡，但它可以揭示额外的经典数据或模型能力难以学习的统计结构。这使得量子费舍尔观点成为一种真正的补充模式，而不是多余的模式。我们证明，QUIVER改进了来自截然不同领域的两个基准数据集的标准性能指标：用于预测分子性质的QM 9和用于预测大型强子对撞机（LHC）上喷气风味的JetClass。然而，其核心贡献是领域不可知的：通过对基本架构进行有针对性的修改，量子费舍尔观点可以融合到广泛的模型架构中，以纳入有关问题量子几何的信息。这些结果表明，从模拟变分电路中提取的量子几何特征可以为标准机器学习任务提供可测量的价值，这早在容错量子硬件出现之前就可以了。


### Abstract

Large machine learning models benefit substantially from multimodal inputs that provide a complementary view of the same example. We introduce QUIVER (QUantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations, a paradigm that enriches classical data-driven features with a quantum Fisher view: a geometrically motivated, basis-independent summary of higher-order correlations captured by a variational quantum circuit (VQC) trained to perform the same task. Unlike classical feature augmentation, the quantum Fisher information matrix encodes the intrinsic geometry of the learned quantum state manifold. While this feature map, motivated by quantum information theory, is ordinarily non-trivial to model classically, it can surface statistical structure that additional classical data or model capacity finds difficult to learn. This makes the quantum Fisher view a genuinely complementary modality rather than a redundant one. We demonstrate that QUIVER improves standard performance metrics on two benchmark datasets from very different fields: QM9 for predicting molecule properties, and JetClass for predicting jet flavor at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The core contribution, however, is domain-agnostic: the quantum Fisher view can be fused into a broad class of model architectures via targeted modifications to the base architecture, to incorporate information about the quantum geometry of the problem. These results demonstrate that quantum-geometric features, extracted from simulated variational circuits, can deliver measurable value for standard machine learning tasks, well before the advent of fault-tolerant quantum hardware.

## 神经网络量子状态的标度定律

**Original Title:** Scaling Laws for Neural-Network Quantum States

**Authors:** Riccardo Rende, Alessandro Sinibaldi, Luciano Loris Viteritti, Roeland Wiersema, Antoine Georges, Giuseppe Carleo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02794v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02794v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

缩放定律是现代神经网络中观察到的损失、架构大小和计算之间的乘势定律关系，提供了一种量化方法来描述学习问题的复杂性，其中控制损失衰减的指数反映了额外资源转化为提高的准确性的速度，以及学习目标的难度。类似的框架是否可以描述物理问题的复杂性仍有待商榷。我们针对神经网络量子状态解决了这个问题，神经网络量子状态是强相关量子多体系统的主要变分方法。使用Transformer波函数来逼近三角形和正方形网格上的$J_1$-$J_2$海森堡模型的底价，具有高达$20 $x 20$的位置，我们发现$V$-分数（变分状态准确性的衡量标准）在训练计算中按照功率定律衰变。在适当的计算重新缩放下，不同系统大小的结果崩溃到一条曲线上，类似于关键现象中的缩放崩溃。由此产生的幂律是，一个很好的近似，独立的网站的数量，表明Transformer Anastomic是大小一致的系统考虑。指数随着挫败而系统性地下降，将其确定为基状态代表难度的量化衡量标准，并建立标度定律作为基准变分反的一般框架。


### Abstract

Scaling laws, the power-law relations between loss, architecture size, and compute observed in modern neural networks, offer a quantitative way to characterize the complexity of a learning problem, with the exponent governing the decay of the loss reflecting how rapidly additional resources translate into improved accuracy, and thus how hard the target is to learn. Whether an analogous framework can characterize the complexity of physical problems remains open. We address this question for Neural-Network Quantum States, a leading variational approach for strongly correlated quantum many-body systems. Using transformer wave functions to approximate ground states of the $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg model on triangular and square lattices with up to $20\times 20$ sites, we find that the $V$-score, a measure of accuracy of a variational state, decays as a power law in training compute. Under an appropriate rescaling of compute, results for different system sizes collapse onto a single curve, analogous to scaling collapse in critical phenomena. The resulting power law is, to a good approximation, independent of the number of sites, showing that the transformer Ansatz is size-consistent for the systems considered. The exponent decreases systematically with frustration, identifying it as a quantitative measure of representational difficulty of the ground state and establishing scaling laws as a general framework for benchmarking variational ansätze.


---


## 尼尔森复杂性和多个成本因素

**Original Title:** Nielsen complexity with multiple cost factors

**Authors:** Marcos Rios Ribeiro, Diego Trancanelli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02817v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02817v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

我们研究了尼尔森在存在多个成本因素的情况下量子复杂性的几何方法，扩展了标准框架，其中单一罚分区分群多管的易方向和硬方向。通过引入与不同程度的非局部性相关的惩罚层次，我们开发了一种广义右不变复杂性几何，并分析其对测地进化的影响。我们推导出修改后的Euler-Arnold和Jacobi方程，并研究多重成本因素如何重塑共点的结构和缩放，其中测地最优性被打破。形式主义在两种环境中得到了说明：具有两个成本因素的单量子位系统，我们在其中推导出复杂性增长及其对惩罚层次结构的依赖性的近似分析解，以及SYK型模型，我们在其中分析自由和混乱状态。在这些多体系统中，我们表明，不同的非本地部门会产生多个共点族，其发生取决于成本层次和系统规模。我们的结果凸显了细化罚结构如何为量子复杂性及其动态行为提供更丰富、更现实的描述。


### Abstract

We investigate Nielsen's geometric approach to quantum complexity in the presence of multiple cost factors, extending the standard framework where a single penalty distinguishes easy from hard directions of the group manifold. By introducing a hierarchy of penalties associated with different degrees of non-locality, we develop a generalized right-invariant complexity geometry and analyze its implications for geodesic evolution. We derive the modified Euler-Arnold and Jacobi equations and study how multiple cost factors reshape the structure and scaling of conjugate points, where geodesic optimality breaks down. The formalism is illustrated in two settings: a single-qubit system with two cost factors, where we derive approximate analytic solutions for the complexity growth and its dependence on penalty hierarchies, and SYK-type models, where we analyze both free and chaotic regimes. In these many-body systems, we show that distinct non-local sectors generate multiple families of conjugate points whose occurrence depends on both the cost hierarchy and the system size. Our results highlight how refining the penalty structure provides a richer and more realistic description of quantum complexity and its dynamical behavior.


---


## 玻色子辐射的表观费米谱：加速电荷动力学

**Original Title:** Apparent Fermionic Spectra for Bosonic Radiation: Accelerated Charge Kinematics

**Authors:** Michael R. R. Good, Evgenii Ievlev, Arsen Almaskhan

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02824v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02824v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

加速点电荷可以发射具有明显费米-狄拉克光谱的量子，尽管辐射是玻色的，并且其占据数不限于0或1。该效应源于一类特殊的加速运动学，并且不依赖于热平衡、视界或统计集合。


### Abstract

An accelerated point charge can emit photons with an apparent Fermi-Dirac spectrum, even though the radiation is bosonic and its occupation numbers are not constrained to 0 or 1. The effect arises from a special class of acceleration kinematics and does not rely on thermal equilibrium, horizons, or statistical ensembles.

## 自旋守恒模型的精确解与Wigner-Araki-Yanase定理

**Original Title:** Exact Solutions for Spin Conserving Models and the Wigner-Araki-Yanase Theorem

**Authors:** Michael Steiner, Ronald Rendell

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02861v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02861v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

Wigner-Araki-Yanase（WAY）定理是一个著名的定理，涉及存在加性保守定律时量子测量的局限性。在冯·诺伊曼测量模型的假设下，系统保守量$L_{S}$是有界的，给定一个保守的总加性系统加上设备量$L_{SA}$，测量操作符$E_{S}$必须与$L_{S}$交换。先前的证明利用了受到动量保持操作约束的么正进化的性质，这些性质往往会模糊WAY定理的物理本质，并导致性能的界限。由于人们普遍认为动量在测量中总是精确保守的，因此我们开发了一个通用的角动量保守测量模型。该模型被证明可以简单地解释WAY定理的主要含义，并提供基于设备模型的测量效果的准确结果。这可以通过根据密度矩阵跟踪设备以及基于Kraus操作符的仅系统通道模型来证明。


### Abstract

The Wigner-Araki-Yanase (WAY) theorem is a well-known theorem regarding limitations of quantum measurement in the presence of additive conservation laws. Under the assumptions of the von Neumann measurement model, for which the system conserved quantity $L_{S}$ is bounded, given a conserved total additive system plus apparatus quantity $L_{SA}$, the measurement operator $E_{S}$ must commute with $L_{S}$. Prior proofs have exploited the properties of unitary evolution constrained by momentum conserving operations that tend to obscure the physical nature of the WAY theorem and as well lead to bounds on performance. As it is generally agreed that momentum is always exactly conserved in measurement, we instead develop a general angular momentum conserving model of measurement. This model is shown to lead to a simple explanation of the major implications of the WAY theorem and provides exact results of the effects of measurement based on the apparatus model. This is shown by both tracing the apparatus from the density matrix and also via a system-only channel model based on Kraus operators.


---


## 通过融合图图案实现量子图状态的有效合成

**Original Title:** Towards Efficient Synthesis of Quantum Graph States by Fusing Graph Motifs

**Authors:** Tingxiang Ji, Hansika Weerasena, Demitry Farfurnik, Jianqing Liu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02880v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02880v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

具有先进布局的光图状态可以实现基于测量的量子计算、分布式量子传感和量子互连。然而，光图状态的有效生成受到光纠缠操作的概率性质和生成率对资源成本的指数依赖性的限制。在这项工作中，我们将光图状态合成作为一个具有成本意识的分解问题来研究，利用局部Clifford（LC）等效性来在分解之前识别目标图状态的更易于合成的表示。具体来说，我们提出了具有成本意识的融合分解（CFA），这是一个三阶段启发式框架，将目标图状态分解为环、星和线性基序，并通过类型I融合操作将它们组装起来，以最大限度地减少融合费用和物理量子位消耗。我们进一步表明，选择具有最小边数的LC等价图状态为接近最优的合成提供了一个非常有效的代理：在许多情况下，它与CFD下LC等效类中观察到的最佳生成速率相匹配，对图态轨道数据和二维、三维格点图态的数值计算表明，计算流体动力学（CFD）可达到84.6%。%的资源开销减少，并且产生跨越多个数量级的光子产生速率的改进。这些结果表明，将结构感知的基序分解与LC等效相结合是一种实用且可扩展的光图状态合成策略。


### Abstract

Photonic graph states with advanced topologies can enable measurement-based quantum computing, distributed quantum sensing, and quantum interconnects. However, the efficient generation of photonic graph states is limited by the probabilistic nature of photonic entangling operations and the exponential dependence of generation rate on resource cost. In this work, we study photonic graph state synthesis as a cost-aware decomposition problem, exploiting local Clifford (LC) equivalence to identify more synthesis-friendly representations of the target graph state before decomposition. Specifically, we propose Cost-aware Fusion-based Decomposition (CFD), a three-stage heuristic framework that decomposes a target graph state into ring, star, and linear motifs, and assembles them via Type-I fusion operations to minimize fusion overhead and physical-qubit consumption. We further show that selecting the LC-equivalent graph state with the minimum number of edges provides a highly effective proxy for near-optimal synthesis: in many cases it matches the best generation rate observed within the LC equivalence class under CFD, and in most remaining cases it remains close to it. Numerical evaluations on graph state orbit data and 2D and 3D lattice graph states demonstrate that CFD achieves up to 84.6\% reduction in resource overhead compared to baseline constructions, and yields improvements in photonic generation rate spanning multiple orders of magnitude. These results suggest that combining structure-aware motif decomposition with LC equivalence is a practical and scalable strategy for photonic graph state synthesis.


---


## 隐式步进对算术网格的快速张量网络虚时间进化

**Original Title:** Fast Tensor Network Imaginary Time Evolution by Implicit Stepping on Logarithmic Grids

**Authors:** John P. Zima, E. Miles Stoudenmire, Steven R. White, Olivier Parcollet, Jason Kaye

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02930v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02930v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

我们提出了一种新的方法来实现以矩阵积状态（MPS）表示的量子多体波函数的有效虚时演化。我们首先表明，对数时间网格足以解决长虚时间动态问题，与标准方法相比，时间步数呈指数级减少。然后，我们表明，常微方程的A稳定隐式时间步方法允许任何时间步大小的稳定传播。由此产生的方案仅需要矩阵-载体积和线性求解，MPS工具箱中的标准操作。我们通过两个例子验证了我们的方法：海森堡旋转链，我们用它来证明比具有均匀时间步的标准时变分原理方法提高几个数量级的加速，以及具有金属浴的单点安德森杂质模型，对于金属浴，传播到大虚时间允许人们观察近藤温度对相互作用强度的指数依赖性。


### Abstract

We present a new method for the efficient imaginary time evolution of quantum many-body wavefunctions represented by matrix product states (MPS). We first show that logarithmic time grids are sufficient to resolve long imaginary time dynamics, yielding an exponential reduction in the number of time steps compared with standard approaches. We then show that A-stable implicit time-stepping methods for ordinary differential equations allow stable propagation for any time step size. The resulting scheme requires only matrix-vector products and linear solves, standard operations in the MPS toolbox. We validate our approach with two examples: a Heisenberg spin chain, which we use to demonstrate a speedup of several orders of magnitude over the standard time-dependent variational principle method with uniform time steps, and a single-site Anderson impurity model with a metallic bath, for which propagation to large imaginary times allows one to observe the exponential dependence of the Kondo temperature on the interaction strength.


---


## 最大化三硬币量子行走中的信息流：从初始纠缠到集成光子实现

**Original Title:** Maximizing Information Flow in Three-Coin Quantum Walk: from Initial Entanglement to Integrated Photonic Implementation

**Authors:** Seyed Mohsen Moosavi Khansari

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02942v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02942v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

离散时间量子行走是模拟量子传输和信息处理的强大平台。在这里，我们在一维网格上引入了一个步行者，其运动由三个纠缠的硬币控制，每个硬币都用阿达玛门初始化，旨在最大化信息流。只有当所有三个硬币产生相同的结果（HHH或TTT）时，步行者才会移动，从而将8维硬币的Hilbert空间与位置自由度相耦合。通过分析完全可分、完全纠缠（GZZ型）和中间初始状态，并使用约化子系统的冯·诺伊曼（von Neumann）信息，我们计算硬币和位置之间的互信息$I（C;P;t）$。结果表明，尽管由于量子干涉，初始三重纠缠表现出短期非单调动力学，但经过十个步骤（与两个可分离状态中较低的状态相比）后，初始三重纠缠在互信息增长18%。我们首次引入了一个可调参数$a $（非位移状态的幅度），并表明GZZ状态在$a\大约0.71$处达到互信息最大值--这是信息流最优控制的关键发现。最后，提出了一种使用极化、空间模式和时间点的集成光学实现，其中$a $可以用非线性或光电元件进行调节。提供了一个可扩展的数字框架（Python代码），用于最多$t = 5$步骤的模拟。我们的研究结果将三方纠缠确立为最大化信息流和空间传播的动态资源，并直接应用于量子状态转移、纠缠辅助传感和可编程光量子处理器。


### Abstract

Discrete-time quantum walks are powerful platforms for simulating quantum transport and information processing. Here we introduce a walker on a one-dimensional lattice whose motion is controlled by three entangled coins, each initialized with the Hadamard gate, aiming to maximize information flow. The walker moves only when all three coins yield the same outcome (HHH or TTT), thus coupling the 8-dimensional coin Hilbert space to the position degree of freedom. By analyzing fully separable, fully entangled (GHZ-type) and intermediate initial states, and using the von Neumann entropy of reduced subsystems, we compute the mutual information $I(C;P;t)$ between coin and position. The results show that initial three-partite entanglement accelerates the growth of mutual information by up to 18\% after ten steps (when compared to the lower of the two separable states), although it exhibits short-term non-monotonic dynamics due to quantum interference. For the first time, we introduce a tunable parameter $α$ (amplitude of non-displacement states) and show that the GHZ state reaches a maximum of mutual information at $α\approx 0.71$ - a key finding for optimal control of information flow. Finally, an integrated photonic implementation using polarization, spatial modes and time bins is proposed, where $α$ can be tuned with nonlinear or electro-optic elements. A scalable numerical framework (Python code) for simulations up to $t = 5$ steps is provided. Our findings establish three-partite entanglement as a dynamical resource for maximizing information flow and spatial spreading, with direct applications in quantum state transfer, entanglement-assisted sensing and programmable photonic quantum processors.


---


## 用纠缠量子测试${\rm ER= BEP}$猜想

**Original Title:** Testing the ${\rm ER=EPR}$ conjecture with entangled photons

**Authors:** Kimet Jusufi, Francisco S. N. Lobo, Douglas Singleton

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02943v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02943v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-01


### 摘要

我们正则化的Aichelburg-Sexl冲击波度规的无质量粒子通过涂抹的点源的字符串启发的长度尺度$l_0$，获得一个奇异的引力势。坐标变换揭示了横向几何是一个零喉Einstein-Rosen虫洞，提供了一个明确的几何实现的纠缠光子的ER=EPR猜想。重要的是，我们证明了引力自能依赖于光子的纵向长度L$（它的波长），对于横向分离的光子对，引力自能被抑制了1/L$，得到E^{\rm GSE}\sim 4G（\hbarω）^2/（c^4 L）\ln（d^2/l_0^2）$。对于在e^{+} e^{-}\to2γ$中产生的背靠背对，虫洞不携带额外的结合能;对数相互作用能只有在纠缠光子分离到距离d$后才出现，从而拉伸了ER桥。我们进一步提供了一个纠缠熵的解释：通过计算冲击波几何中零区间的纠缠熵，并引入有效纠缠温度$k_B T_{\rment}\sim\hbar c/（2πL）$，我们恢复了引力自能的相同标度和归一化。对于可见光子，相应的坍缩时间超过10 ^{30}$年，使得孤立光子不受引力引起的波函数坍缩的影响。这些发现为测试ER=EPR建立了严格的操场，并揭示了超相对论量子的量子引力效应的深度抑制。


### Abstract

We regularize the Aichelburg-Sexl shock-wave metric for massless particles by smearing the point-like source over a string-inspired length scale $l_0$, obtaining a singularity-free gravitational potential. A coordinate transformation reveals that the transverse geometry is a zero-throat Einstein-Rosen wormhole, providing an explicit geometric realization of the ER=EPR conjecture for entangled photons. Crucially, we show that the gravitational self-energy depends on the photon's longitudinal extent $L$ (its wavelength) and, for a transversely separated photon pair, is suppressed by a factor $1/L$, giving $E^{\rm GSE}\sim 4G(\hbarω)^2/(c^4 L)\ln(d^2/l_0^2)$. For the coincident back-to-back pair created in $e^{+} e^{-}\to2γ$, the wormhole carries no additional binding energy; the logarithmic interaction energy emerges only after the entangled photons separate to a distance $d$, stretching the ER bridge. We further provide an entanglement-entropy interpretation: by computing the entanglement entropy of null intervals in the shock-wave geometry and introducing an effective entanglement temperature $k_B T_{\rm ent}\sim\hbar c/(2πL)$, we recover the same scaling and normalization of the gravitational self-energy. For optical photons the corresponding collapse time exceeds $10^{30}$ years, making isolated photons immune to gravity-induced wave-function collapse. These findings establish a rigorous playground for testing ER=EPR and reveal a deep suppression of quantum-gravity effects for ultra-relativistic quanta.


---


## 基于集体自旋和光谱特征的量子Fisher信息的机器学习预测

**Original Title:** Machine-Learning Prediction of Quantum Fisher Information from Collective Spin and Spectral Features

**Authors:** Yusef Maleki, Luis D. Zambrano Palma

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02986v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02986v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

量子费舍尔信息（QFI）是量子计量学中的基本量化器，通过量子Cramér-Rao界限确定参数估计协议中可实现的最终精度。然而，QFI的直接评估通常需要详细了解密度矩阵，随着Hilbert空间维度的增长，其要求越来越高。在这项工作中，我们研究了使用支持载体回归（SVR）从有限的实验可访问量集预测多元量子系统的QFI的程度。通过比较不同的物理动机特征，我们确定了管理QFI的主导特征集，并表明单独集体旋转矩的预测能力随着系统规模的增长而下降，从而导致Hilbert空间维度的增长而下降。我们证明QFI主要由集体协方差和密度矩阵的低级谱矩之间的相互作用决定。我们的结果确定了管理QFI的物理相关信息部门，并证明可以从一组有限的实验可访问量来实现对RST灵敏度的准确估计，而不需要完全的量子状态断层扫描。


### Abstract

Quantum Fisher information (QFI) is a fundamental quantifier in quantum metrology, determining the ultimate precision achievable in parameter-estimation protocols through the quantum Cramér-Rao bound. However, direct evaluation of the QFI generally requires detailed knowledge of the density matrix, making it increasingly demanding as the Hilbert-space dimension grows. In this work, we investigate the extent to which the QFI of multipartite quantum systems can be predicted from a limited set of experimentally accessible quantities using support vector regression (SVR). By comparing different physically motivated features, we identify a dominant feature set governing QFI and show that the predictive power of collective spin moments alone decreases as system size and consequently Hilbert-space dimension grows. We demonstrate that QFI is governed primarily by the interplay between collective covariance and low-order spectral moments of the density matrix. Our results identify the physically relevant information sectors governing the QFI and demonstrate that accurate estimation of metrological sensitivity can be achieved from a restricted set of experimentally accessible quantities without requiring full quantum-state tomography.


---


## 准二维约束中两个异向超冷原子的散射和束缚态

**Original Title:** Scattering and Bound States of Two Heteronuclear Ultracold Atoms in a Quasi-Two-Dimensional Confinement

**Authors:** B. Wang, F. Yang, P. Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02987v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02987v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

我们在准二维（准2D）几何中解决超冷杂原子的二体问题。准2D限制是通过沿着纵向（$z$-）方向的谐振陷阱实现的，两个原子的陷阱频率不同，就像当前关于超冷杂散气体的许多实验中一样。因此，纵向质量中心（CoM）运动与相对运动相耦合，这使两体问题显着复杂化。我们精确地解决了这个问题，并推导出2D散射长度$a_2D}、2D有效射程参数$R_2D}和束缚态能量，作为自由三维（3D）空间中两个原子的$s$波散射长度和有效射程的函数。我们发现，多个二维散射共振可以诱导的纵向CoM和相对运动之间的耦合。在这些共振附近，a_{\rm 2D}$随着三维散射参数的变化而迅速变化，而R_{\rm 2D}$则被强烈增强。由于准二维超冷气体中的有效成对相互作用由下式确定，即，的两体散射振幅和束缚态能量，我们的结果可以用于操纵有效的二维原子间相互作用的准二维超冷异质结气体通过调整限制频率和三维散射参数。


### Abstract

We solve the two-body problem of ultracold heteronuclear atoms in a quasi-two-dimensional (quasi-2D) geometry. The quasi-2D confinement is realized by a harmonic trap along the longitudinal ($z$-) direction, with different trap frequencies for the two atoms, as in many current experiments on ultracold heteronuclear gases. As a consequence, the longitudinal center-of-mass (CoM) motion is coupled to the relative motion, which significantly complicates the two-body problem. We solve this problem exactly and derive the 2D scattering length $a_{\rm 2D}$, the 2D effective range parameter $R_{\rm 2D}$, and the bound-state energies, as functions of the $s$-wave scattering length and effective range of the two atoms in free three-dimensional (3D) space. We show that multiple 2D scattering resonances can be induced by the coupling between the longitudinal CoM and relative motion. Around these resonances, $a_{\rm 2D}$ varies rapidly with the 3D scattering parameters, while $R_{\rm 2D}$ is strongly enhanced. Since the effective pairwise interaction in quasi-2D ultracold gases is determined by i.e., the two-body scattering amplitudes and bound-state energies, our results can be used for manipulating the effective 2D interatomic interaction in quasi-2D ultracold heteronuclear gases by tuning the confinement frequencies and the 3D scattering parameters.


---


## 前向辅助净化：超越传统限制的时空框架

**Original Title:** Forward-Assisted Purification: A Spatiotemporal Framework Beyond Conventional Limits

**Authors:** Fei Meng, Jinge Bao, Yunlong Xiao

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02990v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.02990v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

噪音仍然是实现量子优势的主要障碍，不断降低实现量子技术的资源。净化的目的是通过从有噪音的集合中提取高保真度资源来扭转这种退化，但其传统配方本质上是静态的，只有在噪音生效后才起作用。在这里，我们将净化重新塑造为一项动态任务，引入了一个时空框架，将干预措施分布在整个噪音过程中。这种公式揭示了现有方法无法实现的操作能力，并产生了扩展可实现性能的前向辅助净化。在某些方案中，单拷贝方案已经超过了在常规纯化下用多达50个拷贝可以实现的方案，证明了所需资源的显著开销。除了这些收益之外，我们的框架还规避了传统协议中的非净化定理，包括贝尔态系综，从而实现了以前认为不可能的净化，并指出了减轻量子系统中噪声的有效途径。


### Abstract

Noise remains the primary obstacle to realizing quantum advantage, continuously degrading the resources that enable quantum technologies. Purification aims to reverse this degradation by extracting high-fidelity resources from noisy ensembles, yet its conventional formulation is intrinsically static, acting only after noise has taken effect. Here we instead recast purification as a dynamical task, introducing a spatiotemporal framework that distributes interventions across the noise process. This formulation reveals operational capabilities inaccessible to existing approaches and gives rise to forward-assisted purifications that extend achievable performance. In certain regimes, a single-copy protocol already exceeds what can be achieved with up to 50 copies under conventional purification, demonstrating a significant overhead in required resources. Beyond these gains, our framework circumvents no-purification theorems within conventional protocols, including for Bell-state ensembles, thereby enabling purification previously considered impossible and pointing toward an efficient route to mitigating noise in quantum systems.

## 通过$k $-庞加莱副产品的运动学相关性

**Original Title:** Kinematical correlations via $κ$-Poincaré coproducts

**Authors:** Mohammad Ali Gorji, Babak Vakili

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03004v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03004v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

我们研究$k $-Minkowski时空中霍普夫-代数动量合成定律的运动学结果。相同的曲动量空间可以用不同的坐标来描述。在双叉积基础中，有序平面波标签是描述生成器特征值，因此相关地图是一对一的。相反，在经典基础上，平移特征值$P_μ$与有序平面波标签$p_μ$非线性相关。这种关系在高动能地区可能无法在全球范围内成为一对一的关系。当给定的经典基四动量允许多于一个实辅助前像时，分支敏感量$P_+\equiv P_0+P_4= ke ^{p_0/k}$进入余积并分解分支在两粒子状态下。因此，施加消失的总动量约束会产生依赖于分支的$k $-变形的背靠背动量相关性。在单分支机制中，这只是一个变形的相关产物，而在多分支机制中，仅由$P_μ$指定的状态可以扩展为不同的辅助分支。如果将$P_μ$视为直接有意义的动量，则物理内容就是由此产生的变形相关模式。如果辅助变量$p_μ$被赋予操作意义，则相同的约束状态可以被解释为不同辅助分支上的叠加。我们还将这种结构与标准的规则自伴随非相对论最小长度模型进行了比较，并在其物理域上发现没有类似的光滑局部两实分支倒置。


### Abstract

We study a kinematical consequence of the Hopf-algebraic momentum composition law in $κ$-Minkowski spacetime. The same curved momentum space can be described in different coordinates. In the bicrossproduct basis the ordered-plane-wave labels are the translation-generator eigenvalues, so the relevant map is one-to-one. In the classical basis, instead, the translation eigenvalues $P_μ$ are nonlinearly related to the ordered-plane-wave labels $p_μ$. This relation can fail to be globally one-to-one in a high-momentum region. When a given classical-basis four-momentum admits more than one real auxiliary preimage, the branch-sensitive quantity $P_+\equiv P_0+P_4=κe^{p_0/κ}$ enters the coproduct and resolves the branches in two-particle states. Imposing the vanishing total-momentum constraint therefore gives branch-dependent $κ$-deformed back-to-back momentum correlations. In a single-branch regime this is just a deformed correlated product, while in a multibranch regime a state specified only by $P_μ$ can be expanded into distinct auxiliary branches. If $P_μ$ are taken as the directly meaningful momenta, the physical content is the resulting deformed correlation pattern. If the auxiliary variables $p_μ$ are assigned operational meaning, the same constrained state can be interpreted as a superposition over different auxiliary branches. We also compare this structure with standard regular self-adjoint nonrelativistic minimal-length models and find no analogous smooth local two-real-branch inversion on their physical domains.


---


## 布尔因子分解的图形和代数方法

**Original Title:** Graphical and algebraic methods for Boolean factoring

**Authors:** Simon Martiel, Priyanka Mukhopadhyay

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04038v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04038v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

布尔方程分解问题在经典和量子计算技术中都有着重要的应用。在本文中，我们开发了用于分解ESOP和SOP表达的新颖算法。我们的目标是优化AND计数。AND计数在确定分别用经典和量子电路实现可逆功能所需的AND门和Toffoli门的数量方面发挥着关键作用。我们开发的第一种算法是图形化的。我们将布尔因子分解的问题简化为用二分法覆盖二部图，因此优化覆盖二部图所需的二分法数量，导致因子数量减少，从而减少AND计数。第二种算法是代数算法，源自多元霍纳方法。我们在最多12个变量的随机函数上将我们的算法与EXORCISM-4和EPOEM 2等现有流行方法的性能进行了比较。我们观察到，我们的多元Horner方法速度要快得多，而我们的基于双进制的方法实现了最大的AND计数减少。事实上，与EXORCism-4相比，我们基于二元联的方法实现了高达5倍的AND计数减少。


### Abstract

The problem of factoring Boolean polynomials has significant applications in both classical and quantum computing technology. In this paper we have developed novel algorithms for factoring both ESOP and SOP expressions. Our aim is to optimize the AND-count. The AND-count plays a key role in determining the number of AND and Toffoli gates required to implement a reversible function with classical and quantum circuits, respectively. The first type of algorithms that we develop, are graphical. We reduce the problem of Boolean factoring to covering a bipartite graph with bicliques, and so optimizing the number of bicliques required to cover the bipartite graph, leads to reduced number of factors, and hence AND-count. The second type of algorithm is algebraic, and is derived from multivariate Horner method. We have compared the performances of our algorithms with existing popular methods like EXORCISM-4 and EPOEM2, on random functions of up to 12 variables. We have observed that our multivariate Horner method is substantially faster, while our biclique-based method achieves the maximum AND-count reduction. In fact, compared to EXORCISM-4 our biclique based method achieves up to 5 times reduction in AND-count.


---


## 博弈、集合、量子：Bayesian博弈中相关均衡的参数化量子电路

**Original Title:** Game, Set, Quantum: Parameterized Quantum Circuit for Correlated Equilibrium in Bayesian Games

**Authors:** Param Pathak, Vidhi Oad, Nouhaila Innan, Adarsh Ganesan, Muhammad Shafique

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03109v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03109v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

不完全信息下许多代理人之间的战略决策对于经济、安全和多代理人工智能（AI）至关重要。在这种环境中计算均衡具有挑战性，因为联合类型动作空间随着玩家数量的增加而呈指数级增长。在二进制类型、二进制行动的Bayesian游戏中，类型行动配置文件的显式表示需要O（22 n）条目，这使得直接线性规划（LP）公式在中等玩家数量下具有内存密集型。我们提出了一个混合量子经典框架，用于使用参数化量子电路（PQC）来逼近Bayes相关平衡。PQC代表具有O（nL）可训练参数的条件策略分布，其中n是球员数量，L是赛道深度;对于这里研究的最大设置，n = 10和L = 2，这对应于60个可训练角度。该电路是通过基于梯度的遗憾最小化、负熵正规化器和针对玩家数量的课程表来训练的。在具有两到十个参与者的扑克风格的Bayesian游戏中，所提出的求解器在所有测试的参与者计数中实现了比MCCFR更低的平均剪辑遗憾，在多达八个参与者的情况下实现了比DCFR更低的遗憾，而DCFR在十个参与者中表现最好。这些结果表明，紧凑的PQC参数化可以为近似平衡计算提供可行的变分表示，同时强调了模拟表达能力、优化策略和经典模拟成本的作用。


### Abstract

Strategic decision-making among many agents under incomplete information is central to economics, security, and multi-agent artificial intelligence (AI). Computing equilibria in such settings is challenging because the joint type-action space grows exponentially with the number of players. In binary-type, binary-action Bayesian games, an explicit representation over type-action profiles requires O(22n) entries, making direct linear-programming (LP) formulations memory intensive at moderate player counts. We propose a hybrid quantum-classical framework for approximating Bayes correlated equilibrium using a parameterized quantum circuit (PQC). The PQC represents the conditional strategy distribution with O(nL) trainable parameters, where n is the number of players and L is the circuit depth; for the largest setting studied here, n = 10 and L = 2, this corresponds to 60 trainable angles. The circuit is trained by gradient-based regret minimization with a negative entropy regularizer and a curriculum schedule over player counts. On a poker-style Bayesian game with two to ten players, the proposed solver achieves lower mean clipped regret than MCCFR across all tested player counts and lower regret than DCFR up to eight players, while DCFR performs best at ten players. These results show that compact PQC parameterizations can provide a viable variational representation for approximate equilibrium computation, while highlighting the roles of ansatz expressivity, optimization strategy, and classical simulation cost.


---


## 强相关多体系统的量子优化算法

**Original Title:** Quantum Optimization Algorithms for Strongly Correlated Many-Body Systems

**Authors:** G. E. L. Pexe, L. A. M. Rattighieri, P. M. Prado, A. R. Fritsch, F. F. Fanchini

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03147v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03147v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

这篇前瞻性文章分析了在噪音中等规模量子时代，采用量子优化算法研究量子多体系统中相转变的潜在和关键挑战。由于希尔伯特空间的指数增长和费米子符号问题，强相关系统的模拟在经典计算机上经常很棘手。在此背景下，我们回顾并比较了传统的变分量子算法（例如变分量子特征解算器和量子逼近优化算法）与新兴的启发式方法（特别是基于反馈的量子算法）的性能。我们探索这些方法在研究凝聚态物理学中开放现象中的适用性，包括解构量子临界性、奇异金属、多体局部化、拓扑相转变和量子旋转液体。我们讨论了基本的操作瓶颈，特别是由可表达性和噪音引起的贫瘠高原，如何严重损害基于梯度的优化。我们得出的结论是，确定性反馈引导的方法为导航这些系统的能源格局提供了几何学上更稳健的轨迹，并认为该领域的进一步进步将依赖于深度杂交和基于物理信息的电路协同设计，以实现故障容限。


### Abstract

This perspective article analyzes the potential and critical challenges of employing quantum optimization algorithms to investigate phase transitions in quantum many-body systems during the Noisy Intermediate-Scale Quantum era. The simulation of strongly correlated systems is frequently intractable on classical computers due to the exponential growth of the Hilbert space and the fermionic sign problem. In this context, we review and compare the performance of traditional Variational Quantum Algorithms, such as the Variational Quantum Eigensolver and the Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm, against emerging heuristic approaches, specifically Feedback-based Quantum Algorithms, such as FALQON. We explore the applicability of these methods in the study of open phenomena in condensed matter physics, including Deconfined Quantum Criticality, strange metals, Many-Body Localization, topological phase transitions, and quantum spin liquids. We discuss how fundamental operational bottlenecks, notably expressibility- and noise-induced barren plateaus, severely compromise gradient-based optimization. We conclude that deterministic feedback-guided methods provide geometrically more robust trajectories for navigating the energy landscape of these systems, arguing that further advancement in the field will rely on deep hybridization and physics-informed circuit co-design towards fault tolerance.


---


## 选择后自由产生多子添加相干态

**Original Title:** Post-Selection Free Generation of Multi-Photon Added Coherent States

**Authors:** Mariano Uria, Ricardo Gutiérrez-Jáuregui, Carla Hermann-Avigliano, Pablo Solano

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03167v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03167v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

非高斯量子态是连续变量量子信息处理和计量学的重要资源。其中，多光子附加相干态桥接经典和非经典行为;然而，它们的产生通常依赖于小光子数和概率预报方案。在这里，我们提出了一个协议，用于后选择自由生成高保真度多光子添加相干态的光子阻塞效应在驱动克尔非线性谐振器中，这样的状态自然出现在动态过程中。我们证明，高保真度的状态可以通过优化的外部驱动功率和相互作用时间。此外，我们表明该协议在实际实验条件下是稳健的，使用当前最先进的参数实现了约99%$的稳定性。我们的结果使用成熟的量子光学平台解锁了一条通往复杂非经典状态的确定性途径。


### Abstract

Non-Gaussian quantum states are essential resources for continuous-variable quantum information processing and for metrology. Among these, multi-photon added coherent states bridge classical and non-classical behaviors; however, their generation typically relies on small photon numbers and probabilistic heralding schemes. Here, we propose a protocol for the post-selection free generation of high fidelity multi-photon added coherent states using the photon blockade effect in a driven Kerr nonlinear resonator, where such states emerge naturally during the dynamics. We demonstrate that high-fidelity states can be prepared by optimizing the external drive power and the interaction time. Furthermore, we show that the protocol is robust under realistic experimental conditions, achieving fidelities of $\approx 99\%$ with current state-of-the-art parameters. Our results unlock a deterministic route to complex non-classical states using well-established quantum optical platforms.

## 任意量子状态和经典信息的广义同时传输

**Original Title:** Generalised simultaneous transmission of arbitrary quantum states and classical information

**Authors:** Timothy C. Ralph, Nicholas Zaunders

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03181v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03181v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

我们提出了一种协议，允许任意光量子状态同时携带和传输经典数据，而不牺牲量子或经典信息的完整性。我们的方案在传输之前通过相空间中的位移对经典信息进行编码，并通过高斯连续变量隐形传输检索每个经典符号。然后通过猜测原始位移并执行适当的逆运算来恢复原始量子状态。在足够高的经典信号和高压缩的限制下，我们的方案能够完美地重建输入的经典信号和输入的量子状态，而不损失相关性。以双轨贝尔状态的传输为例。


### Abstract

We present a protocol which allows for arbitrary optical quantum states to simultaneously carry and transmit classical data, without sacrificing the integrity of either the quantum or classical information. Our scheme encodes classical information via displacements in the phase space prior to transmission and retrieves each classical symbol via a Gaussian continuous-variable teleportation. The original quantum state is then restored by guessing the the original displacement and performing the appropriate inverse operation. In the limit of sufficiently high classical signal and high squeezing, we show that our scheme is capable of perfectly reconstructing both the input classical signal and the input quantum state without loss of coherence. An example is given in terms of the transmission of a dual-rail Bell state.


---


## Denspirk-子图问题的混合量子增强解

**Original Title:** Towards a Hybrid Quantum Enhanced Solution for Densest k-Subgraph Problem

**Authors:** Ravi Sangwan, Prabhat Anand, M Girish Chandra

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03196v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03196v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

本文研究了高斯玻色子采样（GBS）在求解可重构子图问题（DkSP）中的应用。由于严格的基数约束，具有硬后选择的GBS具有较差的采样效率。为了解决这个问题，我们引入了有效的经典后处理策略，将接近k的样本转换为可行的解决方案。一组全面的模拟进行，表明这些方法实现了接近最优的解决方案的质量，同时提高采样效率约4倍相比，社区结构图上的后选择，也后选择往往无法达到稀疏随机图上的最优解，即使大量的样本。此外，针对中等大小的图形，所提出的方法的性能与已建立的经典方法相当，甚至在某些情况下优于这些方法。总体而言，结果表明，虽然仅采用后选择的GBS还不够，但其与轻量级经典细化的结合可以非常有效。这强调了混合量子经典框架的潜力，并将GBS定位为组合图优化的有前途的采样基元。


### Abstract

We study the application of Gaussian Boson Sampling (GBS) to the densest k-subgraph problem (DkSP). GBS with hard post-selection suffers from poor sampling efficiency due to strict cardinality constraints. To address this limitation, we introduce effective classical post-processing strategies that transform, otherwise discarded, near-k samples into feasible solutions. A comprehensive set of simulations is carried out, demonstrating that these approaches achieve near-optimal solution quality while improving sampling efficiency by approximately 4X compared to post-selection on community-structured graphs, and also post-selection often fails to reach the optimal solution on sparse random graphs even with large number of samples. Furthermore, the proposed methods perform on par with, and in some cases outperform, established classical approaches for graphs up to moderate size. Overall, the results indicate that while GBS with post-selection alone is insufficient, its combination with lightweight classical refinement can be highly effective. This underscores the potential of hybrid quantum-classical frameworks and positions GBS as a promising sampling primitive for combinatorial graph optimization.

## 分数量子力学的微扰结果

**Original Title:** Perturbative results for fractional quantum mechanics

**Authors:** Claude Semay, Clara Tourbez, Loïc Keszeli

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03226v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03226v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

研究分数薛定汉方程的动能稍微偏离通常的非相对论形式。谐振子和Kepler问题都在小扰动的背景下处理。使用通常的微扰理论并与信封理论进行比较。分析结果显示两种方法之间具有良好的一致性，这表明了多体系统未来可能的发展。简要讨论了与实验观察的可能联系。


### Abstract

The fractional Schrödinger equation is studied with a kinetic energy that slightly deviates from the usual nonrelativistic form. The harmonic oscillator and the Kepler problem are both treated in the context of small perturbations. The usual perturbation theory is used and compared with the envelope theory. The analytical results show good agreement between both methods, indicating possible future developments for many-body systems. A possible connection with experimental observations is briefly discussed.

## AND-函数的量子经典等效性

**Original Title:** Quantum-Classical Equivalence for AND-Functions

**Authors:** Sreejata Kishor Bhattacharya, Farzan Byramji, Arkadev Chattopadhyay, Yogesh Dahiya, Shachar Lovett

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03249v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03249v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

量子通信复杂性中的一个主要开放问题是，量子协议在计算总布尔函数方面是否可以比经典协议以指数级更高效;普遍的猜测是，它们不可能如此。在一项开创性的工作中，Razborov（2002）解决了形式为$$ F（x，y）= f（x_1 \land y_1，\ldots，x_n \land y_n），$$当外部函数$f$对称时，通过证明它们的有界误差量子复杂性和经典通信复杂性是多元相关的。从那时起，将此结果扩展到所有AND函数一直处于开放状态，并已由几位作者提出。   在这项工作中，我们以强有力的方式解决了这个问题。我们表明，对于每个布尔函数$f$，函数$f \circ \mathrm{AND}_2$的有界误差量子和经典确定性通信复杂性是多元相关的，直到$n$中的多对数因子。我们通过证明两者都由$f$的德摩根稀疏度的对数值来描述（直到多项损失）来证明这一点。   我们的结果基于Chattopadhyay、Dahiya和Lovett（2025）最近关于非稀疏布尔函数结构特征的工作，我们将其扩展以解决一般AND函数的猜测。


### Abstract

A major open problem in quantum communication complexity is whether quantum protocols can be exponentially more efficient than classical protocols for computing total Boolean functions; the prevailing conjecture is that they cannot be so. In a seminal work, Razborov (2002) resolved this question for AND-functions of the form $$ F(x,y) = f(x_1 \land y_1, \ldots, x_n \land y_n), $$ when the outer function $f$ is symmetric, by proving that their bounded-error quantum and classical communication complexities are polynomially related. Since then, extending this result to all AND-functions has remained open and has been posed by several authors.
  In this work, we settle this problem in a strong way. We show that for every Boolean function $f$, the bounded-error quantum and classical deterministic communication complexities of the function $f \circ \mathrm{AND}_2$ are polynomially related, up to polylogarithmic factors in $n$. We prove this by showing that both are characterized--up to polynomial loss--by the logarithm of the De Morgan sparsity of $f$.
  Our results build on the recent work of Chattopadhyay, Dahiya, and Lovett (2025) on structural characterizations of non-sparse Boolean functions, which we extend to resolve the conjecture for general AND-functions.


---


## 在WSe$2 $包封单层石墨烯中定制纯valley-Zeeman旋转轨道耦合

**Original Title:** Tailoring pure valley-Zeeman spin-orbit coupling in WSe$_2$-encapsulated monolayer graphene

**Authors:** Yaqing Han, Siqi Jiang, Jingkuan Xiao, Jiawei Jiang, Yulu Liu, Jiabei Huang, Yu Du, Di Zhang, Fuzhuo Lian, Wanting Xu, Siqin Wang, Kenji Watanabe, Takashi Taniguchi, Xiaoxiang Xi, Alexander S. Mayorov, Renjun Du, Kai Chang, Hongxin Yang, Lei Wang, Geliang Yu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03278v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03278v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

扭曲范德华异质结构中的工程邻近效应为设计电子特性提供了一个强大的平台。虽然过渡金属二硫属化物封装的石墨烯中的量子干涉的理论预测可以选择性地控制自旋轨道耦合分量，但实验实现仍然难以捉摸。在这里，我们报告纯谷塞曼自旋轨道耦合在单层石墨烯，实现两个平行的扭曲WSe$_2$单层之间的封装。我们观察到朗道能级的一种强迫重排，这是由固定的谷塞曼能量和磁场依赖的回旋能量之间的竞争驱动的。这种重新排序的特征是从量子霍尔效应中的果冻破缺状态转变为具有整或半整量子霍尔序列的恢复的四重简并性。我们还证明了通过调整封装的几何形状来完全抑制邻近旋转轨道耦合的能力。


### Abstract

Engineering proximity effects in twisted van der Waals heterostructures offers a powerful platform for designing electronic properties. While theoretical predictions of quantum interference in transition metal dichalcogenide-encapsulated graphene can selectively control the spin-orbit coupling component, experimental realizations have remained elusive. Here, we report pure valley-Zeeman spin-orbit coupling in monolayer graphene, achieved by encapsulation between two parallel twisted WSe$_2$ monolayers. We observed a symmetry-enforced reordering of Landau levels, which is driven by the competition between the fixed valley-Zeeman energy and the magnetic-field-dependent cyclotron energy. This reordering is characterized by a transition from symmetry-broken states in the quantum Hall effect to a restored fourfold degeneracy with integer or half-integer quantum Hall sequences. We also demonstrate the ability to completely quench the proximity spin-orbit coupling by tuning the encapsulated geometry.

## 确定性地生成具有超过100美元的量子消耗下的猫状态

**Original Title:** Deterministic generation of cat states with more than $100$ photons under dissipation

**Authors:** Zhu-yao Jin, Jun Jing

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03293v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03293v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

大尺寸猫态对于探索量子到经典的转变尤其有意义和基础，也是量子计量和容错量子计算的有前途的资源。然而，由于去同下的脆弱性日益增加，放大猫状态的规模仍然具有挑战性。我们提议在厄米特或非厄米特含时Hamilton下使用混合量子位玻色子系统的动力学不变量来生成大猫状态。这是一项使用普适量子控制（UQC）理论的研究，其中通过以量子位状态为条件的正变换在辅助图像中分析系统动力学。可以编码在动力不变量的演变中的可控动力学由海森堡方程给出，该方程对汉密尔顿量施加了约束。当量子位在平衡叠加状态下准备时，玻色子模可以从真空状态决定性地演变为平均量子数超过120美元的猫状态。在埃尔米特主义的情况下，一代是完美的;在非埃尔米特主义的情况下，保真度超过0.962美元。我们的协议还可以应用于本质猫状态和大尺寸四分量猫状态的生成。通过制备宏观量子状态，我们的工作本质上将UQC推进到混合离散-连续变量系统。


### Abstract

Large-size cat states are especially meaningful and fundamental for exploring the quantum-to-classical transition, as well as promising resources for quantum metrology and fault-tolerant quantum computation. However, amplifying the magnitude of cat states remains challenging because of the growing fragility under decoherence. We propose to generate large cat states by using the dynamical invariant of hybrid qubit-bosonic systems under Hermitian or non-Hermitian time-dependent Hamiltonian. It is a study with the universal quantum control (UQC) theory, in which the system dynamics is analyzed in the ancillary picture via a unitary transformation conditional on the qubit state. The controllable dynamics that can be encoded in the evolution of the dynamical invariant is presented by the Heisenberg equation, which imposes constrains on the Hamiltonian. When the qubit is prepared in a balanced superposed state, the bosonic mode can evolve deterministically from the vacuum state to the cat state of a mean photon number over $120$. In the Hermitian case, the generation is perfect; and in the non-Hermitian case, the fidelity is over $0.962$. Our protocol can also be applied to the generation of the intrinsic cat states and the four-component cat states of large size. Through the preparation of macroscopic quantum states, our work essentially advances UQC to hybrid discrete-continuous variable systems.


---


## 芯片纠缠纯化中剩余纠缠的观察

**Original Title:** Observation of residual entanglement in chip-based entanglement purification

**Authors:** Yonghe Yu, Mujtaba Zahidy, Siyan Zhou, Caterina Vigliar, Karsten Rottwitt, Leif Katsuo Oxenløwe, Yunhong Ding

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03343v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03343v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

纠缠净化是量子转发器的重要组成部分，因为它可以提高分布纠缠态的保真度并减轻有噪通道的影响。成功的纯化产生了保真度增加的纠缠状态，而失败的事件仍然可以保留剩余纠缠，当两个自由度（DOF）的错误率不平衡时，这些纠缠仍然可用于进一步的纯化。本文利用硅芯片演示了一种基于超纠缠的单副本纠缠纯化方案，并实验观察了剩余纠缠的存在。利用集成光电子学的可重新配置性，我们的方案确保在作用于两个自由度的位翻转噪音下，始终可以获得适合进一步纯化的剩余纠缠，无论哪个自由度具有更高的错误率。我们的结果展示了集成光电子学在量子信息处理中的优势，并为片上纠缠纯化和未来量子转发器系统中纠缠资源的优化利用提供指导。


### Abstract

Entanglement purification is an essential component of quantum repeaters, as it can improve the fidelity of the distributed entangled states and mitigate the effects of the noisy channel. Successful purification yields entangled states with increased fidelity, whereas failed events can still retain residual entanglement that remains usable for further purification when the error rates of the two degrees of freedom (DOFs) are unbalanced. In this paper, we demonstrate a single-copy entanglement purification scheme based on hyperentanglement using silicon chips and experimentally observe the presence of residual entanglement. Leveraging the reconfigurability of integrated photonics, our scheme ensures that, under bit-flip noise acting on the two DOFs, residual entanglement suitable for further purification can always be obtained, regardless of which DOF has the higher error rate. Our results demonstrate the advantages of integrated photonics for quantum information processing and provide guidance for the optimized utilization of entanglement resources in on-chip entanglement purification and future quantum repeater systems.


---


## 基于伊辛哈密顿相位预言的能量选择量子搜索

**Original Title:** Energy-selective quantum search with Ising Hamiltonian phase oracles

**Authors:** A. S. Plyashechnik, A. A. Zhukov, A. V. Lebedev, W. V. Pogosov

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03380v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.03380v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

伊辛·汉密尔顿体是无序磁铁的基本模型，也是量子和经典优化的标准语言。我们研究了一个能量选择性量子搜索基元，其中物理进化\（\BEP（-\mathrm{i} TH）\）直接用作汉密尔顿相预言。与布尔Oracle不同，该Oracle通过相连续标记配置，并选择有限的共振带而不是预先分配的标记集。我们表明，将其与格罗弗扩散操作符交替仍然会产生格罗弗型放大峰。精确的光谱回归和生成函数表示确定峰位置、宽度和高度。对于已变形的高斯态密度，当共振包含\（M\）配置时，高密度尾部中的目标能量需要\（（\squtt {2 ' n/M}）\）Oracle调用。对于随机伊辛光谱，拉曼引起的相关性会移动和扭曲峰值;光谱对称化和迭代校准消除了规定能量目标的失调。


### Abstract

Ising Hamiltonians are basic models of disordered magnets and a standard language for quantum and classical optimization. We study an energy-selective quantum search primitive in which the physical evolution \(\exp(-\mathrm{i} T H)\) is used directly as a Hamiltonian phase oracle. Unlike a Boolean oracle, this oracle marks configurations continuously by their phases and selects a finite resonance band rather than a preassigned marked set. We show that alternating it with the Grover diffusion operator nevertheless produces a Grover-type amplification peak. An exact spectral recurrence and a generating-function representation determine the peak position, width, and height. For an annealed Gaussian density of states, target energies in a high-density tail require \(Θ(\sqrt{2^n/M})\) oracle calls when the resonance contains \(M\) configurations. For random Ising spectra, overlap-induced correlations shift and distort the peak; spectral symmetrization and iterative calibration remove this detuning for prescribed-energy targeting.
