## 全计数统计揭示量子弦相互作用

**Original Title:** Quantum String Interactions Revealed by Full Counting Statistics

**Authors:** Chang-Yan Wang, Xue-Feng Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04086v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04086v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

量子弦如何相互作用是量子多体物理学中扩展物体的一个基本问题。即使是最简单的硬核约束（无交叉），也可以产生一个非平凡的有效势，其微观形式很难确定，因为弦之间的相对距离本质上是非局部的。在这里，我们表明这种非局部性自然会被全计数统计量（FCS）捕获。对于两个硬核量子弦，我们通过识别两个弦接触和跳回的虚拟过程来推导出紧急相互作用的解析FCS表达。使用FCS--纠缠关系，我们发现有效势具有纠缠控制的渐进形式$\lnA E（r）\sim -pi #2 r#2/（12 S_\ell）$直到次引导项，其中$S_\ell$是量子弦两半之间的纠缠量。我们使用高精度数值计算和有限规模的FCS估计来证实该理论。我们的结果揭示了FCS是量子布局线缺陷之间有效相互作用的直接途径，其也可以扩展到更高级形式的电荷。


### Abstract

How quantum strings interact is a basic question for extended objects in quantum many-body physics. Even the simplest hard-core constraint (no crossing), can generate a nontrivial effective potential, whose microscopic form is difficult to determine because the relative distance between the strings is intrinsically nonlocal. Here we show that this nonlocality is naturally captured by full counting statistics (FCS). For two hard-core quantum strings, we derive an analytic FCS expression for the emergent interaction by identifying the virtual process in which the two strings touch and hop back. Using the FCS--entanglement relation, we find the effective potential has the entanglement-controlled asymptotic form $\lnΔE(r)\sim -π^2 r^2/(12 S_\ell)$ up to subleading terms, where $S_\ell$ is the entanglement entropy between the two halves of a quantum string. We confirm the theory using high-precision numerical calculations and finite-size FCS estimates. Our results reveal FCS as a direct route to effective interactions between quantum topological line-defects, which may also be extended to higher-form charge.


---


## 具有最大似然估计的更好泡利通道学习

**Original Title:** Better Pauli Channel Learning with Maximum Likelihood Estimation

**Authors:** Daniel Belkin, Faisal Alam, Matthew Thibodeau, Alireza Seif, Ewout van den Berg, Bryan K. Clark

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04096v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04096v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

有噪量子设备中的错误缓解需要对噪音通道进行非常好的估计。概率误差消除的准确性通常受到通道断层扫描的高样本复杂性的限制。原则上，最佳样本复杂性是通过最大似然估计（MLE）获得的，但MLE在计算上具有挑战性。我们表明，在某些感兴趣的情况下，MLE可以在计算上易于处理。对于1D本地稀疏Pauli-Lindblad通道的常见情况，似然函数简化为可高效评估的Bayesian网络。我们表明，由此产生的计算极大地改善了断层扫描。此外，我们通过模拟证明，这可以带来有意义的改进错误缓解的费用。我们还讨论了将我们的算法扩展到更一般的设置，例如非1D电路和非泡利误差。


### Abstract

Error mitigation in a noisy quantum device requires a very good estimate of the noise channel. The accuracy of probabilistic error cancellation is often limited by the high sample complexity of channel tomography. In principle, optimal sample complexity is attained by maximum likelihood estimation (MLE), but MLE is computationally challenging. We show that MLE can be made computationally tractable in certain cases of interest. For the common case of a 1D-local sparse Pauli-Lindblad channel, the likelihood function reduces to an efficiently-evaluable Bayesian network. We show that the resulting computation leads to substantially improved tomography. In addition, we demonstrate by simulation that this can lead to meaningful improvements to the overhead of error mitigation. We also discuss possible extensions of our algorithm to more general settings, such as non-1D circuits and non-Pauli errors.


---


## 宏观物体的引力引起的量子退相关

**Original Title:** Gravitationally Induced Quantum Decoherence of Macroscopic Objects

**Authors:** Hiroki Takeda, Shogo Tomizuka, Takahiro Tanaka

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04099v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04099v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

我们公式化了在空间叠加中准备的大质量物体的引力引起的量子退散。从线性化重力与大质量系统粒子和环境纯量场的耦合开始，我们推导出了控制简化系统动力学的封闭时间路径影响函数。在非相对论性和准静态区域中，去相干指数可以写成系统应力-能量张量之差的双线性函数，以及通过用引力子传播子修饰环境应力-能量张量相关器而获得的有效噪音核。然后，我们将这个框架应用于牛顿的远程引力相互作用，并评估由有限波包建模并在时间和空间上粗粒度的稀释非相对论气体的退散函数。通过执行受控逼近，我们获得了累积去相关函数的解析表达，并表明主要贡献在很宽的距离范围内以数学方式积累，而在现实条件下仍然低于传统的碰撞去相关。


### Abstract

We formulate the gravitationally induced quantum decoherence of a massive object prepared in a spatial superposition. Starting from linearized gravity coupled to a massive system particle and an environmental scalar field, we derive a closed-time-path influence functional governing the reduced system dynamics. In the nonrelativistic and quasi-static regime, the decoherence exponent can be written as a bilinear functional of the difference of the system stress-energy tensors and an effective noise kernel obtained by dressing the environmental stress-energy tensor correlator with graviton propagators. We then apply this framework to the Newtonian long-range gravitational interaction and evaluate the resulting decoherence function for a dilute nonrelativistic gas modeled by finite wave packets and coarse-grained in time and space. By performing controlled approximations, we obtain analytic expressions for the cumulative decoherence function and show that the dominant contribution is accumulated logarithmically over a broad range of distances, while remaining subdominant to conventional collisional decoherence under realistic conditions.


---


## 并行量子流算法捕获量子信息

**Original Title:** Quantum Information Harvesting with the Parallel Quantum Flow Algorithm

**Authors:** Nicholas P. Bauman, Ajay Panyala, Chenxu Liu, Muqing Zheng, Meng Wang, Karol Kowalski

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04186v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04186v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

量子流（QFlow）算法提供了一个资源高效的框架，用于描述混合量子经典架构上的相关多体系统。通过实现量子和经典资源的并行利用，QFlow提供了一种模拟现实系统的可扩展途径。在这封信中，我们报告了一种基于单双模型的QFlow形式主义的高性能计算（IPC）实现。我们展示了其对包含82和114个轨道的目标空间的性能，其中流包括6个活性轨道类型活性空间中的所有6个活性电子。在最大的QFlow模拟中，我们使用相当于12个量子比特的值优化了117万个波函数参数。尽管适度的量子位的要求的基本活动空间的问题，该方法恢复超过95\%$的总相关能量与耦合簇的单打和双打（CCSD）的方法为主的系统的动态相关效应，这仍然是具有挑战性的现有的量子算法。我们进一步表明，QFlow形式主义在扩展的基组与扩散函数中保持了高精度，突出了其现实的大规模量子化学模拟的潜力。


### Abstract

The Quantum Flow (QFlow) algorithm provides a resource-efficient framework for describing correlated many-body systems on hybrid quantum-classical architectures. By enabling parallel utilization of quantum and classical resources, QFlow offers a scalable pathway toward simulations of realistic systems. In this Letter, we report a high-performance computing (HPC) implementation of the QFlow formalism based on a singles-and-doubles model. We demonstrate its performance for target spaces comprising 82 and 114 orbitals, where the flow includes all 6 active electrons in 6 active orbitals type active spaces. In the largest QFlow simulations, we optimize 1.17 million wave function parameters using the equivalent of 12 qubits. Despite the modest qubit requirements of the underlying active-space problems, the method recovers over $95\%$ of the total correlation energy obtained with the coupled cluster singles and doubles (CCSD) approach for systems dominated by dynamical correlation effects, which remain challenging for existing quantum algorithms. We further show that the QFlow formalism retains high accuracy in extended basis sets with diffuse functions, highlighting its potential for realistic large-scale quantum chemistry simulations.

## 通过零平移模出现宏观量子序

**Original Title:** Emergence of Macroscopic Quantum Order via Translational Zero Modes

**Authors:** Kenan Gundogdu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04187v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04187v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

固体（例如超流体、超导体和凝聚物）中的宏观量子相干性通常仅限于低温，因为有序在固定的激发光谱内形成，随着温度的升高，其竞争状态变得热填充。在这里，我们表明电子激励和可变形网格之间的强耦合可以实现不同的路径。在临界密度以上，这种耦合使自发的限制势成核，从而捕获产生它们的激发。与刚性外部陷阱不同，这些势可以在不改变其内部结构的情况下通过宿主网格进行平移，从而定义了平移零模式。与这个零模式的耦合提供了一个共享的动力学坐标，该坐标降低和隔离了单个集体的多体配置，打开了一个依赖密度的间隙，该间隙抑制竞争状态的热占据，并支持高温下的非对角长程有序。作为一个具体的实现，我们将卤铅钙钛中的高温超荧光识别为这种零模修饰有序激子状态的辐射不稳定性。更广泛地说，这建立了通往宏观量子有序的一般途径：不是在固定光谱内冷却，也不是配对不稳定性，而是一种自生成的移动限制结构，其平移零模重建了多体光谱以保护相干性。


### Abstract

Macroscopic quantum coherence in solids, such as in superfluids, superconductors, and condensates, is generally limited to low temperatures because order forms within a fixed excitation spectrum whose competing states become thermally populated as temperature rises. Here, we show that strong coupling between electronic excitations and a deformable lattice enables a different route. Above a critical density, this coupling nucleates self generated confining potentials that trap the very excitations generating them. Unlike rigid external traps, these potentials can translate through the host lattice without changing their internal structure, defining a translational zero mode. Coupling to this zero mode provides a shared dynamical coordinate that lowers and isolates a single collective many body configuration, opening a density dependent gap that suppresses thermal occupation of competing states and supports off diagonal long range order at elevated temperatures. As a concrete realization, we identify high-temperature superfluorescence in lead halide perovskites as the radiative instability of this zero mode dressed ordered excitonic state. More broadly, this establishes a general route to macroscopic quantum order: not cooling within a fixed spectrum, nor pairing instabilities, but a self generated mobile confining structure whose translational zero mode reconstructs the many-body spectrum to protect coherence.


---


## 通过部署的多核光纤上的全核模式编码进行多维量子密钥分发

**Original Title:** High-Dimensional Quantum Key Distribution via full Core-mode Encoding over Deployed Multicore Fibers

**Authors:** G. H. dos Santos, K. B. Sawada, N. Villalba, C. Jara, N. Guerrero, C. Melo, M. H. Magiotto, D. Martínez, G. B. Xavier, J. Cariñe, G. Saavedra, E. S. Gómez, S. P. Walborn, G. Lima

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04211v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04211v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

量子密钥分发（QKD）提供植根于量子物理学的信息理论安全性，而多维（HD）编码则提高了噪音容限和密钥收益率。多核光纤（MFC）是下一代电信网络的领先平台，是HD-QKD的天然基础。到目前为止，部署的MFC上的现场演示依赖于混合qudit编码策略，该策略将两条路径（核心模式）与时间点光自由度相结合，而不是利用全套可用的核心模式。尽管实用，但这种方法会带来随着维度而增长的内在效率损失。在这里，我们实现了一个四维（$d=4$）QKD协议，直接利用了一个四核心MCF的核心模式的全套，在安装MCF网络在康塞普西翁大学校园连续环境扰动下运行。我们进一步使用超导纳米线探测器在10 dB信道损耗下对该方案进行基准测试，实现了R = 6.19 × 10 - 3，$bits/脉冲的可组合有限密钥速率，这是迄今为止报道的HD-QKD在可比损耗下的最高单脉冲速率。这一结果确立了核心模式编码作为一个可行的架构，现实的，高速率的量子安全通信。


### Abstract

Quantum key distribution (QKD) provides information-theoretic security rooted in quantum physics, while high-dimensional (HD) encoding increases both noise tolerance and secret-key yield. Multicore fibers (MCFs), a leading platform for next-generation telecom networks, are a natural substrate for HD-QKD. Field demonstrations over deployed MCFs have so far relied on a hybrid qudit encoding strategy that combines two path (core modes) with the time-bin photonic degree of freedom, rather than exploiting the full set of available core modes. Although practical, this approach incurs intrinsic efficiency penalties that grow with dimension. Here we implement a four-dimensional ($d=4$) QKD protocol that directly exploits the full set of core modes of a four-core MCF, operating over an installed MCF network across the Universidad de Concepción campus under continuous environmental perturbations. We further benchmark the scheme using superconducting nanowire detectors at $10\,$dB channel loss, achieving a composable finite-key rate of $R = 6.19\times 10^{-3}\,$bits/pulse, the highest per-pulse rate reported to date for HD-QKD at comparable loss. This result establishes core-mode encoding as a viable architecture for realistic, high-rate quantum-secure communications.

## 量子镜实现连续变量量子状态断层扫描

**Original Title:** Continuous-Variable Quantum State Tomography Enabled by Quantum Mirrors

**Authors:** Mariano Uria, Amaru Moya, Carla Hermann-Avigliano, Pablo Solano, Aldo Delgado

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04277v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04277v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

在量子技术中，连续变量系统比离散系统具有优势。然而，连续变量断层扫描的样本复杂性呈指数级增长。我们提出了使用量子镜将事件光态的完整信息传输到控制原子系统的协议。这使得通过仅对控制原子进行测量来实现完全的光状态特征化，通过核函数、直接波函数重建和逐点维格纳函数测量来实现。我们的方法克服了传统的光子计数，统计推断和逆变换的局限性，提供了一个强大的框架基准和验证非高斯状态在连续变量量子光学。


### Abstract

In quantum technologies, continuous-variable systems offer advantages over their discrete counterparts. However, continuous-variable tomography suffers from exponentially growing sample complexity. We propose protocols using quantum mirrors to transfer the complete information of incident photonic states onto a control atomic system. This enables full photonic state characterization through measurements on the control atom alone, realized via kernel functions, direct wavefunction reconstruction, and pointwise Wigner function measurements. Our approach overcomes the limitations of conventional photon counting, statistical inference, and inverse transformation, providing a robust framework for benchmarking and verifying non-Gaussian states in continuous-variable quantum optics.


---


## 交换相关函数的派生知情学习

**Original Title:** Derivative Informed Learning of Exchange-Correlation Functionals

**Authors:** Eike S. Eberhard, Luca A. Thiede, Abdul Aldossary, Andreas Burger, Nicholas Gao, Vignesh Bhethanabotla, Alán Aspuru-Guzik, Stephan Günnemann

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04279v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04279v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

Machine-learned (ML) exchange-correlation (XC) functionals aim to replace human-designed density functional approximations by learning directly from reference data, but they still do not consistently outperform traditional $\mathcal{O}(N^4)$-scaling hybrid functionals. We study a hybrid-distillation setting in which $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$-scaling ML-XC functionals are trained to reproduce B3LYP/def2-SVP targets. We introduce Derivative Informed XC-Loss (DI-Loss), a loss that incorporates additional information from the reference hybrid functional by supervising first and second derivatives of the energy on the Grassmannian of admissible density matrices. Rather than only matching the self-consistent fixed point, DI-Loss aligns the local first- and second-order response of the learned functional with that of the target functional. Across four evaluated architectures, DI-Loss consistently improves the main energy metrics. Averaged uniformly across architectures, the total-energy MAE decreases by 66% relative to energy and density supervision alone. The density-sensitive mean-field energy metric $E_ρ$ improves from $1.2$ to $0.8$ mEh on average, while dipole and $\mathcal{L}_2$ density errors do not improve uniformly. We further show that densities from the distilled functionals reduce hybrid-functional SCF iterations by up to 50%. In downstream TDDFT calculations, Hessian supervision improves excited-state predictions, with XCdiff reducing the mean excitation-energy MAE by 19 - 35%.


### Abstract

Machine-learned (ML) exchange-correlation (XC) functionals aim to replace human-designed density functional approximations by learning directly from reference data, but they still do not consistently outperform traditional $\mathcal{O}(N^4)$-scaling hybrid functionals. We study a hybrid-distillation setting in which $\mathcal{O}(N^3)$-scaling ML-XC functionals are trained to reproduce B3LYP/def2-SVP targets. We introduce Derivative Informed XC-Loss (DI-Loss), a loss that incorporates additional information from the reference hybrid functional by supervising first and second derivatives of the energy on the Grassmannian of admissible density matrices. Rather than only matching the self-consistent fixed point, DI-Loss aligns the local first- and second-order response of the learned functional with that of the target functional. Across four evaluated architectures, DI-Loss consistently improves the main energy metrics. Averaged uniformly across architectures, the total-energy MAE decreases by 66% relative to energy and density supervision alone. The density-sensitive mean-field energy metric $E_ρ$ improves from $1.2$ to $0.8$ mEh on average, while dipole and $\mathcal{L}_2$ density errors do not improve uniformly. We further show that densities from the distilled functionals reduce hybrid-functional SCF iterations by up to 50%. In downstream TDDFT calculations, Hessian supervision improves excited-state predictions, with XCdiff reducing the mean excitation-energy MAE by 19 - 35%.

## 半经典逼近下数字量子计算机上半导体超快光谱的量子模拟

**Original Title:** Quantum simulations of ultrafast optical spectroscopy of semiconductors on digital quantum computers in the semi-classical approximation

**Authors:** Mykhailo Klymenko, Bahar Goldozian, Thong Hoang, Jared H. Cole, Muhammad Usman

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04295v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04295v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-02


### 摘要

我们提出了一个用于半导体材料超快光谱的数字量子模拟框架。该框架基于布里渊区离散化和二次量子化形式主义，被设计为基于半导体布洛赫方程的经典模拟的量子替代方案。其当前的能力包括线性吸收和光学收益光谱的量子模拟，结合洛伦兹增宽、有限温度带填充效应和降维效应。与经典模拟的基准比较证明了无噪音极限的定量一致。NISQ时代量子计算机的现实硬件噪音有效地表现为散射过程的额外来源，导致光谱增宽。虽然在单粒子逼近中预计不会出现指数级量子优势，但该框架自然扩展到多体体系，其中经典模拟面临层次问题，并且指数级缩放和可证明的量子优势将成为可能。这项工作中考虑的量子模拟捕捉了半导体光谱学的核心元素，例如开放量子系统、光物质相互作用、统计力学、非平衡量子动力学和多体物理学。因此，它提供了一种物理驱动且可扩展的模型，用于对量子计算机进行复杂现实世界问题的应用程序进行基准测试。


### Abstract

We present a digital quantum simulation framework for ultrafast optical spectroscopy of semiconductor materials. The framework is based on Brillouin-zone discretization and the second-quantization formalism, and is designed as a quantum alternative to classical simulations based on the semiconductor Bloch equations. Its current capabilities include quantum simulations of linear absorption and optical gain spectra, incorporating Lorentzian broadening, finite-temperature band-filling effects, and reduced-dimensionality effects. Benchmark comparisons with classical simulations for GaAs demonstrate quantitative agreement in the noiseless limit. The inclusion of realistic hardware noise of NISQ-era quantum computers effectively manifests itself as an additional source of scattering processes, resulting in increased spectral broadening. While no exponential quantum advantage is expected in the single-particle approximation, the framework naturally extends to many-body regimes where classical simulations face the hierarchy problem and exponential scaling and provable quantum advantage will be possible. The quantum simulations considered in this work capture central elements of semiconductor spectroscopy, the aspects such as open quantum systems, light-matter interactions, statistical mechanics, non-equilibrium quantum dynamics, and many-body physics. As such, it provides a physically motivated and scalable model for benchmarking quantum computers in applications to complex, real-world problems.


---


## 非相互作用量子发射极之间的光预示量子操作中误差的特征

**Original Title:** Characterization of errors in photon-heralded quantum operations between non-interacting quantum emitters

**Authors:** Mahsa Karimi, Samuel Mister, Christoph Simon, Stephen C. Wein

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04312v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04312v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们开发了一个分析微扰框架，该框架能够分析非相互作用发射体之间的概率、量子预示量子操作中的小马尔科夫误差。在零光生成（ZPG）框架的基础上并扩展了封闭形式的微扰解，该解捕获了以时间积分的量子计数为条件的理想（零阶）和有噪（低级）门动力学。我们的框架为过程矩阵和泡利误差权重提供了最高阶的分析解决方案，弥合了系统的详细物理缺陷与其相应的抽象泡利噪音模型之间的差距。此外，我们的框架捕捉到了整个物理系统堆栈中的缺陷，从量子产生到光学操纵。我们将重复直至成功的CZ门上产生的微扰预测与数值模拟进行基准测试，展示了源感应噪音的准确建模，然后应用相同的框架来分析作为光学操纵错误的代表性示例的连贯移相器误校准。这项工作中开发的方法使得基于物理学的参数调整能够优化门设计，并开发定制的量子误差纠正协议，以实现使用混合光-物质量子系统的容差量子计算。


### Abstract

We develop an analytic perturbative framework that enables the analysis of small Markovian errors in probabilistic, photon-heralded quantum operations between non-interacting emitters. Building on and extending the Zero-Photon-Generation (ZPG) framework, we derive closed-form perturbative solutions that capture both ideal (zero-order) and noisy (low-order) gate dynamics conditioned on time-integrated photon counting. Our framework provides analytic solutions to process matrices and Pauli error weights up to leading order, bridging the gap between detailed physical imperfections of a system and its corresponding abstract Pauli noise models. Moreover, our framework captures imperfections across the full physical system stack, from photon generation to optical manipulation. We benchmark the resulting perturbative predictions on a repeat-until-success CZ gate against numerical simulations, demonstrating accurate modeling of source-induced noise, and then apply the same framework to analyze coherent phase-shifter miscalibrations as a representative example of optical-manipulation errors. The methods developed in this work enable physics-informed parameter tuning to optimize gate designs and develop tailored quantum error correction protocols toward fault-tolerant quantum computing using hybrid light--matter quantum systems.


---


## 光谱融合识别对称量子旋转链中早期状态排斥

**Original Title:** Spectral Fusion for Identifying Early State Exclusion in Symmetric Quantum Spin Chains

**Authors:** Mia Escobar, Valentin Garcia, Anastasiia Minenkova

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04353v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04353v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

一维量子旋转链中的完美状态转移（BST）提供了一种自然环境，可以使用光谱方法分析量子信息输运。在单激励子空间中，具有最近邻相互作用的链的动力学由雅可比矩阵决定，从而允许状态转移问题根据特征值分布和特征值的对称性来公式化。在这项工作中，我们研究了\{早期状态排除}（SSE）现象，即时间演变的状态与初始状态的重叠在严格早于完美状态转移第一次发生的时间消失。在具有和不具有SSE的情况下表现出CST的汉密尔顿学派的早期构造的基础上，我们为任意奇长链提供了显式的Jacobi矩阵实现，并建立了SSE发生或不发生的一般条件。我们提出\{谱融合}（SF）的过程来构建此类汉密尔顿的无限家族。这些结果拓宽了已知类型的显示早期状态排斥的旋转链，并进一步澄清了汉密尔顿谱结构的作用。


### Abstract

Perfect state transfer (PST) in one-dimensional quantum spin chains provides a natural setting in which quantum information transport can be analyzed using spectral methods. In the single-excitation subspace, the dynamics of a chain with nearest-neighbor interactions are governed by a Jacobi matrix, allowing questions of state transfer to be formulated in terms of eigenvalue distributions and symmetry properties of eigenvectors. In this work, we investigate the phenomenon of \emph{early state exclusion} (ESE), whereby the overlap of the time-evolved state with the initial state vanishes at a time strictly earlier than the first occurrence of perfect state transfer. Building on earlier constructions of Hamiltonians exhibiting PST with and without ESE, we provide explicit Jacobi matrix realizations for arbitrary odd-length chains and establish general conditions under which ESE occurs or does not occur. We propose the process of \emph{spectral fusion} (SF) to build infinite families of such Hamiltonians. These results broaden the known class of spin chains displaying early state exclusion and further clarify the role of spectral structure of the Hamiltonians.


---


## 质子散粒噪音限制里德伯格-EIT静电法

**Original Title:** Photon shot-noise-limited Rydberg-EIT electrometry

**Authors:** Gyeongmin Ju, Ye Jin Yu, Heewoo Kim, Hansol Jeong, Jinhyuk Bae, Changhoon Baek, Han Seb Moon

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04354v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04354v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

里德伯原子静电法是开发高灵敏量子电场传感器的核心技术。其基于原子-量子相互作用的灵敏度通常受到量子散粒噪音（PSN）和光谱增宽的限制。在这里，我们通过实验证明了来自85 Ra原子蒸气电池的近PSN限制的里德堡电测法。通过控制剩余磁场和激光频率噪音来设计原子的一致性，我们实现了1.6 MHz窄谱线宽度的里德伯格电磁感应透明度（EIT），为高灵敏度里德伯格-EIT静电法产生了增强的光谱斜坡。在优化的超外差探测条件下，我们在37 GHz获得了12.5（8）nV cm^-1 Hz^-1/2的电场灵敏度，与计算的PSN极限非常接近。这些结果为高灵敏度的量子电学提供了直接的实验证据，并为量子噪声限制的里德伯电学建立了一条实用的途径。


### Abstract

Rydberg-atom electrometry is a core technique in the development of highly sensitive quantum electric-field sensors. Its sensitivity based on atom-photon interaction is typically limited by photon shot-noise (PSN) and spectral broadenings. Here, we experimentally demonstrate a near PSN-limited Rydberg electrometry from a 85Rb atomic vapor cell. By engineering atomic coherence through control of residual magnetic fields and laser frequency noise, we achieve the Rydberg electromagnetically induced transparency (EIT) with the narrow linewidth of 1.6 MHz, yielding an enhanced spectral slope for high-sensitivity Rydberg-EIT electrometry. Under optimized superheterodyne detection conditions, we obtain an electric-field sensitivity of 12.5(8) nV cm^-1 Hz^-1/2 at 37 GHz, in close agreement with the calculated PSN limit. These results provide direct experimental evidence of the high-sensitive quantum electrometry and establish a practical route toward quantum-noise-limited Rydberg electrometry.

## 通过关键特征提取和矩阵结构保留的鲁棒可操纵性分类

**Original Title:** Robust Steerability Classification via Key Feature Extraction and Matrix Structure Preservation

**Authors:** Yutao Xin, Huixian Meng, Zhongyan Li, Pu Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04363v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04363v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

概括能力对于评估量子可操纵性分类器的稳健性至关重要。在这项工作中，我们从关键特征提取和矩阵结构保存的角度研究了鲁棒可操纵性分类。Phys. Rev. A 100，022314（2019）中引入的数据集为当前工作提供了培训基础。通过严格不可操纵的随机状态、T对角状态和全有对抗无（AVN）状态，我们评估了基于全信息特征训练的支持向量机（SVMs）、多层感知器（MLPs）和深度感知器控制分类器（DP）的概括性能。这些分类器中没有一个在T对角或AVN状态上一致地执行。考虑到随机局部操作和经典通信和局部酉变换保持可操纵性，我们引入了一个决定可操纵性的关键特征。在此特征上训练的SVM克服了T对角状态的不稳定性，但在AVN状态上仍然失败。此外，这个功能本身是不足以训练强大的基于神经网络的可操纵性分类器。认识到将量子状态压平为一维载体可能会破坏其固有的矩阵结构，我们引入了这两个特征的矩阵版本，并在它们上训练卷积神经网络。只有当保留矩阵结构并同时提取关键特征时，测试分类器中最稳健的总体性能才能实现。最后，作为一个应用程序，我们采用最鲁棒的分类器来预测检测轴对称状态的可操纵性所需的投影测量数量


### Abstract

Generalization ability is essential for assessing the robustness of quantum steerability classifiers. In this work, we investigate robust steerability classification from the perspective of key feature extraction and matrix structure preservation. The dataset introduced in Phys. Rev. A 100, 022314 (2019) provides the training basis for the present work. With strictly unsteerable random states, T-diagonal states, and All-Versus-Nothing (AVN) states, we evaluate the generalization performance of support vector machines (SVMs), multilayer perceptrons (MLPs), and deep perceptron control classifiers(DPs) trained on full-information features. None of these classifiers perform consistently on T-diagonal or AVN states. Given that stochastic local operations and classical communication and local unitary transformations preserve steerability, we introduce a key feature that determines steerability. SVMs trained on this feature overcome the instability on T-diagonal states but still fail on AVN states. Moreover, this feature alone is insufficient for training robust neural-network-based steerability classifiers. Recognizing that flattening quantum states into one-dimensional vectors may destroy their intrinsic matrix structure, we introduce matrix versions of both features and train convolutional neural networks on them. The most robust overall performance among the tested classifiers is achieved only when the matrix structure is preserved and key features are extracted simultaneously. Finally, as an application, we employ the most robust classifiers to predict the number of projective measurements required to detect the steerability of axially symmetric states


---


## 通过非异常缺陷操作优化非Hermitian感知中的灵敏度-噪音权衡

**Original Title:** Optimizing the Sensitivity-Noise Trade-off in Non-Hermitian Sensing via Off-Exceptional-Deficiency Operation

**Authors:** Shangxuan Li, Bin Guo

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04386v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04386v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

非埃尔米特传感的一个核心挑战是光谱奇异性同时放大信号和环境噪音。我们在具有单向层间耦合的双链Hatano-Nelson模型中解决了这一困境。在异常缺陷（ED）限制下，该系统表现出宏观简并的复光谱和明显的非厄米特集肤效应（NHSE），产生的灵敏度随网格尺寸$N$呈指数级扩展，同时在六个数量级的失调范围内保持稳健。通过引入对角空间无序，我们证明了NHSE通过特征空间Cosine相似性分析量化定义良好的故障容忍阈值而被逐步抑制。为了协调灵敏度与噪音的权衡，我们描述了“在ED”和“非ED”操作制度。虽然At-ED配置施加了在次优平台处饱和的分数阶噪音放大（SNR $\propto δ ' s），但迁移到Off-ED状态消除了这种几何奇异性并恢复了线性缩放定律（SNR $\propto δ '' s），实现了几个数量级的SNR增强。至关重要的是，这一改进是在完全保留指数灵敏度缩放的同时实现的，尽管与严格的At-ED限制相比，绝对灵敏度略有降低。我们的研究结果将Off-ED框架确立为下一代拓扑传感器的具体范式，该传感器将极端的灵敏度与强大的抗噪性相协调。


### Abstract

A central challenge in non-Hermitian sensing is that spectral singularities simultaneously amplify both the signal and environmental noise. We address this predicament in a double-chain Hatano-Nelson model featuring unidirectional interlayer coupling. At the exceptional deficiency (ED) limit, the system exhibits a macroscopically degenerate complex spectrum and a pronounced non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE), yielding a sensitivity that scales exponentially with lattice size $N$ while remaining robust across a six-order-of-magnitude detuning range. By introducing diagonal spatial disorder, we demonstrate that the NHSE is progressively suppressed, whith eigenspace cosine similarity analysis quantifying a well-defined fault-tolerance threshold. To reconcile the sensitivity-noise trade-off, we delineate "At-ED" and "Off-ED" operating regimes. While the At-ED configuration imposes fractional-order noise amplification (SNR $\propto δ^{-1/2}$) that saturates at a suboptimal plateau, migrating to the Off-ED regime eliminates this geometric singularity and restores a linear scaling law (SNR $\propto δ^{-1}$), achieving an SNR enhancement of several orders of magnitude. Crucially, this improvement is achieved while fully preserving the exponential sensitivity scaling, albeit at a slightly reduced absolute sensitivity compared to the strict At-ED limit. Our findings establish the Off-ED framework as a concrete paradigm for next-generation topological sensors that reconcile extreme sensitivity with robust noise immunity.


---


## 恒定磁场中具有旋转和风味的中微子振荡的Leggett-Garg测试不等式

**Original Title:** Leggett-Garg test inequality with spin and flavour neutrino oscillations in a constant magnetic field

**Authors:** I. A. Monroy, S. D. Madrid

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04412v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04412v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

莱格特-加格不等式（LGI）是Belletten不等式的模拟，涉及系统上不同时间观察对象测量值的相关性，是量子力学针对经典预测的标志性测试之一。在这项工作中，我们研究了在恒定横向磁场存在下的中微子味道（$VID_{e}' s &#39对于具有强磁场的系统，我们表明，对于这两种情况，都存在长度区域$A L$，其中LGI被违反，由相关器函数$K_{3}$和$K_{4}$量化。


### Abstract

The Leggett-Garg inequality (LGI), an analogue of Bellś inequality involving correlations of measurements of one observable on a system at different times, stands as one of the hallmark tests of quantum mechanics against classical predictions. In this work, we investigate its implications in the context of neutrino flavour ($ν_{e}^{L}\leftrightarrowν_μ^{L}$) and spin ($ν_{e}^{L}\leftrightarrowν_{e}^{R}$) oscillations in the presence of a constant transverse magnetic field. For systems with strong magnetic fields, we show that, for both cases, there are length regions $ΔL$ where the LGI is violated, as quantified by the correlator functions $K_{3}$ and $K_{4}$.

## 横向光学模的原子干涉术

**Original Title:** Atom Interferometry with Transverse Optical Modes

**Authors:** Ryan Husband, Ryan J. Thomas, Yosri Ben-Aïcha, Rhys H. Eagle, Jessica Eastman, John E. Debs, Patrick J. Everitt, Michael Larsen, Eric Imhof, Charles A. Sackett, John D. Close, Simon A. Haine, Samuel Legge

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04430v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04430v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们使用光学模的横向相分布实验证明原子干涉术。作为原理证明，我们使用超几何高斯束的螺旋相绕线进行拉姆齐干涉测量，具有弹道膨胀冷RB 87原子的集合，并且我们表明干涉仪可以测量由电机引起的旋转，其灵敏度与轨道角动量和干涉仪时间成线性比例。我们描述了干涉仪的热退散性，推导并通过实验证实了螺旋相绕奇异性附近出现的空间变化干涉仪可见性的封闭形式表达，从而激励了在环形陷阱中使用凝聚原子。


### Abstract

We experimentally demonstrate atom interferometry using the transverse phase profile of an optical mode. As proof-of-principle, we use the helical phase windings of Hypergeometric Gaussian beams for Ramsey interferometry with ensembles of ballistically-expanding cold Rb87 atoms, and we show that the interferometer can measure rotations induced by a motor with a sensitivity that scales linearly with orbital angular momentum and interferometer time. We characterize the thermal decoherence of the interferometer, deriving and experimentally confirming a closed-form expression for the spatially-varying interferometer visibility arising near the singularity of the helical phase winding, motivating the use of condensed atoms in ring-shaped traps.

## 随机张量网络中的多熵

**Original Title:** Multi-entropy in random tensor networks

**Authors:** Miao Hu, Simon Lin, Ion Nechita

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04470v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04470v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

研究了在大键维极限下随机张量网络（RTN）态中Rényi多熵S^{（q）} n$的计算.对于Rényi指数$n=2$和任意数目的当事人$q$的情况下，我们证明了，多熵是通过网络的最小多路切割。当最小多路割是退化的时，我们用相容的最小割族刻画了最小集的全极小集，并给出了所有极小集都来自普通割划分的一个判据。对于$n=2$，这给出了一个自然的推广的最小切割描述的二体纠缠的多体系统与任意多的缔约方。对于整元$n>2$的情况，我们通过为单个随机张量和由等距瓦片构建的网络提供明确的反例，表明最小多路切割猜想一般是\ð {not true}。我们讨论了RTN和全息术中多方纠缠结构结果的含义。


### Abstract

We study the evaluation of Rényi multi-entropies $S^{(q)}_n$ in Random Tensor Network (RTN) states in the large bond-dimension limit. For the case of Rényi index $n=2$ and arbitrary number of parties $q$, we prove that that multi-entropies are determined by minimal multiway cuts through the network. When the minimal multiway cut is degenerate, we characterize the full minimizer set via compatible families of minimal cuts and give a criterion for all minimizers to come from ordinary cut partitions. For $n=2$, this gives a natural generalization of the minimal cut description of bipartite entanglement to multipartite systems with arbitrarily many parties. For the case of integer $n>2$, we show that the minimal multiway cut conjecture is in general \emph{not true} by providing explicit counter examples for both the single random tensor and for the network built from isometric tilings. We discuss the implication for our results on the multipartite entanglement structures in RTN and holography.


---


## 作为噪声偏置量子比特的各向异性Rabi模型

**Original Title:** Anisotropic Rabi Model as a Noise Biased Qubit

**Authors:** Jia-Wen Yu, Ke-Xiong Yan, Yuan Qiu, Yiming Yu, Yexiong Zeng, Adam Miranowicz, Zhi-Cheng Shi, Ye-Hong Chen, Yan Xia, Franco Nori

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04487v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04487v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们提出量子各向异性Rabi模型作为噪音偏置量子位的潜在资源。可以通过调整回旋波和反旋转波相互作用的相对强度来偏置系统-环境耦合，其特征是各向异性参数$n $。这种各向异性选择性地抑制了主导的去相干路径，从而能够在超强和深强耦合机制中构建受保护的逻辑量子位。与各向异性Rabi模型的基本和第一激发态相比，逻辑状态（由各向异性Rabi模型的基本和第一激发态形成）具有增强的相干时间。此外，我们在逻辑状态子空间内构建了一组通用门操作，并证明与$n $的不同值相关的门操作对外部噪音具有鲁棒性。这些发现预计将启发各向异性Rabi模型的应用和研究方向，并产生良好的潜在影响。


### Abstract

We present the quantum anisotropic Rabi model as a potential resource for a noise biased qubit. The system-environment coupling can be biased by tuning the relative strengths of the rotating-wave and counter-rotating-wave interactions, characterized by the anisotropy parameter $η$. This anisotropy selectively suppresses dominant decoherence pathways, thereby enabling the construction of a protected logical qubit in the ultrastrong and deep-strong coupling regimes. The logical states (formed by the ground and first excited states of the anisotropic Rabi model) possess coherence times that are enhanced compared to the isotropic case. Moreover, we construct a set of universal gate operations within the logical-state subspace and demonstrate that the gate operations associated with different values of $η$ exhibit robustness against external noise. These findings are expected to inspire applications and research directions for the anisotropic Rabi model with promising potential impacts.

## 六方BN核旋转的任意操纵

**Original Title:** Arbitrary manipulation of nuclear spins in hexagonal boron nitride

**Authors:** Fattah Sakuldee, Mehdi Abdi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04497v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04497v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

由于其定域性质和可控性，六方BN（hBN）中带负电荷的B空位中心（V$_\text{B}）是一个有前途的旋转平台，用于访问其邻近核，具有执行量子计算任务的潜力。然而，利用和操纵核旋转的方法仍然缺乏。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种在核旋转上准备单量子位和多量子位门的协议，利用电子旋转作为辅助量子位。通过应用背景磁场和多音连续驱动，我们表明可以有效地设计与原子核耦合的电子旋转。这允许通过哈恩回声脉冲序列抑制不希望的电子-核相互作用。然后通过使用适当的RF驱动器来实现目标门。我们对现实参数的数值结果显示，单量子位门的门灵敏度高达99美元，多量子位门的门灵敏度高达95美元。由于门执行持续时间小于300美元$ ns，我们的协议避免了电子旋转退散效应。因此，我们的方案为V$_\text{B}^-$在hBN中用于量子计算目的的实际应用奠定了基础。


### Abstract

Due to its localized nature and controllability, the negatively charged boron vacancy centers (V$_\text{B}^-$) in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) are a promising spin platform for accessing its neighboring nuclei with potential for performing quantum computational tasks. However, the methods of utilizing and manipulating the nuclear spins are still lacking. In this work, we propose a protocol for the preparation of single- and multi-qubit gates on the nuclear spins, utilizing the electron spin as an auxiliary qubit. By applying a background magnetic field and a multi-tone continuous drive, we show that the electron spin coupling to the nuclei can be efficiently engineered. This allows for suppressing the undesired electron-nuclear interactions through the Hahn echo pulse sequence. The target gates are then implemented by employing proper RF drives. Our numerical results for realistic parameters show gate fidelities as high as $99\%$ for single-qubit and $95\%$ for multi-qubit gates. With the gate execution durations being less than $300$ ns, our protocol evades electron spin decoherence effects. Therefore, our scheme sets the stage for the practical application of V$_\text{B}^-$ in hBN for quantum computation purposes.

## 用射频反射仪探测铅Te-铅纳米线器件

**Original Title:** Probing PbTe-Pb nanowire devices with radio-frequency reflectometry

**Authors:** Xin-Yi Tang, Lin Li, Zezhou Xia, Jierong Huo, Wenyu Song, Lining Yang, Zonglin Li, Jiaye Xu, Peilin Li, Runan Shang, Qi-Kun Xue, Ke He, Hao Zhang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04544v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04544v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们报告的射频（rf）反射测量的选择性区域生长的PbTe-Pb纳米线器件上的CdTe衬底上的实施。这些纳米线被预测主机马约拉纳零模式。我们证明了射频技术的兼容性，电阻和电容传感，与这些纳米线。文中还讨论了CdTe衬底的介电损耗对器件性能的影响。在发生零能量模式的有限磁场下也验证了射频反射计的可行性。我们的结果能够快速控制PtTE量子器件，为其在拓扑量子计算中的应用铺平了道路。


### Abstract

We report the implementation of radio-frequency (rf) reflectometry on selective-area-grown PbTe-Pb nanowire devices on a CdTe substrate. These nanowires were predicted to host Majorana zero modes. We demonstrate the compatibility of the rf technique, both resistive and capacitive sensing, with these nanowires. The effect of dielectric loss from the CdTe substrate is also discussed. The feasibility of rf reflectometry is also verified at finite magnetic fields where zero-energy modes occur. Our results enable the fast control of PbTe quantum devices, paving the way for its application in topological quantum computation.

## 纠缠选择性输运的分布变分量子优化

**Original Title:** Distributed Variational Quantum Optimisation by Entanglement-Selective Transport

**Authors:** Edric Matwiejew, Pascal Elahi, Ugo Varetto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04548v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04548v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

分布式量子优化具有挑战性，因为跨多个量子处理器计算问题成本函数需要非本地门，这可能会带来延迟和保真度方面的额外费用。在这里，我们介绍QESTO，这是一种用于基于图的离散优化的分布式变分类比器，仅需要持久的预共享Bell对来进行远程操作。使用局部操作，它将局部约束信息编码在贝尔对中，利用该信息产生向全局有效分布式解状态的幅度转移。QESTO需要问题图的每个分布式边有一个Bell对，并且在Bell状态初始化后，不使用非本地门。在两个有界加权Wang瓦片匹配问题集合上，QESTO比在两个或更高的模拟深度没有分布式门的等效分区QAOA实现了更强的向低成本瓦片的收敛，并且超过了单片QAOA在两个集合中研究最深深度的平均性能。这些结果表明，持续纠缠可以支持有用的变分通信，同时减少每层的非本地门开销。


### Abstract

Distributed quantum optimisation is challenging because computing the problem cost function across multiple quantum processors requires non-local gates, which can incur overhead in latency and fidelity. Here we introduce QESTO, a distributed variational ansatz for graph-based discrete optimisation that requires only persistent pre-shared Bell pairs for remote operations. Using local operations, it encodes local constraint information in the Bell pairs that is leveraged to produce amplitude transfer towards globally valid distributed solution states. QESTO requires one Bell pair per distributed edge of the problem graph and, after initialisation of the Bell states, uses no non-local gates. On two bounded weighted Wang tile-matching problem ensembles, QESTO achieves stronger convergence to low-cost tilings than equivalently partitioned QAOA with no distributed gates at ansatz depths of two or higher, and exceeds the mean performance of monolithic QAOA at the deepest studied depth in both ensembles. These results suggest that persistent entanglement can support useful variational communication while reducing per-layer non-local gate overhead.


---


## 量子采样数据中最小海明距离的缩放极其缓慢

**Original Title:** Extremely slow scaling of minimal Hamming distance in quantum sampling data

**Authors:** P. S. Golubev, I. A. Iakovlev, V. V. Mazurenko

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04558v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04558v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

量子数据可以从多种来源获得，包括来自有噪音的量子处理器、冷原子模拟器以及经典逼近（例如变分神经网络状态）的直接测量。然而，我们描述这些系统的能力从根本上受到限制，因为与系统的指数级大的希尔伯特空间相比，可用的测量数据通常是稀疏的。为了解决这个问题，我们建议使用为一组唯一位串计算的平均最小海明距离作为揭示普遍乘势定律行为的稳健指标。通过真实实验和模拟的各种例子，我们表明，乘势定律参数可以可靠地捕捉量子状态的复杂性，并从有限的量子信息中识别量子相转变，而无需积累大量的统计数据或显式地计算物理可观测量。这使得可以在单一框架内分析完全不同的量子实验。


### Abstract

Quantum data can be obtained from a diverse range of sources, including direct measurements from noisy quantum processors, cold-atom simulators, and classical approximations such as variational neural-network states. However, our ability to characterize these systems is fundamentally limited, as the available measurement data is often sparse compared to the exponentially large Hilbert space of the system. To address this, we propose using the average minimal Hamming distance calculated for a set of unique bitstrings as a robust metric revealing a universal power-law behaviour. Through various examples of real experiments and simulations, we show that the power-law parameters reliably capture the complexity of quantum states and identify quantum phase transitions from limited quantum information, without the need for accumulating extensive statistics or explicitly calculating physical observables. This enables the analysis of completely different quantum experiments within a single framework.


---


## 通过平板电路中的穿梭进行电路级噪音估计

**Original Title:** Circuit-Level Noise Estimation via Shuttling in Plaquette Circuits

**Authors:** Huyen Do, Alexandru Paler

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04629v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04629v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们提出了一种用于估计QEC电路级噪音水平的方法，假设只有单次测量可用（例如测量速度慢并且以分区/并行方式执行），并且较低级别的量子硬件校准是不可能的（例如云访问）或不可行的（例如大规模计算）。我们使用两种综合症量子位配置开发并运行表面代码空斑实验：FRESH，涉及每次空斑重复的新鲜量子位，而RECCYCY，重复使用量子位。为了验证我们的方法，我们将模板编译到离子陷阱（IonQ Aria 1）原生门集，并应用硬件感知重写模板以减少电路深度和执行时间。我们还在非穿梭的超导处理器（IBM Torino）上运行了实验。我们根据所得的单次斑块测量统计数据估计电路级噪音率，并从数字上得出低深度QEC实验的可行性结论。


### Abstract

We present a method for estimating QEC circuit-level noise levels assuming that only single-shot measurements are available (e.g. measurements are slow and performed in a zoned/parallel fashion), and that lower level quantum hardware calibration is not possible (e.g. cloud access) or not feasible (e.g. large scale computing). We develop and run surface code plaquette experiments using two syndrome qubit configurations: FRESH, involving fresh qubits for each plaquette repetition, and RECYCLE, reusing qubits. To validate our approach, we compile plaquettes to ion-trap (IonQ Aria1) native gate set and apply hardware-aware rewrite templates to reduce circuit depth and execution time. We also run the experiments on a non-shuttling, superconducting processor (IBM Torino). We estimate circuit-level noise rates from the resulting single-shot plaquette measurement statistics, and conclude numerically about the viability of low-depth QEC experiments.

## 量子传感中的非可逆分散耦合

**Original Title:** Nonreciprocal Dispersive Coupling for Quantum Sensing

**Authors:** Dong Xie, Chunling Xu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04666v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04666v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

分散耦合被广泛用于量子信息读出。大多数先前的研究都集中在互频耦合上。在这里，我们进一步构建非互惠频散耦合并将其应用于量子传感。对于腔体量子数测量，非可逆扩散耦合比其可逆扩散耦合提供更高的精确度，并且随着量子数的增加，这一优势变得更加明显。然而，当直接测量单量子驱动强度时，非倒数扩散耦合并没有表现出比倒数扩散耦合更好的优势。通过我们提出的策略将驱动强度信息转化为腔量子数，非可逆扩散耦合在精度上再次优于可逆扩散耦合，并且在驱动强度更大时优势变得越来越明显。这项工作提出了一种新型方法来增强量子传感并实现超精确量子传感器的制造。


### Abstract

Dispersive coupling is widely utilized for quantum information readout. Most prior studies have concentrated on reciprocal dispersive coupling. Here, we further construct nonreciprocal dispersive coupling and apply it to quantum sensing. For cavity photon number measurement, nonreciprocal dispersive coupling delivers higher precision than its reciprocal counterpart, and this advantage grows more pronounced with an increase in photon number. When directly measuring the single-photon driving strength, however, nonreciprocal dispersive coupling shows no superiority over reciprocal dispersive coupling. By converting the information of driving strength into cavity photon numbers via our proposed strategy, nonreciprocal dispersive coupling again outperforms reciprocal dispersive coupling in precision, with the advantage becoming increasingly significant at larger driving strength. This work presents a novel method to boost quantum sensing and enable the fabrication of ultra-precise quantum sensors.

## 硬核电子-离子路径积分蒙特卡罗

**Original Title:** Electron-Ion Path Integral Monte Carlo with Hard Core

**Authors:** Riccardo Fantoni

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04667v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04667v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们从第一原理出发对金属氢进行了数字（限制）路径积分蒙特卡洛实验。我们研究量子二成分等离子体，其中一种成分由负单位电荷的点状粒子组成，另一种成分由正单位电荷的带电硬球体组成。我们研究添加剂混合物和非添加剂混合物，其中我们只在不同物种之间保留硬核。我们专门研究电子-质子等离子体的情况，两种物质的摩尔分数之间的比例为1：1。我们测量了等离子体的热力学和结构性质。从结构分析中，我们看到随着温度降低，从金属氢相转变为分子氢相。正如预期的那样，在高密度下相关性会减弱。


### Abstract

We performed numerical (restricted) path integral Monte Carlo experiments on metallic Hydrogen from first principles. We study a quantum two component plasma where one component is made of pointwise particles of negative unitary charge and the other is made of charged hard spheres of positive unitary charge. We study both the additive mixture and a nonadditive mixture where we only keep a hard core between unlike species. We specialize to the case of the electron-proton plasma with a 1:1 ratios between the molar fraction of the two species. We measured thermodynamic and structural properties of the plasma. From an analysis of the structure we see a transition from a metallic Hydrogen phase, to a molecular Hydrogen phase as the temperature is lowered. As expected at high density the correlations are diminished.

## 用于解决非线性偏出问题的混合量子-经典物理学神经网络：杂交何时何地有效？

**Original Title:** Hybrid quantum-classical physics-informed neural networks for solving nonlinear PDEs: when and where hybridization is effective?

**Authors:** Kaveh Zabihi, Hamid Montazeri, Akke S. J. Suiker

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04679v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04679v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

基于物理的神经网络（PINN）经常在具有尖锐梯度、严格动态、高频内容或多尺度结构的非线性偏微方程（PED）上遇到困难。这些局限性源于谱偏差、病态优化和不稳定收敛，限制了最需要高级求解器的区域中的PINN准确性。在这项工作中，我们开发了一种混合量子-经典物理学信息神经网络（HQPINN），该网络将经典神经网络主干与参数化量子电路（PQC）集成在一起，以丰富解决方案表示。该框架以经典PINN为基准，基于三个代表性的非线性偏出方程：Burgers方程、Allen-Cahn方程和Korteweg-de Vries（Kdis）方程。通过对量子位计数、电路深度、PQC放置、搭配密度和经典网络宽度的系统敏感性分析进一步检查该框架。在所有基准测试中，HQPINN表现出更平稳的训练动态、减少的损失振荡和提高的最终准确性，其中最大的收益发生在僵硬和多尺度机制中。Burgers方程的相对L2误差降低了大约四倍，Allen-Cahn方程的相对L2误差降低了大约五倍，而Kdis方程的改进则较为温和。总体而言，结果表明，精心联合设计的混合量子-经典架构可以减轻经典PINN的关键局限性，并为近期量子增强型PDL求解器提供实用设计指导。


### Abstract

Physics-informed neural networks (PINNs) often struggle on nonlinear partial differential equations (PDEs) with sharp gradients, stiff dynamics, high-frequency content, or multiscale structure. Such limitations, rooted in spectral bias, ill-conditioned optimization, and unstable convergence, restrict PINN accuracy in regimes where advanced solvers are most needed. In this work, we develop a hybrid quantum-classical physics-informed neural network (HQPINN) that integrates a classical neural-network backbone with a parameterized quantum circuit (PQC) to enrich the solution representation. The framework is benchmarked against a classical PINN on three representative nonlinear PDEs: Burgers' equation, the Allen-Cahn equation, and the Korteweg-de Vries (KdV) equation. The framework is further examined through a systematic sensitivity analysis of qubit count, circuit depth, PQC placement, collocation density, and classical-network width. Across all benchmarks, HQPINNs exhibit smoother training dynamics, reduced loss oscillations, and improved final accuracy, with the largest gains occurring in stiff and multiscale regimes. Relative L2 error decreases by about fourfold for Burgers' equation and fivefold for the Allen-Cahn equation, while improvements for the KdV equation are more moderate. Overall, the results demonstrate that carefully co-designed hybrid quantum-classical architectures can mitigate key limitations of classical PINNs and provide practical design guidance for near-term quantum-enhanced PDE solvers.


---


## 通过超芝诺效应和反相干保护量子态

**Original Title:** Protecting Quantum States via the Super-Zeno Effect and Anticoherence

**Authors:** C. Chryssomalakos, A. G. Flores-Delgado, E. Guzmán-González, L. Hanotel

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04681v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04681v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们考虑了通过相互作用Hamilton $H$耦合到噪音环境的旋转系统，Hamilton $H$是旋转操作符$S_i$（$n$-磁性Hamilton）中$n$的次数的多元性，并表明将量子超芝诺效应与旋转反相干子空间结合使用在保护旋转免受噪音方面非常有效。当$n=1$时，就像杂散磁场引起的不想要的旋转一样，我们的方案提供了量子陀螺仪，这个概念自然地推广到更高的$n$值（量子$n$-陀螺仪）。拟议协议的要点是利用量子超芝诺效应将状态限制在子空间中，然后利用反相关性将其进化冻结在子空间中。


### Abstract

We consider a spin system coupled to a noisy environment via an interaction Hamiltonian $H$ which is a polynomial of degree $n$ in the spin operators $S_i$ ($n$-magnetic Hamiltonian), and show that the use of the quantum super-Zeno effect in conjunction with a spin-anticoherent subspace, is highly effective in protecting the spin from the noise. When $n=1$, as in the case of unwanted rotations induced by stray magnetic fields, our scheme provides a quantum gyroscope, a concept that generalizes naturally to higher $n$ values (a quantum $n$-gyroscope). The gist of the proposed protocol is to use the quantum super-Zeno effect to confine a state to the subspace, and then exploit anticoherence to freeze its evolution within it.


---


## ATM时间序列预测的数字量子水库计算

**Original Title:** Digital Quantum Reservoir Computing for ATM Time Series Prediction

**Authors:** Chiara Vercellino, Giacomo Vitali, Valeria Zaffaroni, Francesca Cibrario, Emanuele Dri, Paolo Viviani, Olivier Terzo, Davide Corbelletto

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04686v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04686v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们研究了一种数字量子水库计算（QRC）框架，用于对近期量子设备上的自动提款机（ATM）现金需求时间序列进行多步预测。所提出的方法使用具有固定结构的参数化四量子位库，利用部分测量和重置，其中时间数据以旋转角编码。训练仅限于经典的岭回归读出。我们系统地分析了电路ansatzë、水库存储器、测量衍生的可观测量和执行后台对预测性能的影响。实验进行了无噪声模拟，噪声感知仿真，和一个真正的IQM Spark量子处理器。虽然QRC模型在平均绝对误差和归一化均方误差指标方面没有优于经典的Prophet基准，但它们在动态时间弯曲指标方面取得了更具竞争力的结果，表明了捕获时间结构的部分能力。这些发现为现实的财务预测提供了对数字QRC的实证评估，并强调了其当前的局限性及其在近期量子硬件上的潜力。


### Abstract

We investigate a digital quantum reservoir computing (QRC) framework for multi-step forecasting of automated teller machine (ATM) cash demand time series on near-term quantum devices. The proposed approach uses parametrized four-qubit reservoirs with a fixed structure exploiting partial measurement and reset, where temporal data is encoded in rotation angles. Training is restricted to a classical Ridge-regression readout. We systematically analyze the impact of the circuit ansatzë, reservoir memory, measurement-derived observables, and the execution backend on the forecasting performance. Experiments are performed with noiseless simulation, noise-aware emulation, and a real IQM Spark quantum processor. Although the QRC models do not outperform the classical Prophet benchmark in terms of Mean Absolute Error and Normalized Mean Squared Error metrics, they achieve more competitive results in Dynamic Time Warping metric, indicating a partial ability to capture temporal structure. These findings provide an empirical assessment of digital QRC for realistic financial forecasting and highlight both its current limitations and its potential on near-term quantum hardware.

## QPredSGG：用于长尾场景图生成的混合量子预测学习

**Original Title:** QPredSGG: Hybrid Quantum Predicate Learning for Long-Tailed Scene Graph Generation

**Authors:** Prerana Ramkumar, Nouhaila Innan, Muhammad Shafique

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04689v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04689v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

场景图生成（SGG）需要对对象及其交互进行关系推理，但性能往往受到严重的长尾谓词不平衡的限制。经典的SGG模型经常依赖于数据集统计数据，导致对频繁关系而不是细粒度语义谓词的有偏见的预测。尽管现有的去偏策略提高了平均召回率，但当前框架中的谓词分类仍然经常依赖于具有高参数成本的大型经典决策模块。本文介绍了一种用于SGG的混合量子谓词分类器，它用加权交叉熵训练的量子谓词头（QP-头）代替因果特征增强网络（CFEN）中的经典谓词头。据我们所知，这是首批评估Visual Genome 150上场景图判定分类混合量子架构的研究之一。我们研究量子位计数、编码策略、纠缠结构和电路深度对关系预测的影响。最好的4量子位QP-Head使用幅度嵌入和强纠缠层将4096维对特征压缩为16维量子兼容的表示，对应于256 $\times $缩减。它的mR@100为57.25%，而经典CFEN参考的mR@100为41.1%，同时仅使用96个可训练量子参数。扩展到8个量子位保持了强大的长尾性能，在384个量子参数下达到了55.38%的mR@100，而深度分析显示了可表达性和运行时负载之间的权衡。这些结果表明，紧凑的混合量子断言头可以支持复杂视觉推理任务中的参数高效长尾关系分类。


### Abstract

Scene Graph Generation (SGG) requires relational reasoning over objects and their interactions, but performance is often limited by severe long-tail predicate imbalance. Classical SGG models frequently rely on dataset statistics, leading to biased predictions toward frequent relations rather than fine-grained semantic predicates. Although existing debiasing strategies improve mean recall, predicate classification in current frameworks still often depends on large classical decision modules with high parameter cost. This work introduces a hybrid quantum predicate classifier for SGG by replacing the classical predicate head in Causal Feature Enhancement Network (CFEN) with a Quantum Predicate Head (QP-Head) trained using weighted cross-entropy. To the best of our knowledge, this is among the first studies to evaluate a hybrid quantum architecture for scene graph predicate classification on Visual Genome 150. We study the effect of qubit count, encoding strategy, entangling structure, and circuit depth on relational prediction. The best 4-qubit QP-Head uses Amplitude Embedding and Strongly Entangling Layers to compress 4096-dimensional pair features into a 16-dimensional quantum-compatible representation, corresponding to a 256$\times$ reduction. It achieves an mR@100 of 57.25%, compared with 41.1% for the classical CFEN reference, while using only 96 trainable quantum parameters. Scaling to 8 qubits maintains strong long-tail performance, reaching an mR@100 of 55.38% with 384 quantum parameters, while the depth analysis shows a trade-off between expressibility and runtime overhead. These results suggest that compact hybrid quantum predicate heads can support parameter-efficient long-tail relational classification in complex visual reasoning tasks.


---


## 三量子位系统中纠缠的量化

**Original Title:** Quantification of Entanglement in Three-Qubit Systems

**Authors:** Zikra Aram

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04721v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04721v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

这项研究通过Acín规范表示对三量子位纯态中的纠缠量化进行了分析研究，该表示是两量子位施密特分解的推广。在多方纠缠的复杂性和当前测量方法的缺点的驱动下，我们采用了从系统内各种二分区的广义并发性派生的全局并发性度量。在一系列SLOCC纠缠类（例如积、可分、GZZ型和W型状态）中从分析和数值上探索了该测量的特征。当与三重纠缠和三重消极性相比时，我们的研究结果表明，这种措施可以对多方相关性产生补充见解。结果强调了这一措施在阐明三量子位量子系统内纠缠的结构和分布方面的重要性。


### Abstract

This study presents an analytical investigation of entanglement quantification in three-qubit pure states through the Acín canonical representation, which serves as a generalization of the two-qubit Schmidt decomposition. Driven by the intricacies of multipartite entanglement and the shortcomings of current measures, we employ a global concurrence measure derived from the generalized concurrence of various bipartitions within the system. The characteristics of this measure are explored both analytically and numerically across a range of SLOCC entanglement classes, such as product, biseparable, GHZ-type, and W-type states. When compared to the three-tangle and tripartite negativity, our findings indicate that this measure yields complementary insights into multipartite correlations. The outcomes underscore the significance of this measure in elucidating the structure and distribution of entanglement within three-qubit quantum systems.

## 量子脉冲参数放大的有效描述

**Original Title:** Efficient Description of Parametric Amplification of Quantum Pulses

**Authors:** Victor Rueskov Christiansen, Klaus Mølmer, Emanuel Hubenschmid

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04759v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04759v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

经过参数放大的单个量子脉冲在输出中最多输入两个脉冲。在这项工作中，我们提出了一种有效的分析方法来寻找这些输出模式的量子状态。我们的方法将放大应用于真空而不是输入状态，然后应用从真空创建输入状态的运算符的变换版本。给定输入和输出脉冲模式函数，该方法是分析的，因此计算效率非常高，并且可以很容易地推广到多种非真空输入模式。我们通过计算由相干量子状态、薛定格猫和单量子输入量子状态的输入产生的输出量子状态来简化该方法。我们进一步使用该方法来获得在另一个最少人口模式中检测到真空时预示的两种输出模式之一的量子状态。


### Abstract

A single quantum pulse undergoing parametric amplification feeds into at most two pulses in the output. In this work, we present an efficient, analytical method for finding the quantum state of these output modes. Our method applies the amplification to the vacuum rather than to the input state, and subsequently applies a transformed version of the operator that creates the input state from vacuum. Given the input and output pulse mode functions, the method is analytical, and therefore computationally very efficient, and it can be readily generalized to multiple non-vacuum input modes. We exemplify the method by computing the output quantum states resulting from the input of a coherent, a Schrödinger cat, and a single photon input quantum state. We further employ the method to obtain the quantum state in one of the two output modes heralded upon detection of vacuum in the other, least populated, mode.

## M.对“原子凝聚体超辐射中微子发射的可能性”的评论。布拉松，L.加斯塔多和F.罗密欧，物理。Rev. D 113，053010（2026）

**Original Title:** Comment on "Possibility of superradiant neutrino emission by atomic condensate" by M. Blasone, L. Gastaldo and F. Romeo, Phys. Rev. D 113, 053010 (2026)

**Authors:** Wolfgang Ketterle, Hanzhen Lin, Yu-Kun Lu

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04761v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04761v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们表明，最近关于超辐射发射的提议无法回避我们的证据，即超辐射发射从根本上来说是不可能的。将分子中的两个费米子配对并不能消除由于费米子反相器而导致的中微子发射中干扰项的抵消。


### Abstract

We show that the recent proposal for superradiant emission of neutrinos cannot evade our proof that superradiant neutrino emission is fundamentally impossible. Pairing two fermions in a molecule does not remove the cancellation of interference terms in neutrino emission due to fermionic anticommutators.

## 想象力见证

**Original Title:** Imaginarity witness

**Authors:** Zhiqi Liang, Yufan Lin, Yu Guo, Yuqi Sun

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04763v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04763v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

想象力已被证明是量子信息中的重要资源。量子资源的证人理论，如纠缠证人、相关证人、相似性证人等已经建立，特别是纠缠证人和相关证人得到了广泛的探索。我们在这里介绍了除了[{Phys. Lett. A} \textBF{530}，130135（2025）]。在我们的框架内，引用基下的任何非实厄米特操作符都是相似性见证者，并且只有有限的操作符才能检测到所有相似性状态。作为纠缠和凝聚证人理论中探索的常见方法，我们然后探索这些相似性证人在不同情况下之间的关系：（i）何时他们可以检测到共同的假想状态，（ii）何时他们可以检测到相同的假想状态，（ii）何时他们服从更细的关系。最后，我们根据证人定义了一个相似性指标，称为目击相似性，并证明它与相似性的踪迹规范和相似性的稳健性相一致。


### Abstract

Imaginarity has shown to be an important resource in quantum information. The witness theory of quantum resource, such as entanglement witness, coherence witness, and imaginarity witness, has been established, in particular entanglement witness and coherence witness have been extensively explored. We present here another class of imaginarity witnesses beyond the one in [{Phys. Lett. A} \textbf{530}, 130135 (2025)]. Within our framework, any nonreal Hermitian operator under the reference basis is an imaginarity witness and only finite of them can detect all the imaginarity states. As the common approaches that were explored in the witness theories of entanglement and coherence, we then explore the relations between these imaginarity witnesses in different cases: (i) when they can detect common imaginary states, (ii) when they can detect the same sets of imaginary states, and (ii) when they obey the finer relation. Finally, we define an imaginarity measure in terms of witnesses, termed witnessed imaginarity, and prove that it coincides with both the trace norm of imaginarity and the robustness of imaginarity.


---


## 超越当前量子模拟，推动一维费米-哈伯德激动力学的经典前沿

**Original Title:** Pushing the Classical Frontier of 1D Fermi-Hubbard Quench Dynamics Beyond Current Quantum Simulations

**Authors:** Roman Rausch, Sukhbinder Singh, Saeed S. Jahromi, Augustine Kshetrimayum, Roman Orus

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04771v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04771v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

建立量子优势需要与最佳可实现的经典模拟进行比较。Q-ALT团队最近在IBM处理器上模拟了一维费米-哈伯德模型的失超动力学，在三分钟内完成了从$L=60$到时间$t=6$的进化，并声称比经典的时间相关变分原理（TDVP）模拟在键维$x =4096$处加速了3000美元。他们的经典基准测试需要在中央处理器集群上运行超过160个小时，未能在高纠缠机制$t\in[5.2，6]$中收敛，并且实验中最具挑战性的窗口未得到验证。在这里，我们通过利用费米-哈伯德Hamilton量的完整$\mathrm{U}（1）\times\mathrm{SU}（2）$对称性与GOP加速张量压缩相结合，突破经典模拟的边界。在四个NVIDIA H200图形处理器上实现高达$xi\approx 62 {，}000$的键合维度--是TDVP模拟中有史以来实现的最大值之一，是Q-ALT经典基线的十五倍--我们在整个模拟窗口内实现了完全收敛的结果，包括对之前未解决的高纠缠机制$t\in[5.2，6]$的严格认证。我们进一步将经典前沿推进到$t=7$，这超出了量子硬件实验和任何之前验证的全波函数经典演变。在键向维度与Q-ALT最佳经典运行相当时，我们的图形处理器实现在$\sim\中完成！100$分钟，直接将声称的3000美元\乘$量子优势减少到$\sim\！36\times$.这些结果大大缩小了量子-经典性能差距，并为大规模量子模拟的张量网络基准测试建立了新标准。


### Abstract

Establishing quantum advantage requires comparison against the best achievable classical simulation. The Q-CTRL team recently simulated quench dynamics of the one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model on an IBM processor, completing a $L=60$ evolution to time $t=6$ in under three minutes and claiming a $3000\times$ speedup over classical Time-Dependent Variational Principle (TDVP) simulation at bond dimension $χ=4096$. Their classical benchmark required over 160 hours on a CPU cluster, failed to converge in the high-entanglement regime $t\in[5.2,6]$, and left the most challenging window of the experiment unverified. Here, we push the boundaries of classical simulation by exploiting the full $\mathrm{U}(1)\times\mathrm{SU}(2)$ symmetry of the Fermi-Hubbard Hamiltonian combined with GPU-accelerated tensor contractions. Reaching bond dimensions up to $χ\approx62{,}000$ on four NVIDIA H200 GPUs -- among the largest ever achieved in TDVP simulations and fifteen times larger than Q-CTRL's classical baseline -- we achieve fully converged results across the entire simulation window, including rigorous certification of the previously unresolved high-entanglement regime $t\in[5.2,6]$. We further advance the classical frontier to $t=7$, which lies beyond the quantum hardware experiment and any previously verified classical evolution of the full wavefunction. At the bond dimension comparable to Q-CTRL's best classical run, our GPU implementation completes in $\sim\!100$ minutes, directly reducing the claimed $3000\times$ quantum advantage to $\sim\!36\times$. These results substantially narrow the quantum-classical performance gap and establish a new standard for tensor-network benchmarking of large-scale quantum simulations.


---


## 通过精确Hamilton变换实现费米ADAPT-VQE中资源高效的基于能量的运营商选择

**Original Title:** Resource-efficient energy-based operator selection in fermionic ADAPT-VQE via exact Hamiltonian transformation

**Authors:** Emanuele Rossi, Erik Rosendahl Kjellgren, Artur F. Izmaylov, Stephan P. A. Sauer, Karl Michael Ziems, Sonia Coriani

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04786v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04786v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

ADAPT-VQE中基于能源的运营商选择方法依赖于为池中每个运营商重建单参数能源格局。在费米子实现中，重建这种能源格局的成本常常成为瓶颈。我们通过精确的Hamilton变换来解决这个问题，该变换根据变换Hamilton的发电机相关碎片重新定义单参数能量格局。虽然我们的方法在数学上与标准费米子Rotoselect相同，但它有效地将成本降低了大约两倍，使其接近基于梯度的ADAPT-VQE。我们使用这个公式来对基于梯度和基于能量的选择方法进行基准测试，并结合两种反式优化策略--“最后”，其中仅优化附加的操作符，或“完整”，其中完整的反式被重新优化--并且具有固定轨道和轨道优化的公式。该基准包括平衡和拉伸几何形状的$\text{LiH}$、$\text{BeH}_2$和$\text{H}_2\text {O}$。在弱相关机制中，“最后”优化策略与基于能量的选择相结合能够高效构建准确的类比，同时避免任何VQE优化。随着相关性的增加，完全模拟重新优化和轨道优化成为决定收敛和总体资源成本的主要因素。这些结果表明，精确的Hamilton变换为减少基于费米能量的ADAPT-VQE的测量负担提供了一种有效途径。此外，该基准明确了操作员评分方法、重新优化策略和眼眶治疗在ADAPT-VQE性能中的相对作用。


### Abstract

The energy-based approach to operator selection in ADAPT-VQE relies on reconstructing the one-parameter energy landscape for each operator in the pool. In fermionic implementations, the cost of reconstructing this energy landscape often becomes a bottleneck. We address this issue through an exact Hamiltonian transformation that reformulates the one-parameter energy landscape according to a generator-dependent fragmentation of the transformed Hamiltonian. While our method is mathematically identical to standard fermionic Rotoselect, it effectively reduces its cost by about a factor of two, bringing it close to that of gradient-based ADAPT-VQE. We use this formulation to benchmark the gradient-based and energy-based selection approaches in combination with two ansatz-optimization strategies -- `last', where only the appended operator is optimized, or `full', where the full ansatz is re-optimized -- and with both fixed-orbital and orbital-optimized formulations. The benchmark comprises $\text{LiH}$, $\text{BeH}_2$, and $\text{H}_2\text{O}$ at both equilibrium and stretched geometries. In the weakly correlated regime, the `last' optimization strategy combined with energy-based selection enables the efficient construction of an accurate ansatz, while avoiding any VQE optimization. As correlation increases, full ansatz re-optimization and orbital optimization become the main factors governing convergence and overall resource cost. These results show that exact Hamiltonian transformations provide an effective route to reducing the measurement overhead of fermionic energy-based ADAPT-VQE. Moreover, the benchmark clarifies the relative role of operator scoring approach, re-optimization strategy, and orbital treatment in the performance of ADAPT-VQE.


---


## 受监控的混乱散射

**Original Title:** Monitored chaotic scattering

**Authors:** C. W. J. Beenakker, J. Sánchez Fernán, J. Tworzydło

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04794v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04794v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们将混乱散射的随机矩阵理论扩展到量子点，量子点的动力学由时间分辨测量来监控。从圆形系综绘制的散射矩阵开始，我们构建了相应的克劳斯操作器系综，用于监测多体密度矩阵的演变。在单粒子领域，测量结果的总和可以通过代数进行，从而给出转移电荷的离散时间量子主方程。我们用数字方法求解这个方程，并将所得的电荷转移统计数据与封闭形式的随机矩阵预测进行比较。后者依赖于被监测粒子的平分规则，我们将其表述为一个猜想并针对主方程进行测试。


### Abstract

We extend the random-matrix theory of chaotic scattering to quantum dots whose dynamics is monitored by time-resolved measurements. Starting from a scattering matrix drawn from a circular ensemble, we construct the corresponding ensemble of Kraus operators for the monitored evolution of the many-body density matrix. In the single-particle sector the sum over measurement outcomes can be carried out algebraically, giving a discrete-time quantum master equation for the transferred charge. We solve this equation numerically and compare the resulting charge-transfer statistics with closed-form random-matrix predictions. The latter rely on an equipartition rule for monitored particles, which we formulate as a conjecture and test against the master equation.


---


## 共振二色场光电子能谱：几何相的作用

**Original Title:** Photoelectron spectroscopy with a resonant dichromatic field: Role of geometric phase

**Authors:** Evan Munaro-Langloÿs, Axel Stenquist, Jan Marcus Dahlström

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04795v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04795v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们研究了暴露在近简并二色性激光脉冲下的共振驱动二原子的几何相控制。与基于相距很远的频率的传统两色方案相反，间隔很近的频率分量会产生缓慢变化的拍频包封，该包封反复逆转布洛赫球上的伪旋转。这使得能够对拉比动力学期间积累的几何相进行一致控制，并强烈修改所得的光电子谱。使用平顶脉冲包封的精确可解模型，我们通过分析推导出本质状态动力学，并分析辅助场和二向色驱动场本身引起的光电离。我们表明，奥特勒-汤斯双峰的形成可以用与完成伪旋转旋转期间获得的几何相相关的破坏性干涉来解释。除了典型的奥特勒-汤斯体系之外，拍频诱导的逆转动力学会导致定性不同的光谱结构，包括重新出现的中心峰和更高级的边带。这些效应源于拍频包线引起的非均匀时间演变，它修改了正激励幅度和负激励幅度之间的平衡。我们的结果确立了拍场控制作为超快光-物质相互作用中工程几何相干涉的一种途径，并建议在原子、分子和X射线驱动系统的连贯控制中有更广泛的应用。


### Abstract

We investigate geometric-phase control in resonantly driven two-level atoms exposed to near-degenerate dichromatic laser pulses. In contrast to conventional two-color schemes based on widely separated frequencies, the closely spaced frequency components generate a slowly varying beating envelope that repeatedly reverses the pseudo-spin rotation on the Bloch sphere. This enables coherent control of the geometric phase accumulated during Rabi dynamics and strongly modifies the resulting photoelectron spectra. Using an exactly solvable model for flat-top pulse envelopes, we derive the essential-state dynamics analytically and analyze photoionization induced both by an auxiliary field and by the dichromatic driving field itself. We show that the formation of Autler--Townes doublets can be interpreted in terms of destructive interference associated with geometric phases acquired during completed pseudo-spin rotations. Beyond the canonical Autler--Townes regime, beat-induced reversal dynamics lead to qualitatively different spectral structures, including re-emergent central peaks and higher-order sidebands. These effects originate from the nonuniform temporal evolution induced by the beating envelope, which modifies the balance between positive and negative excitation amplitudes. Our results establish beating-field control as a route toward engineering geometric-phase interference in ultrafast light--matter interactions and suggest broader applications in coherent control of atoms, molecules, and x-ray-driven systems.


---


## 极化子凝聚动力学中的极化库

**Original Title:** Polalrized reservoirs in dynamics of polariton condensation

**Authors:** I. A. Shelykh, A. V. Yulin

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04808v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04808v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们回顾了驱动消散旋量极化子凝聚物的动力学描述问题，重点关注与凝聚物的宏观波函数和非共振泵产生的非连贯激子库之间的耦合相对应的项。我们证明，当储层具有对应于面内线极化的斯托克斯分量的非零分量时，该理论的现有版本就会崩溃。利用旋转密度矩阵形式主义，建立了储层与凝聚层耦合的极化不变理论。


### Abstract

We review the problem of description of the dynamics of driven-disspipative spinor polariton condensates, focusing on the terms corresponding to the coupling between a macroscopic wavefunction of the condensdate and incoherent excitonic reservoir created by a non-resonant pump. We demonstrate that the existing version of the theory breaks down in case, when reservoir has non-zero components of the Stokes vector corresponding to in-plane linear polarization. The polarization invariant theory of reservoir to condensate coupling is formulated with use of the spin density matrix formalism.

## 各向同性误差对Grover算法复杂度的影响

**Original Title:** Effect of isotropic errors on the complexity of Grover's algorithm

**Authors:** Anurag Saha Roy, Jesús Lacalle

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04817v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04817v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

已证明各向同性误差不受传统误差修正技术的影响。虽然已经提出了通用理论框架来建模此类错误，但迄今为止还没有研究分析其对实际用例的具体影响。在这里，我们通过数值模拟探索各向同性误差对Grover搜索算法复杂性的影响，并分析其对算法性能和成功概率的影响。这些结果深入了解了Grover算法对各向同性误差的鲁棒性，凸显了在有噪量子硬件上实现的潜在挑战。这里给出的所有结果都是通过使用作为本工作的一部分开发的开源Python库\textttt {isotropic}通过数值模拟获得的。该库的源代码、数值模拟和文档可在https://www.github.com/lazyoracle/isotropic-error-analysis上在线获取。


### Abstract

Isotropic errors have been shown to be immune to conventional error correction techniques. While general theoretical frameworks have been proposed to model such errors, there have been no studies so far analysing their concrete impact on practical use-cases. Here we explore the effect of isotropic errors on the complexity of Grover's search algorithm through numerical simulations, with an analysis of the impact on the algorithm's performance and success probability. The results provide insights into the robustness of Grover's algorithm against isotropic errors, highlighting potential challenges for implementations on noisy quantum hardware. All results presented here are obtained through numerical simulations using the open-source python library \texttt{isotropic} developed as part of this work. The source code, numerical simulations and documentation for the library are available online at https://www.github.com/lazyoracle/isotropic-error-analysis .

## 强光与物质相互作用的有效汉密尔顿分子的调和

**Original Title:** Reconciliation of effective Hamiltonians for intense light-matter interaction

**Authors:** Jakob Nicolai Bruhnke, Jan Marcus Dahlström

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04835v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04835v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

微观状态模型是光物质相互作用广泛区域中量子控制和技术的核心。典型有效Hamilton量是从隔热消除、马尔科夫逼近和极点逼近中等效获得的。众所周知，这些近似会在高强度下分解，从而显着限制了它们对温和光物质相互作用的适用性。我们展示了如何通过应用准简并Rayleigh-Schrödinger微扰理论（QD-RSTP）来解决这一限制。我们将QD-RSPP与隔热消除相调和，并提出了隔热消除的准简并扩展，当本质状态的失调不可忽略时，该扩展是稳健的。QD-RSPAN的准确性在低频和高频区域均得到了证明，与高强度下的Floquet计算具有良好的一致性。对隔热消除的关键修正使得有效Hamilton的本征量是非垂直的。从物理上讲，这使我们能够解释不同基本状态与非基本状态耦合的不对称强度。我们预计，我们从QD-RSTP中对有效Hamilton体的系统方法将构成强光-物质相互作用和量子光学领域的新技术水平，具有可以想象的新型强耦合和量子控制现象。


### Abstract

Essential-state models are central for quantum control and technology in broad regimes of light-matter interaction. The canonical effective Hamiltonian is obtained equivalently from adiabatic elimination, the Markov approximation, and the pole approximation. These approximations are known to break down at high intensities, significantly limiting their applicability to moderate light-matter interaction. We show how this limitation can be addressed by applying quasi-degenerate Rayleigh-Schrödinger perturbation theory (QD-RSPT). We reconcile QD-RSPT with adiabatic elimination and propose a quasi-degenerate extension of adiabatic elimination that is robust when the detuning of the essential states is non-negligible. The accuracy of QD-RSPT is demonstrated in both the low- and high-frequency regime, showing excellent agreement with Floquet calculations at high intensities. The crucial corrections to adiabatic elimination make the eigenvectors of the effective Hamiltonian non-orthogonal. Physically, this allows us to account for the asymmetric strength with which different essential states couple to the non-essential states. We expect that our systematic approach to effective Hamiltonians from QD-RSPT will constitute a new state of the art in intense light-matter interaction and quantum optics with novel forms of strong coupling and quantum control phenomena being conceivable.


---


## 超越海明的解码量子干涉术：等级度量和翻译关联方案

**Original Title:** Decoded Quantum Interferometry Beyond Hamming: Rank-Metric and Translation Association Schemes

**Authors:** Alexandre Krajenbrink, Colin Krawchuk, Ansis Rosmanis, Matthias Rosenkranz

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04843v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04843v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

解码量子干涉术（DQI）使用连贯解码和量子傅里叶变换来寻找结构化优化问题的高质量解决方案。现有的分析与海明空间密切相关，海明空间是优化目标、迪克状态准备和算法的解码步骤的基础。在这里，我们将核心DQI机制扩展到海明空间之外具有平移对称性的有限几何体，其中点根据与基点的距离分组为壳。从数学上讲，这些几何图形是翻译关联方案。在这种设置中，可以通过跟踪每个壳的一个幅度来分析算法，并将准备好的状态偏向高质量的解决方案成为有限三对角特征值问题。作为一个非Hamming示例，我们开发了一个高效的DQI协议，用于寻找与目标矩阵具有最小阶差的m x n有限域矩阵。初始状态是固定排序矩阵上的均匀叠加，Gabidulin码为截止值l的高效低排序解码提供了候选。为了这一目标，它找到了具有接近min（m，n）-1的有效排序代理的解决方案，并且相应的预期分数可以转换为样本剩余排序上的恒概率界。对于Gabidulin最近的码字的情况下，覆盖半径的障碍表明，这一界并不意味着一个真正的最佳的附加保证，我们不要求一个量子的秩度量建设的优势。相反，结果识别了汉明空间之外的DQI的几何和编码成分。


### Abstract

Decoded Quantum Interferometry (DQI) uses coherent decoding and a quantum Fourier transform to find high-quality solutions of structured optimisation problems. Existing analyses are closely tied to Hamming space, which underlies the optimisation objective, Dicke state preparation and the decoding step of the algorithm. Here we extend the core DQI mechanism beyond Hamming space to finite geometries with translation symmetry, where points are grouped into shells by their distance from a basepoint. Mathematically, these geometries are translation association schemes. In this setting the algorithm can be analysed by tracking one amplitude per shell, and biasing the prepared state towards high-quality solutions becomes a finite tridiagonal eigenvalue problem. As a non-Hamming example, we develop an efficient DQI protocol for finding an m x n finite-field matrix with smallest rank difference to a target matrix. Initial states are uniform superpositions over fixed-rank matrices, and Gabidulin codes provide candidates for efficient low-rank decoding up to a cutoff l. For this objective, this finds solutions with an effective-rank proxy near min(m,n)-l, and the corresponding expected score can be converted into a constant-probability bound on the residual rank of a sample. For Gabidulin nearest-codeword instances, a covering-radius obstruction shows that this bound does not imply an additive guarantee for the true optimum, and we do not claim a quantum advantage for the rank-metric construction. The results instead identify the geometric and coding ingredients for DQI beyond Hamming space.


---


## 可调谐共振器集成磁力测量

**Original Title:** Tunable Resonator Integrated Magnetometry

**Authors:** Colin Stack, Brian Sears, Aruna Ramanayaka, David Ferguson, Ilya Sochnikov, Tony X. Zhou

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04914v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04914v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

量子技术革命正在重塑计算、传感和通信。在磁力测量中，最近的进展利用了对固态晶体中的旋转量子位和色心的精确控制，以进行介观尺度的传感。然而，在极低的温度下，由于其非侵入性和更高的灵敏度，超导传感技术仍然无与伦比。在这里，我们描述了一类具有低损耗和量子非破坏测量特性的超导传感器。我们在一家超级芯片铸造厂中设计和制造了一个超级通量可调共振器（tRes），并将其成熟到将电感-电容电路的速度与超级量子干涉器件（SQUID）的通量灵敏度相结合的水平，以在毫开氏温度下执行磁力测量来研究目标。我们以MHz磁采样率轻松介绍其基本功能，展示了两种测量模式，并研究了三个复杂性逐渐增加的电路，以提取特定于目标的信息。高灵敏度和快速读出特性的结合使tRes成为一款有吸引力且多功能的磁力计。


### Abstract

The quantum-technology revolution is reshaping computing, sensing, and communication. In magnetometry, recent advances leverage precise control of spin qubits and color centers in solid-state crystals for mesoscopic-scale sensing. Yet at very low temperatures, superconducting sensing technology remains unrivaled because of its non-invasiveness and higher sensitivity. Here we describe a class of superconducting sensors that offers low loss and quantum non-demolition measurement characteristics. We designed and fabricated a superconducting flux-tunable resonator (tRes) in a superconducting chip foundry and matured it to a level that combines the speed of an inductor-capacitor circuit with the flux sensitivity of a superconducting quantum interference device (SQUID) to perform magnetometry at milli-kelvin temperature to investigate targets. We introduce its fundamental functionality readily at MHz magnetic sampling rate, showcase two measurement modalities, and investigate three circuits with gradually increasing complexity to extract target-specific information. The combination of high sensitivity and fast readout characteristics make tRes an attractive and versatile magnetometer.

## 泡利代数Hermitian平方和谱系的收敛速度

**Original Title:** Convergence rates of Sum-of-Hermitian-Squares Hierarchies for the Pauli algebra

**Authors:** Ali Almasi, Dávid Bugár, Cambyse Rouzé, Peter Brown

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04940v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04940v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

非对易多元优化问题的矩/厄米平方和松弛已成为分析量子理论中问题的重要工具。尽管它们取得了广泛的成功，但人们对其收敛速度以及准确性知之甚少。在这项工作中，我们开发了由泡利代数生成的非交换多元优化问题的松弛的显式收敛速度--涵盖了n量子位系统的底价能量问题的应用。特别是，我们表明，收敛速度可以根据称为Krawtchouk多元性的一族的最小根来有界。我们的结果首次定量分析了非交换多项优化问题的松弛收敛速度。


### Abstract

Moment/Sum-of-Hermitian-Squares relaxations for noncommutative polynomial optimization problems have become an important tool for analyzing problems within quantum theory. Despite their widespread success, little is known about their rate of convergence and, consequently, their accuracy. In this work, we develop explicit convergence rates for relaxations of noncommutative polynomial optimization problems generated from the Pauli algebra -- covering applications to the ground state energy problem for n-qubit systems. In particular, we show that the rate of convergence can be bounded in terms of the smallest roots of a family of orthogonal polynomials known as Krawtchouk polynomials. Our result represents the first quantitative analysis of the rate of convergence for relaxations of noncommutative polynomial optimization problems.
