## 以千兆赫速率工作的无相相关量子密钥分发源

**Original Title:** Phase-correlation-free quantum key distribution source operating at gigahertz rates

**Authors:** Shashank Kumar, Alessandro Marcomini, Loïc Millet, Towsif Taher, Aurélien Cavalié, Raphael Houlmann, David Cabrerizo, Gianluca Boso, Marcos Curty, Rob Thew, Boris Korzh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04947v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04947v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

阶段随机化对于实际诱饵状态量子密钥分发（QKD）系统的安全性至关重要。通常，实现依赖于主动相随机化或放大切换的激光源。然而，在高重复率下，这些表现出相关性，这最终可能会损害安全性和性能。我们提出了一种基于在C频段工作的超发光发光二极管（SLED）的1.25 GHz相随机QKD光源，作为一种紧凑且经济高效的替代方案。该源生成$100 $ ps的光脉冲，脉冲间分离为$400$ ps，与高速时间点编码兼容。干涉测量表明相邻时间点之间的可见性> 99%，确认了相同量子信号内的强一阶相关性，而SLED的自发发射驱动性质确保了相邻信号之间固有的全局相随机化。这项工作为高速创建和测量QKD系统建立了一个基于SLED的可扩展平台。


### Abstract

Phase randomization is essential for the security of practical decoy-state quantum key distribution (QKD) systems. Commonly, implementations rely on laser sources which are either actively phase-randomized, or gain-switched. However, at high repetition rates these show correlations, which can ultimately compromise security and performance. We present a 1.25 GHz phase-randomized QKD source based on a super-luminescent light emitting diode (SLED) operating in the C-band as a compact and cost-effective alternative. The source generates $\sim100$ ps optical pulses with $400$ ps pulse-to-pulse separation, compatible with high-speed time-bin encoding. Interferometric measurements demonstrate $>99\%$ visibility between adjacent time bins, confirming strong first-order coherence within the same quantum signals, while the spontaneous-emission-driven nature of the SLED ensures intrinsic global phase randomization between adjacent signals. This work establishes a scalable SLED-based platform for high-speed prepare-and-measure QKD systems.

## VQE模拟器选择中的表达性、噪音和错误缓解

**Original Title:** Expressibility, Noise, and Error Mitigation in VQE Ansatz Selection

**Authors:** Peter Annis, Abe Kassem, Evan Coleman

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04955v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04955v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

变分量子本征解算器（VQE）是近期量子化学应用的一种有前途的算法，但选择最佳模拟电路仍然具有挑战性。表现性是一种量化电路探索希尔伯特空间能力的指标，已被提出作为模拟器选择的指南，但最近的工作表明，它在实际噪音下预测VQE性能的效果不一致，价格为H_2美元。我们将这项调查扩展到涵盖四种执行场景下的$H_2$和$H_3^+$：理想、有噪和有零噪音外推（ZNE）或概率错误消除（AEC）的有噪。我们发现错误缓解并不能可靠地恢复可表达性的预测能力。ZNE只减少了12个$H_2$电路中的4个和6个$H_3^+$电路中的4个的误差，而PEC实际上增加了12个$H_2$电路中的11个和所有6个$H_3^+$电路的误差。我们复制和扩展Saib等人。的关键发现，电路的排名在噪音下争夺（斯皮尔曼$ρ\约-0.1$之间的理想和嘈杂的排名），并确定一个新的结果：ZNE很大程度上保留嘈杂的排名（$ρ= +0.80$为$H_2$），而PEC积极重新排序他们（$ρ= -0.22$）。从密度矩阵模拟计算的噪声可表达性强烈地预测了$H_3^+$（Pearson $r =+0.91$，$p = 0.01$）的未减轻的性能，但是该度量在规模上是计算上难以处理的。我们证明，零成本电路布局指标（例如两量子位门数）为AEC降级提供了相当或更好的预测能力（对于$H_3，$r = +0.96$），而标准表达能力最好地预测$H_2$（$r = +0.74$和$r = +0.77$）的噪音和ZNE性能。


### Abstract

The variational quantum eigensolver (VQE) is a promising algorithm for near-term quantum chemistry applications, but selecting optimal ansatz circuits remains challenging. Expressibility, a metric quantifying a circuit's ability to explore the Hilbert space, has been proposed as a guide for ansatz selection, but recent work showed it inconsistently predicts VQE performance under realistic noise for $H_2$. We extend this investigation to cover both $H_2$ and $H_3^+$ under four execution scenarios: ideal, noisy, and noisy with zero-noise extrapolation (ZNE) or probabilistic error cancellation (PEC). We find that error mitigation does not reliably restore expressibility's predictive power. ZNE reduces error for only 4 of 12 $H_2$ circuits and 4 of 6 $H_3^+$ circuits, while PEC actually increases error in 11 of 12 $H_2$ circuits and all 6 $H_3^+$ circuits. We reproduce and extend Saib et al.'s key finding that circuit rankings scramble under noise (Spearman $ρ\approx -0.1$ between ideal and noisy rankings), and identify a new result: ZNE largely preserves noisy rankings ($ρ= +0.80$ for $H_2$) while PEC actively reorders them ($ρ= -0.22$). Noisy expressibility, computed from density matrix simulations, strongly predicts unmitigated performance for $H_3^+$ (Pearson $r = +0.91$, $p = 0.01$), but this metric is computationally intractable at scale. We demonstrate that zero-cost circuit topology metrics such as two-qubit gate count provide comparable or superior predictive power for PEC degradation ($r = +0.96$ for $H_3^+$), while standard expressibility best predicts noisy and ZNE performance for $H_2$ ($r = +0.74$ and $r = +0.77$).


---


## 量子最优输运的纠缠度量

**Original Title:** An Entanglement Measure from Quantum Optimal Transport

**Authors:** Enmin Shao, Lin Chen, Huixia He

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04969v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04969v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们提出了一个双方纠缠度量$E（p）$，定义为从一个状态到可分离状态集的最小1阶量子沃瑟斯坦距离。由于沃瑟斯坦度量的普遍数据处理不平等，该度量满足单一几何框架内的所有基本公理。Lipschitz二元公式给出了纯态和混合态的明确下限、两量子位系统的尖锐常数以及哈尔随机纯态的期望值。我们进一步建立了与纠缠证人的定量联系：任何负证人期望值都证明$E$的下限，而二元变分界正是Lipschitz-1证人可实现的最大违背。该方法自然地提供了次可加性、踪迹距离估计和局部可观测量的界限，同时指向大偏差猜想。这项工作在纠缠理论、最佳输运和实验纠缠检测的界面上建立了一个通用范式。


### Abstract

We propose a bipartite entanglement measure $E(ρ)$ defined as the minimal order-1 quantum Wasserstein distance from a state to the set of separable states. Owing to the universal data-processing inequality of the Wasserstein metric, the measure satisfies all fundamental axioms within a single geometric framework. A Lipschitz dual formulation yields explicit lower bounds for pure and mixed states, a sharp constant for two-qubit systems, and an expected value for Haar-random pure states. We further establish a quantitative connection to entanglement witnesses: any negative witness expectation value certifies a lower bound on $E$, and the dual variational bound is exactly the maximal violation achievable by a Lipschitz-1 witness. The approach naturally provides subadditivity, trace-distance estimates, and bounds on local observables, while pointing toward large-deviation conjectures. This work furnishes a versatile paradigm at the interface of entanglement theory, optimal transport, and experimental entanglement detection.


---


## 带反馈环的钍-229光学核钟

**Original Title:** A thorium-229 optical nuclear clock with feedback loop

**Authors:** L. Toscani De Col, T. Riebner, I. Morawetz, F. Schneider, N. Sempelmann, J. Schlachet-Lépinay, F. Schaden, M. Bartokos, G. A. Kazakov, K. Beeks, B. Gerstenecker, M. Pimon, S. Lahs, A. Hellerschmied, T. Lercher, J. Premper, A. Niessner, M. Matus, H. Denker, M. Cizek, O. Cip, V. Lal, G. Zitzer, V. Petrov, J. Tiedau, M. V. Okhapkin, E. Peik, T. Schumm

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.04997v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.04997v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

钍-229同位素的激光可访问核转变已被确定为实现光学核钟的有希望的候选者。这样的核时钟可能会与基于原子或离子电子壳层转变的当前光学时钟相媲美或优于基于原子或离子电子壳层转变的光学时钟，预计对外部扰动更加稳健，并在物理学基本原理的基于时钟的测试中提供更高的灵敏度。在这里，我们通过基于连续吸收光谱的快速反馈将连续波激光稳定到148纳米核转变，来实现钍-229核时钟。钍-229原子核嵌入毫米大小的室温CGM晶体中。将148纳米辐射的亚调和频连续与ZB+单离子时钟进行比较。核钟显示了$3 ' cdot 10 ' s的分数频率不稳定性的简单散粒噪音限制缩放，其中$T $是平均时间，连续运行1天内接近$10 ' s $不稳定性。预计未来的固体核钟的不稳定性将改善几个数量级。我们使用核钟通过在20秒到1天之间的时间尺度上寻找核过渡能的周期性波动和缓慢漂移来约束超轻暗物质的模型。得益于钍-229跃迁增强的灵敏度，这些约束与暗物质与光子耦合的最佳原子钟竞争，并超越了先前关于与强力和夸克耦合的测量。


### Abstract

The laser-accessible nuclear transition in the thorium-229 isotope has been identified as a promising candidate for the realization of an optical nuclear clock. Such a nuclear clock might rival or outperform current optical clocks based on electron-shell transitions in atoms or ions, is expected to be more robust against external perturbations, and provides enhanced sensitivity in clock-based tests of fundamental principles of physics. Here, we implement a thorium-229 nuclear clock by stabilizing a continuous-wave laser to the 148 nm nuclear transition with rapid feedback based on continuous absorption spectroscopy. The thorium-229 nuclei are embedded into a millimeter-sized, room temperature calcium fluoride crystal. A subharmonic of the 148 nm radiation is continuously compared to a Yb+ single-ion clock. The nuclear clock shows a simple shot-noise limited scaling of the fractional frequency instability of $3\cdot 10^{-12} \sqrt{τ/\text{s}}$ where $τ$ is the averaging time, approaching $10^{-15}$ instabilities over 1 day of continuous operation. Improvements of the instability by several orders of magnitude can be projected for future solid-state nuclear clocks. We use the nuclear clock to constrain models of ultralight dark matter by searching for periodic fluctuations and slow drifts in the nuclear transition energy, on time scales between 20 s and 1 day. Drawing benefit from the enhanced sensitivity of the thorium-229 transition, these constraints compete with the best atomic clocks concerning dark matter coupling to photons and go beyond previous measurements regarding coupling to the strong force and quarks.


---


## 多量子位转换子处理器中测量引发的状态转变

**Original Title:** Measurement-induced state transitions in multi-qubit transmon processors

**Authors:** Baptiste Hoyau, Alexander McDonald, Boris M. Varbanov, Manuel H. Muñoz-Arias, Alexandre Blais

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05010v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05010v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

众所周知，电路QED中传输子量子位的分散读出在小到中等的测量驱动幅度下会失去其量子非破坏特性。据了解，这种现象起源于偶然多量子共振时的Laundau-Zener转变，其中$n$驱动量子可以将转换子促进$m$水平。这种解释已被证明与描述单个传输子的频散读出的实验一致。然而，嵌入多量子位芯片中的转换子的这些测量引起的状态转变（MIST）的影响在很大程度上仍然没有被探索。在这里，我们表明，其他组件（例如量子位和耦合器）的存在可能会影响测量传输子的MIST阈值。为了得到这些结果，我们提出了一种通用方法来描述当读出下的量子位耦合到其他电路元件时测量引发的转变，这是基于电路QED的量子处理器中普遍存在的情况。作为一个例子，我们考虑两个转换子量子位的情况，并表明旁观量子位可能受到读出量子位的测量引发的转变的影响，相反，旁观量子位的存在可以降低读出量子位的MIST阈值。最后，我们探索在两个量子位之间添加耦合器模式如何进一步修改这些效应。


### Abstract

Dispersive readout of the transmon qubit in circuit QED is known to lose its quantum non-demolition character at small to moderate measurement drive amplitudes. This phenomenon is understood to originate from Laundau-Zener transitions at accidental multi-photon resonances, where $n$ drive photons can promote the transmon by $m$ levels. This interpretation has been shown to be in agreement with experiments characterizing the dispersive readout of a single transmon. The impact of these measurement-induced state transition (MIST) of a transmon embedded in a multi-qubit chip, however, remains largely unexplored. Here, we show that the presence of other components, such as qubits and couplers, can affect the MIST threshold of a measured transmon. To arrive at these results, we present a general method to characterize measurement-induced transition when the qubit under readout is coupled to other circuit elements, a ubiquitous situation in circuit QED-based quantum processors. As an example, we consider the case of two transmon qubits, and we show that the spectator qubit can be impacted by the measurement-induced transition of the readout qubit and, conversely, that the presence of the spectator qubit can lower the MIST threshold of the readout qubit. Finally, we explore how adding a coupler mode between the two qubits further modifies these effects.


---


## 量子信道经典识别能力的高斯平均宽度强逆界

**Original Title:** Gaussian mean width strong converse bound on the classical identification capacity of quantum channels

**Authors:** Satvik Singh

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05032v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05032v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们在量子通道的经典识别能力上建立了单字母且可有效计算的强逆界。通过为$n$-fold通道输出空间配备积状态加权$Sigma $-欧几里得几何，我们允许识别码的踪迹距离分离约束由欧几里得覆盖估计控制。使用Sudakov不等式，我们通过加权几何中的高斯平均宽度来限制$n$重通道输出的覆盖数，其$n$的指数增长由单字母正操作符的操作符规范决定。在对所有加权状态$Sigma $进行优化后，这会产生通道识别能力的强逆界，这也允许半定表示。我们的方法改进了几个重要例子（例如去极化、泡利、擦除和幅度衰减通道）的识别能力的最著名的逆界。我们还讨论了该方法对输出空间上更一般的欧几里得几何的扩展。


### Abstract

We establish a single-letter and efficiently computable strong converse bound on the classical identification capacity of quantum channels. By equipping the $n$-fold channel output space with a product state-weighted $σ$-Euclidean geometry, we allow trace-distance separation constraints for identification codes to be controlled by Euclidean covering estimates. Using Sudakov's inequality, we bound the covering numbers of the $n$-fold channel outputs via their Gaussian mean widths in the weighted geometry, whose exponential growth in $n$ is governed by the operator norm of a single-letter positive operator. Upon optimizing over all weighing states $σ$, this yields a strong converse bound on the identification capacity of the channel, which also admits a semidefinite representation. Our method improves the best known converse bounds on the identification capacity of several important examples, such as depolarizing, Pauli, erasure, and amplitude damping channels. We also discuss extensions of this method to more general Euclidean geometries on the output space.


---


## 量子点旋转法拉第光学控制中拉比振荡到隔热布居转换的交叉

**Original Title:** Crossover from Rabi oscillations to adiabatic population switching in the Faraday optical control of quantum dot spins

**Authors:** Jan M. Kaspari, Zhe Xian Koong, Dorian A. Gangloff, Michał Gawełczyk, Doris E. Reiter

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05033v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05033v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

法拉第几何结构中的受激拉曼跳变允许同时进行单次量子位读出和量子位控制。它涉及通过辅助激发状态驱动不平衡的$~$系统。由于同时驱动两个转变，并具有不等的失调，因此产生的时间相关斯塔克位移会产生超出常规图像的额外共振条件。我们确定了一个独特的机制，其中重复通过避免的交叉点会导致兰道-齐纳-施图克尔伯格干扰引起的阶跃式种群倒置。通过改变去调和节拍音符，我们展示了从拉比类振荡到隔热粒子数切换的受控连续交叉。这些发现确立了振荡斯塔克位移作为法拉第几何中工程和控制旋转动力学的机制。


### Abstract

Stimulated Raman transitions in Faraday geometry allow for simultaneous single-shot qubit readout and qubit control. It involves driving an unbalanced $Λ$ system via an auxiliary excited state. Due to the simultaneous driving of both transitions with unequal detuning, the resulting time-dependent Stark shift gives rise to additional resonance conditions beyond the conventional picture. We identify a distinct regime in which repeated passages through avoided crossings lead to step-like population inversion arising from Landau-Zener-Stückelberg interference. By changing the detuning beatnote, we demonstrate a controlled continuous crossover from Rabi-like oscillations to adiabatic population switching. These findings establish the oscillating Stark shift as a mechanism for engineering and controlling spin dynamics in Faraday geometry.

## 作为循环子模的广义Bicycle码及其自同构结构

**Original Title:** Generalized Bicycle Codes as Cyclic Submodules and their Automorphism Structure

**Authors:** AJ Davenport, John Blue, Isaac Chuang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05044v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05044v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

当量子码的自同质存在时，它们可以通过量子位重新标记提供一条实现故障门的途径。尽管很有用，但人们对给定代码中自同射出现的条件仍然知之甚少。在本文中，我们开发了一个代数框架，用于系统地分析和工程广义自行车（GB）码中的自同射。我们方法的核心是推导出多项环空间、检验矩阵空间和$\mathbb{F}_2^{2\ell}$量子位空间之间的三空间依赖关系，类似于经典循环码研究中发现的结构。通过将GB码表示为$R_\ell ' 2 $的一对循环子模，其中$R_\ell \cong \mathbb{F}_2[x]/\langle x^\ell-1\rangle $，我们将代码自同性的搜索简化为确定性代数问题，推导出了由循环转移、环自同性和块交换构建的块可分自同性存在的充分必要条件。我们将这些条件与折叠横向门框架联系起来，为$H$-、$S$-和$CX$-型折叠横向门的存在提供了明确的标准。我们进一步讨论逻辑运算符的结构化基础，以确定给定自同射的逻辑动作。最后，我们介绍了最大立方体根（MCR）代码家族，这是一个围绕最大化自同灵活性和折叠CX门原则构建的GB代码家族。我们展示了一组$k=2$ MCR代码，最多$d=13$，通过自同射和折叠横向门生成2量子位Clifford群，稳定器权重范围从8到16，以及$k>2$ MCR代码，至少有20个不同的逻辑门可从自同射实现。这是反向设计的第一次演示：使用这些方法从头开始围绕丰富的自同结构构建代码。


### Abstract

Automorphisms of quantum codes, when they exist, offer a pathway toward fault-tolerant gate implementation via qubit relabeling. Although useful, the conditions under which automorphisms appear in a given code remain poorly understood. In this paper, we develop an algebraic framework for systematically analyzing and engineering automorphisms in Generalized Bicycle (GB) codes. Central to our approach is the derivation of a three-space dependency between the polynomial ring space, the parity check matrix space, and the $\mathbb{F}_2^{2\ell}$ qubit space, similar to the structure found in the study of classical cyclic codes. By expressing GB codes as a pair of cyclic submodules of $R_\ell^2$, where $R_\ell \cong \mathbb{F}_2[x]/\langle x^\ell-1\rangle$, we reduce the search for code automorphisms to a deterministic algebraic problem, deriving necessary and sufficient conditions for the existence of block-separable automorphisms built from cyclic shifts, ring automorphisms and block-swaps. We connect these conditions to the fold-transversal gate framework, providing explicit criteria for the existence of $H$-, $S$-, and $CX$-type fold-transversal gates. We further discuss structured bases for logical operators in order to determine the logical action of a given automorphism. Finally, we introduce the Maximal Cube Root (MCR) code family, a family of GB codes constructed around the principle of maximizing automorphism flexibility and fold-CX gates. We demonstrate a collection of $k=2$ MCR codes up to $d=13$ generating the 2-qubit Clifford group via automorphism and fold-transversal gates, with stabilizer weight ranging from 8 to 16, and $k>2$ MCR codes with a minimum of 20 distinct logical gates achievable from automorphisms. This serves as a first demonstration of inverse design: using these methods to build codes around a rich automorphism structure from the ground up.


---


## 测量量子位系统中的纠缠

**Original Title:** Measuring Entanglement in Qubit System

**Authors:** Vignesh S, Tabish Qureshi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05056v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05056v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

提出了一种在平衡双路径干涉仪中测量纠缠的操作方法，其中路径信息由一定的内部自由度承载，而该自由度反过来又与辅助系统纠缠。该分析基于三重描述，涉及路径、内部量子位自由度以及与内部自由度纠缠在一起的一些辅助状态。然后将其应用于两种物理上不同的实验情况：具有1/2旋转粒子的改进型斯特恩-格拉赫干涉仪和具有携带极化的量子的马赫-曾德干涉仪。辅助自由度可能无法通过实验获得。追踪辅助系统，并采用基于内部自由度的量子擦除过程，证明了内部自由度和辅助之间的基于并发的纠缠测量可以直接从两个输出通道的可测量不对称性中提取。这些结果表明，干涉实验中的相干性损失、量子擦除和纠缠估计源于相同的基础相关结构，并为量化量子位系统中的纠缠提供了一个紧凑的实验可访问的框架。


### Abstract

An operational way of measuring entanglement in a balanced two-path interferometers is presented, where path information is carried by some internal degree of freedom which, in turn, gets entangled with an ancilla system. The analysis is based on a tripartite description involving paths, an internal qubit degree of freedom, and some ancillary states entangled with the internal degree of freedom. It is then applied to two physically distinct experimental situations: a modified Stern-Gerlach interferometer with spin-1/2 particles and a Mach-Zehnder interferometer with photons carrying polarization. The ancilla degree of freedom may not be experimentally accessible. Tracing out the ancillary system, and employing a quantum erasing procedure based on the internal degree of freedom, it is demonstrated that a concurrence-based measure of the entanglement, between the internal degree of freedom and the ancilla, can be extracted directly from measurable asymmetry of the two output channels. These results show that loss of coherence, quantum erasure, and entanglement estimation in interferometric experiments arise from the same underlying correlation structure and provide a compact experimentally accessible framework for quantifying entanglement in qubit systems.


---


## 利用低级Hessian优化的高保真中性原子门

**Original Title:** High-fidelity neutral atom gates leveraging low-rank Hessian optimization

**Authors:** Genyue Liu, Guillaume Bornet, Deniz Kurdak, Mingxuan Xiao, Chenyuan Li, Bichen Zhang, Jeff D. Thompson

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05060v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05060v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

量子最优控制可以产生快速且鲁棒的多量子位门，但通过实验校准产生的多维波波仍然具有挑战性，因为在大参数空间上的直接搜索收敛缓慢。我们以量子控制景观的低等级结构为基础，开发并测试了基于黑森式的最佳控制门校准方法。该方法识别了影响领先阶保真度的少数几个波型方向，方向数量由可访问的泄漏和一致误差通道设置，并仅在此主空间内使用闭环实验反馈进行优化。我们将这种方法应用于亚稳态171 Mb核旋转量子位上的幅度稳健受控Z门。通过实验，我们验证了预测的黑森敏感方向，并展示了优化协议的快速收敛。优化后的门达到了0.9959（2）的原始保真度，在没有检测到损失的情况下增加到0.99902（7），并且在激光功率变化高达20%的情况下性能基本上没有变化。我们进一步表明，相同的保真度黑森方向可以纠正某些Hamilton参数误差。这些结果将低阶Hessian优化建立为用于多维最优控制门的一种高效且物理激励的校准策略，该策略广泛适用于许多量子位类型。


### Abstract

Quantum optimal control can produce fast and robust multi-qubit gates, but experimentally calibrating the resulting high-dimensional waveforms remains challenging because direct searches over large parameter spaces converge slowly. Building on the low-rank structure of quantum-control landscapes, we develop and benchmark a Hessian-based calibration method for optimal-control gates. The method identifies the few waveform directions that affect fidelity to leading order, with the number of directions set by the accessible leakage and coherent error channels, and optimizes only within this principal space using closed-loop experimental feedback. We apply this approach to an amplitude-robust controlled-Z gate on metastable-state 171Yb nuclear-spin qubits. Experimentally, we verify the predicted Hessian-sensitive directions and demonstrate rapid convergence of the optimization protocol. The optimized gate reaches a raw fidelity of 0.9959(2), increasing to 0.99902(7) after postselection on no detected loss, and the performance is essentially unchanged under laser-power variations of up to 20%. We further show that the same fidelity Hessian directions can correct certain Hamiltonian parameter errors. These results establish low-rank Hessian optimization as an efficient and physically motivated calibration strategy for high-dimensional optimal-control gates, which is broadly applicable to many qubit types.


---


## 贝尔抽样的费米子非高斯性：单调和高效量子算法

**Original Title:** Fermionic non-Gaussianity via Bell sampling: monotones and efficient quantum algorithms

**Authors:** Poetri Sonya Tarabunga

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05066v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05066v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

费米子非高斯性是释放费米子量子平台全部计算能力的重要资源。在这项工作中，我们开发了费米非高斯性的单调和有效的量子算法，所有这些算法都建立在运算符$Á = \sum_{j=1}&{2n}γ_j\otimesγ_j$的本征值结构之上，定义在$n$模式费米状态的两个副本上，通过贝尔采样访问。特别是，我们引入了偶数纯状态的\ð {桥度}，这是一种新型的非高斯单调，被定义为由状态的两个副本填充的$ð $的最大特征值部分。我们的关键技术结果是，在后选择的高斯协议下，桥度是不增加的，这产生了高斯转换的不去定理，比从以前已知的单调中获得的定理更强，并表明费米子非高斯性的资源理论在精确转换设置中是不可逆转的。除此之外，桥度还表现出几个进一步的特征：它（i）易于计算，（ii）通过贝尔采样有效地见证，（iii）状态准备的非高斯门复杂度的下限，（iv）控制产生量子状态设计的非高斯门复杂度，（v）通过Choi--Jamiozowski同形自然扩展到混合状态。我们进一步开发了一个近似变体以及一个有效可测量的下限，直接基于贝尔采样数据，产生了大约准备任何状态的非高斯成本的可实验证明的下限。最后，相同的特征值结构构成了两个基于Bell采样的算法基元的基础，两者都具有多项样本复杂性：具有完美完整性的两副本高斯性测试，在共享该属性的两副本测试中是最佳的，以及针对状态2美元-匹配门不变集合的设计属性的测试。


### Abstract

Fermionic non-Gaussianity is an essential resource for unlocking the full computational power of fermionic quantum platforms. In this work we develop monotones and efficient quantum algorithms for fermionic non-Gaussianity, all built on the eigenvalue structure of the operator $Λ= \sum_{j=1}^{2n}γ_j\otimesγ_j$ defined on two copies of an $n$-mode fermionic state, accessible via Bell sampling. In particular, we introduce the \emph{bridge degree} of even pure states, a novel non-Gaussianity monotone defined as the largest eigenvalue sector of $Λ$ populated by two copies of the state. Our key technical result is that the bridge degree is non-increasing under post-selected Gaussian protocols, which yields no-go theorems for Gaussian conversion stronger than those obtainable from previously known monotones and shows that the resource theory of fermionic non-Gaussianity is irreversible in the exact-conversion setting. Beyond this, the bridge degree exhibits several further features: it (i) is easy to compute, (ii) is efficiently witnessed through Bell sampling, (iii) lower-bounds the non-Gaussian gate complexity of state preparation, (iv) controls the non-Gaussian gate complexity of producing quantum state designs, and (v) naturally extends to mixed states via the Choi--Jamiołkowski isomorphism. We further develop an approximate variant together with an efficiently measurable lower bound, yielding an experimentally certifiable lower bound on the non-Gaussian cost of approximately preparing any state, based directly on Bell-sampling data. Finally, the same eigenvalue structure underlies two Bell-sampling-based algorithmic primitives, both with polynomial sample complexity: a two-copy Gaussianity test with perfect completeness, optimal among two-copy tests sharing this property, and a test for the state $2$-design property of matchgate-invariant ensembles.


---


## 通过Floquet控制的固体缺陷的压缩音素激光

**Original Title:** Squeezed Phonon Lasing via Floquet-Controlled Solid-State Defects

**Authors:** Hugo Molinares, Gianluca Rastelli, Victor Montenegro, Vitalie Eremeev

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05083v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05083v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们提出了一种用于音素激光发射的通用Floquet工程方案，该方案能够从传统激光发射连续过渡到锁定压缩音素激光发射。我们专注于基于嵌入圆形六方BN（hBN）膜中的色心的固态平台，证明了与主旋转和辅助旋转相耦合、并通过有效的Floquet驱动同时控制的机械振荡器表现出压缩状态放大和冷却动力学，导致稳定的压缩音素激光器的出现。我们分析了系统的稳态特性，包括激光阈值、机械占据、发射光谱和二阶相关性。此外，我们表明Floquet工程可以实现锁相激光发射，同时实现受控的垂直压缩，从而提供了一条简单而有效的量子力学系统压缩激光发射途径。我们的结果为固态平台中压缩音素激光器的产生提供了新的见解，并在量子计量学中具有潜在的应用。


### Abstract

We propose a general Floquet-engineered scheme for phonon lasing that enables a continuous transition from conventional lasing to phase-locked squeezed phonon lasing. Focusing on a solid-state platform based on color centers embedded in a circular hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) membrane, we demonstrate that a mechanical oscillator coupled to principal and ancilla spins, and controlled via effective Floquet driving simultaneously exhibits squeezed-state amplification and cooling dynamics, leading to the emergence of a stable squeezed phonon laser. We analyse the steady-state properties of the system, including the lasing threshold, mechanical occupation, emission spectrum and second-order correlations. Furthermore, we show that Floquet engineering can realize phase-locked lasing while enabling controlled quadrature squeezing, thereby providing a simple yet effective route toward squeezed lasing in quantum mechanical systems. Our results offer new insights into the generation of squeezed phonon lasers in solid-state platforms, with potential applications in quantum metrology.


---


## 相互作用Majorana链超对称带隙相位中的孤子-反孤子对

**Original Title:** Soliton-antisoliton pairs in the supersymmetric gapped phase of an interacting Majorana chain

**Authors:** Alberto Nocera, Mobin Shakeri, Armin Rahmani, Ian Affleck

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05095v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05095v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

马约拉纳费米子的强相互作用链实现了超对称三临界伊辛相，超对称性（SUSY）延伸到与三临界点相邻的泡沫破缺有序相。尽管超对称性在三临界点的特征已经很好地理解，但它们在间隙阶段的行为仍然不太清楚。在这里，我们解决了两个关键问题：SUSY如何在间隙阶段表现出来以及该阶段兴奋的性质是什么。我们表明，在热力学极限下，在三临界点保持有限的传统SUSY诊断在伊辛侧立即偏离，但在间隙相更深处不断衰减到零，从而发出SUSY持续存在的信号。聚焦于超对称有间隙区域中的最低激发态，我们发现激发由分隔不同有序区域的孤立子-反孤立子对组成。每个孤立子结合了一个涌现的局部马约拉纳模，并共同形成了一个非局部狄拉克费米子。这种狄拉克模式的占据区分了具有偶数费米子宇称和奇费米子宇称的本征状态。


### Abstract

A strongly interacting chain of Majorana fermions realizes the supersymmetric tricritical Ising phase, with supersymmetry (SUSY) extending into a symmetry-broken ordered phase adjacent to the tricritical point. Although the signatures of SUSY at the tricritical point are well understood, their behavior in the gapped phase remains less clear. Here, we address two key questions: how SUSY manifests in the gapped phase and what is the nature of the excitations in this phase. We show that, in the thermodynamic limit, a conventional SUSY diagnostic that remains finite at the tricritical point diverges immediately on the Ising side, yet decays continuously to zero deeper in the gapped phase, signaling the persistence of SUSY. Focusing on the lowest excited states in the supersymmetric gapped regime, we find that the excitations consist of soliton-antisoliton pairs separating distinct ordered regions. Each soliton binds an emergent localized Majorana mode, and together the pair forms a nonlocal Dirac fermion. The occupation of this Dirac mode distinguishes eigenstates with even and odd fermion parity.


---


## 来自分数可扩展性的高斯量子重复器的禁区定理

**Original Title:** No-Go Theorem for Gaussian Quantum Repeaters from Fractional Extendibility

**Authors:** Rabsan Galib Ahmed, Graeme Smith

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05097v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05097v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

光通道中的光损失从根本上限制了远程可靠的量子通信。克服这一限制的标准方法是使用量子转发器节点，这些节点通常执行实验要求高的非高斯操作。然而，高斯转发器协议是否可以提高玻色子衰减通道上的量子通信速率仍然悬而未决。在这项工作中，我们证明了量子网络中高斯量子转发器的不通过定理。具体来说，我们表明，任何由高斯运算、零差测量和任意经典通信组成的转发器链都无法将纯损耗衰减通道的量子容量增强到超出直接传输可实现的容量的范围。我们的证明将$k$-可扩展性推广到高斯状态的分数可扩展性概念，并建立了其一些有用的性质，从而为分析高斯量子网络提供了一个强大的框架。


### Abstract

Photon loss in optical channels fundamentally limits long-range reliable quantum communication. A standard approach to overcoming this limitation is the use of quantum repeater nodes, which typically perform experimentally demanding non-Gaussian operations. However, whether Gaussian repeater protocols can enhance quantum communication rates over bosonic attenuation channels has remained open. In this work, we prove a no-go theorem for Gaussian quantum repeaters in a quantum network. Specifically, we show that any repeater chain composed of Gaussian operations, homodyne measurements, and arbitrary classical communication cannot enhance the quantum capacity of a pure-loss attenuation channel beyond that achievable by direct transmission. Our proof introduces a generalisation of $k$-extendibility to a notion of fractional extendibility for Gaussian states and establishes some of its useful properties, thereby providing a powerful framework for analysing Gaussian quantum networks.


---


## 通过排列不变性确定量子时间下限

**Original Title:** Quantum Time Lower Bounds by Permutation Invariance

**Authors:** Qisheng Wang

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05099v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05099v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

文献中已知各种计算问题的量子样本复杂性和量子查询复杂性的严格界限，而量子时间复杂性的严格界限（即，量子电路的大小）仍然悬而未决。在本文中，我们提供了一个框架，通过降低量子样本复杂性来建立量子时间复杂度的下限，以测试量子状态的排列不变性质。作为一个应用，当给定对输入量子状态的样本访问时，我们获得了一系列匹配的下限，包括：   1. SWAP测试由Buhrman、Cleve、Watrous和de Wolf完成（Phys. Rev. Lett. 2001）对于估计纯度$\operatorName{tra}（p ' 2）$和盗汗$\operatorName{tra}（p Sigma）$来说是时间最优的。   2.轮班测试由Ekert、Alves、Oi、Horodecki、Horodecki和Kwek完成（Phys. Rev. Lett. 2002）对于估计高级函元$\operatorName{tra}（p ' k）$来说是时间最优的。   3. Harrow和Montanaro提出的多方纯状态的产品性测试器（J. ACN 2013）是时间最优的。   4. Lloyd、Mohseni和Rebentrost（Nat. Phys. 2014）提出的LMR协议对于实现关于纯状态的反射运算符来说是时间最优的。   5. Wang和Zhang提出的采样器（IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory 2025）对于纯状态来说是时间最优的。   6. Wang和Zhang提出的纯状态轨迹距离和保真度估计器（ICALP 2026）是时间最优的。   据我们所知，这是第一种允许我们系统性地建立量子时间复杂性严格下限的方法。


### Abstract

Tight bounds on quantum sample complexity and quantum query complexity have been known for various computational problems in the literature, whereas tight bounds on quantum time complexity (i.e., the size of quantum circuits) remain unresolved. In this paper, we provide a framework to establish lower bounds on the quantum time complexity for testing permutation-invariant properties of quantum states, via a reduction from quantum sample complexity. As an application, we obtain a series of matching lower bounds when given sample access to the input quantum states, including:
  1. The SWAP test due to Buhrman, Cleve, Watrous, and de Wolf (Phys. Rev. Lett. 2001) is time-optimal to estimate the purity $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^2)$ and the inner product $\operatorname{tr}(ρσ)$.
  2. The Shift test due to Ekert, Alves, Oi, Horodecki, Horodecki, and Kwek (Phys. Rev. Lett. 2002) is time-optimal to estimate the high-order functionals $\operatorname{tr}(ρ^k)$.
  3. The productness tester for multipartite pure states due to Harrow and Montanaro (J. ACM 2013) is time-optimal.
  4. The LMR protocol due to Lloyd, Mohseni, and Rebentrost (Nat. Phys. 2014) is time-optimal to implement the reflection operator about a pure state.
  5. The samplizer due to Wang and Zhang (IEEE Trans. Inf. Theory 2025) is time-optimal for pure states.
  6. The estimator for pure-state trace distance and fidelity due to Wang and Zhang (ICALP 2026) is time-optimal.
  To the best of our knowledge, this is the first method that allows us to systematically establish tight lower bounds on quantum time complexity.


---


## 倒相谐振子中的量子物理实验探索

**Original Title:** Experimentally probing the Quantum Physics in the Inverted Harmonic Oscillator

**Authors:** Si-Cong Ji, Philipp Schüttelkopf, Nataliia Bazhan, Federica Cataldini, Mohammadamin Tajik, Frederik S. Møller, Igor Mazets, Sebastian Erne, Jörg Schmiedmayer

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05125v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05125v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

当量子系统通过不稳定的不稳定点时，局部动力学就会减弱为反相谐振子（IHO）。它沿着一个象限呈指数级放大，同时压缩另一个象限，从微观零点涨落产生宏观扩展的量子状态。我们通过原子芯片上的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体来实现这种动态。射频敷料将横向和谐限制翻转到IHO中。通过相空间断层扫描，我们遵循演变量子状态的完整维格纳函数，观察到10.6（1.3）分贝的亚真空压缩，并通过时间逆转IHO演变来测试相干可逆性。两个子云之间的物质波干涉证实了远远超出初始膨胀的时间尺度上的量子一致性。我们的实验将超冷原子建立为不稳定量子动力学的清洁、受控、多体平台，为基于时间逆转的一致性认证的力传感开辟了一条道路，并为暴胀场动力学中量子涨落放大的模拟研究开辟了道路。


### Abstract

When a quantum system passes through an unstable fixed point the local dynamics reduces to the inverted harmonic oscillator (IHO). It exponentially amplifies along one quadrature while squeezing the other, producing macroscopically extended quantum states from microscopic zero-point fluctuations. We realize this dynamics with a Bose-Einstein condensate on an AtomChip. Radio-frequency dressing flips the transverse harmonic confinement into an IHO. Through phase-space tomography we follow the full Wigner function of the evolving quantum state, observe sub-vacuum squeezing of 10.6(1.3) dB, and test coherent reversibility by time-reversing the IHO evolution. Matter-wave interference between the two daughter clouds confirms quantum coherence over timescales far beyond the initial expansion. Our experiment establishes ultra-cold atoms as a clean, controlled, many-body platform for unstable quantum dynamics opening a route to force sensing with time-reversal-based coherence certification and to analog studies of the amplification of quantum fluctuations in inflationary field dynamics.


---


## 化学精确激发态的变分低能量子空间

**Original Title:** Variational low-energy subspaces for chemically accurate excited states

**Authors:** Clemens Giuliani, Rocco Martinazzo, Giuseppe Carleo, Riccardo Rossi

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05148v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05148v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

准确的电子激发态对于光化学、光谱学和非隔热分子动力学至关重要，但高级计算通常规模很大，并且需要对目标状态的特征或对称性的先验知识。在这里，我们表明，变分激励状态优化可以被重新表述为电子Hamilton的低能量子空间的迭代类接地状态问题。将这种变分原理应用于非垂直斯莱特决定符，从而产生EXIDOS，这是一种仅受状态数和每个状态决定符控制的激发态计算的自动方法。EXIDOS同时优化多个激发态，无需明确的垂直约束或强加的旋转和点群对称性。针对FCI和最先进的量子化学方法的基准显示，N$2和CO中的多种状态、HC1中的电荷转移状态、NH$3中的里德堡状态、C$2中的双激发和扩展的势能曲线的化学准确性，并避免了乙烯中的交叉和圆锥形交叉。这些结果确立了EXIDOS是一种低尺度、完全可变的获得化学准确激发态的途径。


### Abstract

Accurate electronic excited states are essential for photochemistry, spectroscopy and non-adiabatic molecular dynamics, but high-level calculations often scale steeply and require prior knowledge of the target state's character or symmetry. Here we show that variational excited-state optimization can be reformulated as an iterated ground-state-like problem for a low-energy subspace of the electronic Hamiltonian. Applying this variational principle to non-orthogonal Slater determinants leads to EXIDOS, an automatic method for excited state calculations controlled only by the number of states and determinants per state. EXIDOS optimizes multiple excited states simultaneously, without explicit orthogonality constraints or imposed spin and point-group symmetries. Benchmarks against FCI and state-of-the-art quantum chemistry methods show chemical accuracy for a multitude of states in N$_2$ and CO, charge-transfer states in HCl, Rydberg states in NH$_3$, double excitations and extended potential-energy curves in C$_2$, and avoided crossings and conical intersections in ethylene. These results establish EXIDOS as a low-scaling, fully variational route to chemically accurate excited states.


---


## 冷原子Dirac格点中Floquet工程宇称反常阶梯

**Original Title:** Floquet-Engineered Parity Anomaly Staircase in a Cold Atom Dirac Lattice

**Authors:** Binayyak Roy, Vito Scarola, Sumanta Tewari

**Link:** http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.05164v1

**PDF:** https://arxiv.org/pdf/2606.05164v1

**Submitted:** 2026-06-03


### 摘要

我们提出了一个Floquet工程冷原子实现的宇称异常启发反常霍尔阶梯在二维$π$-通量晶格。有效的模型主机的时间反演对称破缺Floquet质量和静态反转破缺质量偏移的联合行动产生的大量狄拉克费米子。一个附加的动量相关标量位移项使不同的狄拉克扇区向相反的能量方向移动，而不改变它们的布洛赫本征向量。因此，Berry曲率的贡献与个别大规模狄拉克部门可以选择性地占据，允许异常霍尔响应逐步演变的化学势或标量位移项的函数。评估完整的格点Berry弯曲积分，我们发现$0$、$e#2/2 h $和$e#2/h$附近存在平台状响应，分别对应于零、一和两个有效大质量狄拉克扇形贡献的激活。我们分析了相关的低能量狄拉克理论、能带布局、Berry弯曲结构和两个参数响应图，并讨论了在超冷原子光学格子中使用拉曼辅助隧道、非共振Floquet驱动和辅助AC-Stark修饰的可能实现。


### Abstract

We propose a Floquet-engineered cold atom realization of a parity anomaly inspired anomalous Hall staircase in a two dimensional $π$-flux lattice. The effective model hosts massive Dirac fermions generated by the combined action of a time reversal symmetry breaking Floquet mass and a static inversion breaking mass offset. An additional momentum dependent scalar displacement term shifts different Dirac sectors in opposite energy directions without modifying their Bloch eigenvectors. As a result, the Berry curvature contribution associated with individual massive Dirac sectors can be selectively occupied, allowing the anomalous Hall response to evolve stepwise as a function of chemical potential or scalar displacement term. Evaluating the full lattice Berry curvature integral, we find plateau-like responses near $0$, $e^2/2h$, and $e^2/h$, corresponding respectively to the activation of zero, one, and two effective massive Dirac sector contributions. We analyze the associated low energy Dirac theory, band topology, Berry curvature structure, and two parameter response maps, and discuss a possible realization using Raman-assisted tunneling, off-resonant Floquet driving, and auxiliary AC-Stark dressing in ultracold atomic optical lattices.


---
